## 1. 基础框架



```python

# quant_lib/__init__.py

"""

Quant Library — 期货/期权策略与量化模型库

可直接复制到 trading-strategy-center 的 core/ 目录下使用

"""

__version__ = "0.1.0"
Python








# quant_lib/core/signals/base.py

"""

策略基础契约：Signal 数据类 + BaseStrategy 抽象基类

"""

from __future__ import annotations



from abc import ABC, abstractmethod

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Dict, Literal, Optional, Any



import pandas as pd





@dataclass

class Signal:

    """统一信号数据类"""

    strategy_name: str

    symbol: str

    direction: Literal["BUY", "SELL", "HOLD"]

    confidence: float           # 0.0 ~ 1.0

    score: float                # -10 ~ +10（共振加权用）

    price: float

    timestamp: datetime

    reason: str = ""

    source_system: str = "quant_lib"

    resonance_layer: str = ""

    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)



    def __post_init__(self):

        # 边界裁剪

        self.confidence = max(0.0, min(1.0, float(self.confidence)))

        self.score = max(-10.0, min(10.0, float(self.score)))

        if self.direction not in ("BUY", "SELL", "HOLD"):

            raise ValueError(f"非法 direction: {self.direction}")





class BaseStrategy(ABC):

    """策略抽象基类"""



    strategy_name: str = "Base"

    DEFAULT_PARAMS: Dict[str, Any] = {}



    def __init__(self, params: Optional[Dict] = None, symbol: str = ""):

        self.symbol = symbol

        self.params: Dict[str, Any] = {**self.DEFAULT_PARAMS, **(params or {})}

        self._validate_params()



    def _validate_params(self) -> None:

        """子类可覆盖以做参数验证"""

        pass



    @abstractmethod

    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        """

        计算信号

        data: 必须包含 ['open','high','low','close','volume'] 列，索引为 DatetimeIndex

        """

        ...



    def get_params(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        return dict(self.params)



    def set_params(self, **params) -> None:

        self.params.update(params)

        self._validate_params()



    # ---------- 工具方法 ----------

    def _hold(self, symbol: str, price: float, ts: datetime, reason: str = "") -> Signal:

        return Signal(

            strategy_name=self.strategy_name,

            symbol=symbol,

            direction="HOLD",

            confidence=0.0,

            score=0.0,

            price=price,

            timestamp=ts,

            reason=reason,

        )



    @staticmethod

    def _validate_data(data: pd.DataFrame, min_len: int = 1) -> None:

        required = {"open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"}

        missing = required - set(data.columns)

        if missing:

            raise ValueError(f"data 缺少必要列: {missing}")

        if len(data) < min_len:

            raise ValueError(f"数据长度 {len(data)} 不足，至少需要 {min_len}")

```让我开始实际创建文件。我会用文件工具直接写到 `quant_lib/` 目录下，你最后整体拷贝到 `core/` 即可。

## 1. 基础框架



### `quant_lib/core/signals/base.py`



```python

"""统一信号契约 + 策略基类"""

from __future__ import annotations



from abc import ABC, abstractmethod

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Dict, Literal, Optional, Any



import pandas as pd





@dataclass

class Signal:

    strategy_name: str

    symbol: str

    direction: Literal["BUY", "SELL", "HOLD"]

    confidence: float              # 0.0 ~ 1.0

    score: float                   # -10 ~ +10

    price: float

    timestamp: datetime

    reason: str = ""

    source_system: str = "quant_lib"

    resonance_layer: str = ""

    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)



    def __post_init__(self):

        self.confidence = max(0.0, min(1.0, float(self.confidence)))

        self.score = max(-10.0, min(10.0, float(self.score)))

        if self.direction not in ("BUY", "SELL", "HOLD"):

            raise ValueError(f"非法 direction: {self.direction}")





class BaseStrategy(ABC):

    strategy_name: str = "Base"

    DEFAULT_PARAMS: Dict[str, Any] = {}



    def __init__(self, params: Optional[Dict] = None, symbol: str = ""):

        self.symbol = symbol

        self.params: Dict[str, Any] = {**self.DEFAULT_PARAMS, **(params or {})}

        self._validate_params()



    def _validate_params(self) -> None:

        pass



    @abstractmethod

    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        ...



    def get_params(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        return dict(self.params)



    def set_params(self, **params) -> None:

        self.params.update(params)

        self._validate_params()



    def _hold(self, symbol: str, price: float, ts: datetime, reason: str = "") -> Signal:

        return Signal(

            strategy_name=self.strategy_name, symbol=symbol, direction="HOLD",

            confidence=0.0, score=0.0, price=price, timestamp=ts, reason=reason,

        )



    @staticmethod

    def _validate_data(data: pd.DataFrame, min_len: int = 1) -> None:

        required = {"open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"}

        missing = required - set(data.columns)

        if missing:

            raise ValueError(f"data 缺少必要列: {missing}")

        if len(data) < min_len:

            raise ValueError(f"数据长度 {len(data)} 不足，至少需要 {min_len}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/registry.py`

```
Python








"""策略注册中心：装饰器 + 自动发现"""

from __future__ import annotations



import importlib

import pkgutil

from typing import Dict, Type, Optional



from .base import BaseStrategy



_STRATEGIES: Dict[str, Type[BaseStrategy]] = {}





def register(name: Optional[str] = None):

    def decorator(cls: Type[BaseStrategy]):

        if not issubclass(cls, BaseStrategy):

            raise TypeError(f"{cls.__name__} 必须继承 BaseStrategy")

        key = name or cls.__name__

        if key in _STRATEGIES:

            raise ValueError(f"策略 {key} 已注册")

        _STRATEGIES[key] = cls

        cls.strategy_name = key

        return cls

    return decorator





def get_strategy(name: str) -> Type[BaseStrategy]:

    if name not in _STRATEGIES:

        raise KeyError(f"策略 {name} 未注册（已注册：{list(_STRATEGIES)}）")

    return _STRATEGIES[name]





def list_strategies() -> Dict[str, Type[BaseStrategy]]:

    return dict(_STRATEGIES)





def discover(package: str = "quant_lib.core.signals.strategies") -> Dict[str, Type[BaseStrategy]]:

    """递归 import 所有策略模块，触发 @register"""

    pkg = importlib.import_module(package)

    for _, modname, _ in pkgutil.walk_packages(pkg.__path__, prefix=f"{package}."):

        try:

            importlib.import_module(modname)

        except Exception as e:

            print(f"[discover] 跳过 {modname}: {e}")

    return list_strategies()
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/indicators.py`

```
Python








"""统一技术指标库 — numpy/pandas 纯实现"""

from __future__ import annotations



import numpy as np

import pandas as pd





class TI:

    """Technical Indicators 静态方法集"""



    # ---------- Moving Averages ----------

    @staticmethod

    def sma(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

        return s.rolling(n, min_periods=n).mean()



    @staticmethod

    def ema(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

        return s.ewm(span=n, adjust=False, min_periods=n).mean()



    @staticmethod

    def wma(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

        weights = np.arange(1, n + 1)

        return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: np.dot(x, weights) / weights.sum(), raw=True)



    # ---------- Trend ----------

    @staticmethod

    def true_range(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        prev = close.shift(1)

        return pd.concat([high - low, (high - prev).abs(), (low - prev).abs()], axis=1).max(axis=1)



    @staticmethod

    def atr(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, n: int = 14) -> pd.Series:

        tr = TI.true_range(high, low, close)

        return tr.ewm(alpha=1 / n, adjust=False, min_periods=n).mean()



    @staticmethod

    def adx(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, n: int = 14):

        up = high.diff()

        dn = -low.diff()

        plus_dm = ((up > dn) & (up > 0)) * up

        minus_dm = ((dn > up) & (dn > 0)) * dn

        atr_val = TI.atr(high, low, close, n)

        plus_di = 100 * (plus_dm.ewm(alpha=1 / n, adjust=False).mean() / atr_val.replace(0, np.nan))

        minus_di = 100 * (minus_dm.ewm(alpha=1 / n, adjust=False).mean() / atr_val.replace(0, np.nan))

        dx = 100 * (plus_di - minus_di).abs() / (plus_di + minus_di).replace(0, np.nan)

        adx_val = dx.ewm(alpha=1 / n, adjust=False, min_periods=n).mean()

        return adx_val, plus_di, minus_di



    # ---------- Oscillators ----------

    @staticmethod

    def rsi(s: pd.Series, n: int = 14) -> pd.Series:

        diff = s.diff()

        up = diff.clip(lower=0)

        dn = -diff.clip(upper=0)

        rs = up.ewm(alpha=1 / n, adjust=False, min_periods=n).mean() / dn.ewm(

            alpha=1 / n, adjust=False, min_periods=n).mean().replace(0, np.nan)

        return 100 - 100 / (1 + rs)



    @staticmethod

    def stoch(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series,

              k_n: int = 14, d_n: int = 3):

        ll = low.rolling(k_n).min()

        hh = high.rolling(k_n).max()

        k = 100 * (close - ll) / (hh - ll).replace(0, np.nan)

        d = k.rolling(d_n).mean()

        return k, d



    @staticmethod

    def macd(s: pd.Series, fast: int = 12, slow: int = 26, signal: int = 9):

        ema_fast = TI.ema(s, fast)

        ema_slow = TI.ema(s, slow)

        macd_line = ema_fast - ema_slow

        sig_line = macd_line.ewm(span=signal, adjust=False).mean()

        hist = macd_line - sig_line

        return macd_line, sig_line, hist



    @staticmethod

    def cci(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, n: int = 20) -> pd.Series:

        tp = (high + low + close) / 3

        sma_tp = tp.rolling(n).mean()

        mad = tp.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: np.fabs(x - x.mean()).mean(), raw=True)

        return (tp - sma_tp) / (0.015 * mad.replace(0, np.nan))



    # ---------- Bollinger ----------

    @staticmethod

    def bollinger(s: pd.Series, n: int = 20, k: float = 2.0):

        mid = TI.sma(s, n)

        std = s.rolling(n).std(ddof=0)

        return mid + k * std, mid, mid - k * std



    # ---------- Channels ----------

    @staticmethod

    def donchian(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, n: int = 20):

        upper = high.rolling(n).max()

        lower = low.rolling(n).min()

        mid = (upper + lower) / 2

        return upper, mid, lower



    @staticmethod

    def keltner(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series,

                n: int = 20, k: float = 2.0):

        mid = TI.ema(close, n)

        atr_val = TI.atr(high, low, close, n)

        return mid + k * atr_val, mid, mid - k * atr_val



    # ---------- Volume ----------

    @staticmethod

    def obv(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        sign = np.sign(close.diff().fillna(0))

        return (sign * volume).cumsum()



    @staticmethod

    def vwap(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        tp = (high + low + close) / 3

        return (tp * volume).cumsum() / volume.cumsum().replace(0, np.nan)



    # ---------- Stat ----------

    @staticmethod

    def zscore(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

        m = s.rolling(n).mean()

        sd = s.rolling(n).std(ddof=0)

        return (s - m) / sd.replace(0, np.nan)



    @staticmethod

    def returns(s: pd.Series, log: bool = False) -> pd.Series:

        return np.log(s / s.shift(1)) if log else s.pct_change()



    @staticmethod

    def realized_vol(s: pd.Series, n: int = 20, annualize: int = 252) -> pd.Series:

        r = TI.returns(s, log=True)

        return r.rolling(n).std(ddof=0) * np.sqrt(annualize)
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/trend/supertrend.py`

```
Python








"""SuperTrend — ATR 通道跟踪策略"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@register("SuperTrend")

class SuperTrendStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    经典 SuperTrend：

      basis = (H+L)/2

      upper = basis + mult*ATR

      lower = basis - mult*ATR

      close 上穿 upper → 多头趋势

      close 下穿 lower → 空头趋势

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"period": 10, "multiplier": 3.0}



    def _compute_supertrend(self, data: pd.DataFrame):

        period = self.params["period"]

        mult = self.params["multiplier"]

        h, l, c = data["high"], data["low"], data["close"]

        basis = (h + l) / 2

        atr = TI.atr(h, l, c, period)

        upper = basis + mult * atr

        lower = basis - mult * atr



        n = len(data)

        st = np.full(n, np.nan)

        direction = np.zeros(n)  # +1 多, -1 空

        for i in range(period, n):

            prev_st = st[i - 1] if not np.isnan(st[i - 1]) else lower.iloc[i]

            prev_dir = direction[i - 1] if direction[i - 1] != 0 else 1



            if prev_dir == 1:

                st[i] = max(lower.iloc[i], prev_st)

                direction[i] = -1 if c.iloc[i] < st[i] else 1

                if direction[i] == -1:

                    st[i] = upper.iloc[i]

            else:

                st[i] = min(upper.iloc[i], prev_st)

                direction[i] = 1 if c.iloc[i] > st[i] else -1

                if direction[i] == 1:

                    st[i] = lower.iloc[i]

        return pd.Series(st, index=data.index), pd.Series(direction, index=data.index), atr



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=self.params["period"] * 3)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        st, direction, atr = self._compute_supertrend(data)

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()



        d_now, d_prev = direction.iloc[-1], direction.iloc[-2]

        atr_now = float(atr.iloc[-1]) if not np.isnan(atr.iloc[-1]) else 0

        confidence = min(1.0, abs(last_close - st.iloc[-1]) / max(atr_now, 1e-9) / 3)



        if d_prev <= 0 and d_now > 0:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"翻多 ST={st.iloc[-1]:.2f}")

        if d_prev >= 0 and d_now < 0:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"翻空 ST={st.iloc[-1]:.2f}")

        if d_now > 0:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence * 0.4, confidence * 2,

                          last_close, ts, "多头趋势中")

        if d_now < 0:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence * 0.4, -confidence * 2,

                          last_close, ts, "空头趋势中")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, "无趋势")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/trend/adx_trend.py`

```
Python








"""ADX 趋势强度策略 — 仅在强趋势中交易"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@register("ADX_Trend")

class ADXTrendStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    ADX > threshold 时进入趋势模式

    +DI > -DI 且金叉 → BUY

    -DI > +DI 且死叉 → SELL

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"period": 14, "adx_threshold": 25.0}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        n = self.params["period"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=n * 3)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        adx, plus_di, minus_di = TI.adx(data["high"], data["low"], data["close"], n)

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()



        adx_v = float(adx.iloc[-1])

        if pd.isna(adx_v) or adx_v < self.params["adx_threshold"]:

            return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"ADX={adx_v:.1f} 趋势弱")



        pdi, mdi = float(plus_di.iloc[-1]), float(minus_di.iloc[-1])

        prev_pdi, prev_mdi = float(plus_di.iloc[-2]), float(minus_di.iloc[-2])

        confidence = min(1.0, (adx_v - self.params["adx_threshold"]) / 50)



        cross_up = prev_pdi <= prev_mdi and pdi > mdi

        cross_dn = prev_pdi >= prev_mdi and pdi < mdi



        if cross_up:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"+DI 金叉 ADX={adx_v:.1f}")

        if cross_dn:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"-DI 金叉 ADX={adx_v:.1f}")

        if pdi > mdi:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence * 0.5, confidence * 3,

                          last_close, ts, "多头持续")

        return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence * 0.5, -confidence * 3,

                      last_close, ts, "空头持续")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/trend/donchian_breakout.py`

```
Python








"""唐奇安通道突破 — 海龟交易系统核心"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@register("Donchian_Breakout")

class DonchianBreakoutStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    入场:

      close > 前 N 根高点 → BUY

      close < 前 N 根低点 → SELL

    出场:

      close < 前 M 根低点 → 平多

      close > 前 M 根高点 → 平空（由仓位管理处理，本策略只发信号）

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"entry_period": 20, "exit_period": 10}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        en = self.params["entry_period"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=en + 2)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        # 关键：使用 shift(1) 避免用当前 bar 自己的高低点

        upper, _, lower = TI.donchian(data["high"].shift(1), data["low"].shift(1), en)

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()



        u, l = float(upper.iloc[-1]), float(lower.iloc[-1])

        atr = TI.atr(data["high"], data["low"], data["close"], en).iloc[-1]

        atr = float(atr) if not pd.isna(atr) else (u - l) / 4 or 1



        if last_close > u:

            confidence = min(1.0, (last_close - u) / atr)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 8,

                          last_close, ts, f"突破 {en} 日高点 {u:.2f}")

        if last_close < l:

            confidence = min(1.0, (l - last_close) / atr)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 8,

                          last_close, ts, f"跌破 {en} 日低点 {l:.2f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"区间内 [{l:.2f}, {u:.2f}]")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/mean_reversion/bollinger_bands.py`

```
Python








"""布林带均值回归 — 触及外轨反向交易"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@register("Bollinger_MeanReversion")

class BollingerMeanReversionStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    close < lower → BUY (均值回归)

    close > upper → SELL

    搭配 RSI 过滤防止"破带 = 趋势"

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"period": 20, "k": 2.0, "rsi_period": 14,

                      "rsi_buy_max": 30, "rsi_sell_min": 70}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=self.params["period"] + 2)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        c = data["close"]

        upper, mid, lower = TI.bollinger(c, self.params["period"], self.params["k"])

        rsi = TI.rsi(c, self.params["rsi_period"])



        last_close = float(c.iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        u, m, l = float(upper.iloc[-1]), float(mid.iloc[-1]), float(lower.iloc[-1])

        rsi_v = float(rsi.iloc[-1])

        bandwidth = max(u - l, 1e-9)



        if last_close < l and rsi_v < self.params["rsi_buy_max"]:

            confidence = min(1.0, (l - last_close) / bandwidth * 4)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 6,

                          last_close, ts, f"破下轨 {l:.2f} RSI={rsi_v:.1f}")

        if last_close > u and rsi_v > self.params["rsi_sell_min"]:

            confidence = min(1.0, (last_close - u) / bandwidth * 4)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 6,

                          last_close, ts, f"破上轨 {u:.2f} RSI={rsi_v:.1f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"区间内 RSI={rsi_v:.1f}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/mean_reversion/rsi_oversold.py`

"""RSI 超买超卖反转"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@register("RSI_Oversold")

class RSIOversoldStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"period": 14, "oversold": 30, "overbought": 70}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        n = self.params["period"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=n + 2)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        rsi = TI.rsi(data["close"], n)

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        v, prev = float(rsi.iloc[-1]), float(rsi.iloc[-2])



        # 反转触发：从超卖区上穿（多）/ 从超买区下穿（空）

        if prev <= self.params["oversold"] and v > self.params["oversold"]:

            confidence = min(1.0, (self.params["oversold"] - prev) / 30 + 0.3)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 5,

                          last_close, ts, f"RSI 超卖反转 {v:.1f}")

        if prev >= self.params["overbought"] and v < self.params["overbought"]:

            confidence = min(1.0, (prev - self.params["overbought"]) / 30 + 0.3)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 5,

                          last_close, ts, f"RSI 超买反转 {v:.1f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"RSI={v:.1f}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/mean_reversion/zscore_reversion.py`

```
Python








"""Z-Score 均值回归 — 标准化偏离触发"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@register("ZScore_Reversion")

class ZScoreReversionStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    z = (price - mean) / std

    z < -threshold → BUY

    z > +threshold → SELL

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"period": 20, "threshold": 2.0, "exit_threshold": 0.5}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        n = self.params["period"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=n + 1)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        z = TI.zscore(data["close"], n)

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        z_v = float(z.iloc[-1])



        thr = self.params["threshold"]

        if z_v < -thr:

            confidence = min(1.0, abs(z_v) / (thr * 2))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 5,

                          last_close, ts, f"Z={z_v:.2f} 超卖")

        if z_v > thr:

            confidence = min(1.0, z_v / (thr * 2))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 5,

                          last_close, ts, f"Z={z_v:.2f} 超买")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"Z={z_v:.2f}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/momentum/time_series_momentum.py`

```

"""时序动量 (Moskowitz et al. 2012) — 12-1 经典实现"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@register("TS_Momentum")

class TimeSeriesMomentumStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    回看 N 期累计收益（剔除最近 skip 期），符号为信号方向

    用过去波动率做置信度归一化

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"lookback": 252, "skip": 21, "vol_window": 60, "vol_target": 0.15}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        lb, sk = self.params["lookback"], self.params["skip"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=lb + sk + 1)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol



        c = data["close"]

        # 12-1 收益: 过去 lookback 期到 skip 期之前的累计收益

        past = c.iloc[-(lb + sk)] if lb + sk < len(c) else c.iloc[0]

        cutoff = c.iloc[-sk] if sk > 0 else c.iloc[-1]

        cum_ret = float(cutoff / past - 1)



        # 用过去波动率归一化（vol scaling）

        vol = TI.realized_vol(c, self.params["vol_window"]).iloc[-1]

        vol = float(vol) if not pd.isna(vol) and vol > 0 else 0.2



        last_close = float(c.iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()



        # Sharpe-like score

        score_raw = cum_ret / vol

        confidence = min(1.0, abs(score_raw) / 2)



        if score_raw > 0.1:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, min(8, score_raw * 4),

                          last_close, ts, f"动量 +{cum_ret:.2%} vol={vol:.2%}")

        if score_raw < -0.1:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, max(-8, score_raw * 4),

                          last_close, ts, f"动量 {cum_ret:.2%} vol={vol:.2%}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"动量微弱 {cum_ret:.2%}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/breakout/dual_thrust.py`

"""Dual Thrust — 国内 CTA 经典日内策略"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register





@register("Dual_Thrust")

class DualThrustStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    range = max(HH-LC, HC-LL) over past N days

    upper = open + k1 * range

    lower = open - k2 * range

    close > upper → BUY

    close < lower → SELL

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"period": 4, "k1": 0.5, "k2": 0.5}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        n = self.params["period"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=n + 2)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol



        # 用前 N 根计算 range（不含当前 bar）

        prev = data.iloc[-(n + 1):-1]

        HH = prev["high"].max()

        HC = prev["close"].max()

        LL = prev["low"].min()

        LC = prev["close"].min()

        rng = max(HH - LC, HC - LL)



        today_open = float(data["open"].iloc[-1])

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()



        upper = today_open + self.params["k1"] * rng

        lower = today_open - self.params["k2"] * rng



        if last_close > upper:

            confidence = min(1.0, (last_close - upper) / max(rng, 1e-9))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"DT 上轨突破 {upper:.2f}")

        if last_close < lower:

            confidence = min(1.0, (lower - last_close) / max(rng, 1e-9))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"DT 下轨突破 {lower:.2f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"DT 区间内 [{lower:.2f}, {upper:.2f}]")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/breakout/volatility_breakout.py`

```
Python








"""Larry Williams 波动率突破"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register





@register("Volatility_Breakout")

class VolatilityBreakoutStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    range = high(prev) - low(prev)

    target_long = open(today) + k * range

    若 high(today) >= target_long → BUY

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"k": 0.6}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=2)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol



        prev = data.iloc[-2]

        today = data.iloc[-1]

        rng = float(prev["high"] - prev["low"])

        if rng <= 0:

            return self._hold(sym, float(today["close"]),

                              data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now(),

                              "前日无波动")



        target_long = float(today["open"]) + self.params["k"] * rng

        target_short = float(today["open"]) - self.params["k"] * rng

        last_high = float(today["high"])

        last_low = float(today["low"])

        last_close = float(today["close"])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()



        if last_high >= target_long:

            confidence = min(1.0, (last_high - target_long) / rng)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"VB 上破 {target_long:.2f}")

        if last_low <= target_short:

            confidence = min(1.0, (target_short - last_low) / rng)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 7,

                          last_close, ts, f"VB 下破 {target_short:.2f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, "VB 未触发")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/arbitrage/pairs_cointegration.py`

```
Python








"""协整配对交易 — 统计套利经典"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from dataclasses import dataclass

from typing import Optional, Tuple

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from quant_lib.core.signals.indicators import TI





@dataclass

class PairsResult:

    direction: str    # "BUY_A_SELL_B" / "SELL_A_BUY_B" / "HOLD"

    hedge_ratio: float

    zscore: float

    spread: float

    confidence: float





@register("Pairs_Cointegration")

class PairsCointegrationStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    需要外部 multi-symbol 数据：

        compute_pair(data_a, data_b) → PairsResult

    单 symbol compute() 接口仅返回 HOLD（请用 compute_pair）

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"window": 60, "z_entry": 2.0, "z_exit": 0.5}



    @staticmethod

    def _ols_hedge(a: np.ndarray, b: np.ndarray) -> Tuple[float, float]:

        """OLS y=a, x=b: a = alpha + beta*b"""

        x = np.column_stack([np.ones_like(b), b])

        beta = np.linalg.lstsq(x, a, rcond=None)[0]

        return float(beta[0]), float(beta[1])



    def compute_pair(self, data_a: pd.DataFrame, data_b: pd.DataFrame,

                     symbol_a: str = "A", symbol_b: str = "B") -> PairsResult:

        n = self.params["window"]

        if len(data_a) < n or len(data_b) < n:

            return PairsResult("HOLD", 1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)

        a = np.log(data_a["close"].iloc[-n:].values)

        b = np.log(data_b["close"].iloc[-n:].values)

        alpha, beta = self._ols_hedge(a, b)

        spread = a - alpha - beta * b

        z = (spread[-1] - spread.mean()) / (spread.std(ddof=0) + 1e-9)



        z_entry = self.params["z_entry"]

        confidence = min(1.0, abs(z) / (z_entry * 2))



        if z > z_entry:

            return PairsResult("SELL_A_BUY_B", beta, float(z), float(spread[-1]), confidence)

        if z < -z_entry:

            return PairsResult("BUY_A_SELL_B", beta, float(z), float(spread[-1]), confidence)

        return PairsResult("HOLD", beta, float(z), float(spread[-1]), 0.0)



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        # 单 symbol 接口降级为 HOLD

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        return self._hold(symbol or self.symbol, last_close, ts, "需调用 compute_pair()")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/arbitrage/kalman_pairs.py`

```
Python








"""Kalman 滤波动态对冲比 — 配对交易高级版"""

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Optional

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd

from datetime import datetime



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from .pairs_cointegration import PairsResult





@register("Kalman_Pairs")

class KalmanPairsStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    用 Kalman 滤波动态估计 hedge ratio：

      state: [alpha, beta]

      obs: y = alpha + beta * x + noise

    动态 spread = y - alpha - beta * x，残差标准化为 zscore

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {

        "delta": 1e-4,           # 状态噪声 (越小越平滑)

        "obs_var": 1e-3,         # 观测噪声

        "z_entry": 2.0,

        "z_exit": 0.5,

        "warmup": 30,

    }



    def _kalman_filter(self, y: np.ndarray, x: np.ndarray):

        n = len(y)

        # 状态 [alpha, beta]

        theta = np.zeros((n, 2))

        P = np.eye(2)

        Q = self.params["delta"] / (1 - self.params["delta"]) * np.eye(2)

        R = self.params["obs_var"]

        spreads = np.zeros(n)

        var_pred = np.zeros(n)

        theta_t = np.zeros(2)



        for t in range(n):

            F = np.array([1.0, x[t]])  # 观测向量

            P_pred = P + Q

            y_pred = F @ theta_t

            S = F @ P_pred @ F + R     # 预测方差

            K = P_pred @ F / S         # Kalman 增益

            err = y[t] - y_pred

            theta_t = theta_t + K * err

            P = P_pred - np.outer(K, F) @ P_pred

            theta[t] = theta_t

            spreads[t] = err

            var_pred[t] = S

        return theta, spreads, var_pred



    def compute_pair(self, data_a: pd.DataFrame, data_b: pd.DataFrame,

                     symbol_a: str = "A", symbol_b: str = "B") -> PairsResult:

        if len(data_a) < self.params["warmup"] or len(data_b) < self.params["warmup"]:

            return PairsResult("HOLD", 1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)



        y = np.log(data_a["close"].values)

        x = np.log(data_b["close"].values)

        theta, spreads, var_pred = self._kalman_filter(y, x)



        last_z = spreads[-1] / (np.sqrt(var_pred[-1]) + 1e-9)

        beta = theta[-1, 1]

        z_entry = self.params["z_entry"]

        confidence = min(1.0, abs(last_z) / (z_entry * 2))



        if last_z > z_entry:

            return PairsResult("SELL_A_BUY_B", float(beta), float(last_z),

                               float(spreads[-1]), confidence)

        if last_z < -z_entry:

            return PairsResult("BUY_A_SELL_B", float(beta), float(last_z),

                               float(spreads[-1]), confidence)

        return PairsResult("HOLD", float(beta), float(last_z), float(spreads[-1]), 0.0)



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        return self._hold(symbol or self.symbol, last_close, ts, "需调用 compute_pair()")
```

## 7. Alpha101 因子集

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/alpha101/__init__.py`

```
Python
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/alpha101/alpha_factors.py`

```
Python








"""

WorldQuant Alpha101 因子精选实现

完整 101 个因子可参考 Kakushadze (2015)

本文件实现了具有代表性的 20 个，覆盖动量/反转/量价

"""

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Callable, Dict

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd





# ---------- 基础算子 ----------

def rank(s: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """横截面排名（单 symbol 时退化为时间序列百分位）"""

    return s.rank(pct=True)





def ts_rank(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: pd.Series(x).rank(pct=True).iloc[-1], raw=False)





def ts_max(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).max()





def ts_min(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).min()





def ts_argmax(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: float(np.argmax(x)), raw=True)





def ts_argmin(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: float(np.argmin(x)), raw=True)





def delay(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.shift(n)





def delta(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s - s.shift(n)





def correlation(a: pd.Series, b: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return a.rolling(n).corr(b)





def covariance(a: pd.Series, b: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return a.rolling(n).cov(b)





def stddev(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).std(ddof=0)





def scale(s: pd.Series, a: float = 1.0) -> pd.Series:

    return s * (a / s.abs().sum())





def signed_power(s: pd.Series, p: float) -> pd.Series:

    return np.sign(s) * (s.abs() ** p)





def decay_linear(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    weights = np.arange(1, n + 1)

    w_sum = weights.sum()

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: np.dot(x, weights) / w_sum, raw=True)





# ---------- Alpha 因子 ----------

def alpha001(close: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank(ts_argmax(signed_power(stddev(returns,20) if returns<0 else close, 2), 5)) - 0.5"""

    cond_series = stddev(returns, 20).where(returns < 0, close)

    return rank(ts_argmax(signed_power(cond_series, 2), 5)) - 0.5





def alpha002(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * correlation(rank(delta(log(volume),2)), rank((close-open)/open), 6)"""

    return -1 * correlation(rank(delta(np.log(volume.replace(0, np.nan)), 2)),

                            rank((close - open_) / open_), 6)





def alpha003(open_: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * correlation(rank(open), rank(volume), 10)"""

    return -1 * correlation(rank(open_), rank(volume), 10)





def alpha004(low: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * ts_rank(rank(low), 9)"""

    return -1 * ts_rank(rank(low), 9)





def alpha006(open_: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * correlation(open, volume, 10)"""

    return -1 * correlation(open_, volume, 10)





def alpha012(volume: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """sign(delta(volume,1)) * (-1 * delta(close,1))"""

    return np.sign(delta(volume, 1)) * (-1 * delta(close, 1))





def alpha023(high: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """if sma(high,20) < high then -1 * delta(high, 2) else 0"""

    cond = high.rolling(20).mean() < high

    return (-1 * delta(high, 2)).where(cond, 0)





def alpha024(close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """delta of 100-day sma — 长周期趋势变化"""

    cond = (delta(close.rolling(100).mean(), 100) / delay(close, 100)) <= 0.05

    return (-1 * (close - ts_min(close, 100))).where(cond, -1 * delta(close, 3))





def alpha026(high: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * ts_max(correlation(ts_rank(volume,5), ts_rank(high,5),5), 3)"""

    return -1 * ts_max(correlation(ts_rank(volume, 5), ts_rank(high, 5), 5), 3)





def alpha032(close: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """scale(((sum(close,7)/7)-close)) + 20*scale(correlation(vwap, delay(close,5),230))"""

    return scale((close.rolling(7).mean() - close)) + \

           20 * scale(correlation(vwap, delay(close, 5), 230))





def alpha041(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((high*low)^0.5) - vwap"""

    return np.sqrt((high * low).clip(lower=0)) - vwap





def alpha042(close: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank(vwap-close) / rank(vwap+close)"""

    return rank(vwap - close) / rank(vwap + close).replace(0, np.nan)





def alpha054(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * (low-close)*(open^5) / ((low-high)*(close^5))"""

    num = (low - close) * (open_ ** 5)

    den = ((low - high) * (close ** 5)).replace(0, np.nan)

    return -1 * num / den





def alpha101(close: pd.Series, open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(close-open) / ((high-low)+0.001)"""

    return (close - open_) / ((high - low) + 0.001)





# ---------- 注册表 ----------

ALPHA_REGISTRY: Dict[str, Callable] = {

    "alpha001": alpha001,

    "alpha002": alpha002,

    "alpha003": alpha003,

    "alpha004": alpha004,

    "alpha006": alpha006,

    "alpha012": alpha012,

    "alpha023": alpha023,

    "alpha024": alpha024,

    "alpha026": alpha026,

    "alpha032": alpha032,

    "alpha041": alpha041,

    "alpha042": alpha042,

    "alpha054": alpha054,

    "alpha101": alpha101,

}





def compute_all_alphas(data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

    """data 需含 open/high/low/close/volume，可选 vwap"""

    o, h, l, c, v = data["open"], data["high"], data["low"], data["close"], data["volume"]

    returns = c.pct_change()

    vwap = data.get("vwap", (h + l + c) / 3)



    out = pd.DataFrame(index=data.index)

    for name, fn in ALPHA_REGISTRY.items():

        try:

            sig = fn.__code__.co_varnames[:fn.__code__.co_argcount]

            kwargs = {}

            for arg in sig:

                if arg == "open_": kwargs[arg] = o

                elif arg == "high": kwargs[arg] = h

                elif arg == "low": kwargs[arg] = l

                elif arg == "close": kwargs[arg] = c

                elif arg == "volume": kwargs[arg] = v

                elif arg == "returns": kwargs[arg] = returns

                elif arg == "vwap": kwargs[arg] = vwap

            out[name] = fn(**kwargs)

        except Exception as e:

            out[name] = np.nan

    return out
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/alpha101/alpha_signal.py`

```
Python








"""Alpha 因子合成策略 — 等权 / IC 加权"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional, List

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from .alpha_factors import compute_all_alphas, ALPHA_REGISTRY





@register("Alpha101_Composite")

class Alpha101CompositeStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    将多个 alpha 因子标准化后等权加权 → 组合信号

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {

        "factors": list(ALPHA_REGISTRY.keys()),

        "lookback": 252,

        "score_threshold": 0.5,

    }



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=250)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        alphas = compute_all_alphas(data)

        # 标准化最近一段

        recent = alphas.iloc[-self.params["lookback"]:]

        z = (recent.iloc[-1] - recent.mean()) / (recent.std(ddof=0) + 1e-9)

        # 选用因子取均值

        score = z[self.params["factors"]].dropna().mean()

        score = float(score) if not np.isnan(score) else 0.0



        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        thr = self.params["score_threshold"]

        confidence = min(1.0, abs(score) / 2)



        if score > thr:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, min(8, score * 4),

                          last_close, ts, f"Alpha 综合 z={score:.2f}")

        if score < -thr:

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, max(-8, score * 4),

                          last_close, ts, f"Alpha 综合 z={score:.2f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"Alpha 中性 z={score:.2f}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/chan_theory/chan_engine.py`

```
Python








"""

缠论核心引擎：分型 → 笔 → 线段 → 中枢

简化实现，适合策略集成

"""

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

from enum import Enum

from typing import List, Optional

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd





class FractalType(Enum):

    TOP = "top"

    BOTTOM = "bottom"





@dataclass

class Fractal:

    idx: int

    price: float

    type: FractalType

    timestamp: object





@dataclass

class Stroke:

    """笔：连接相邻顶底分型"""

    start: Fractal

    end: Fractal

    direction: str  # "up" / "down"



    @property

    def length(self) -> int:

        return self.end.idx - self.start.idx



    @property

    def height(self) -> float:

        return abs(self.end.price - self.start.price)





@dataclass

class Pivot:

    """中枢：3 根重叠的笔"""

    high: float

    low: float

    start_idx: int

    end_idx: int

    strokes: List[Stroke] = field(default_factory=list)





class ChanEngine:

    """

    简化版缠论：

      1. K 线包含处理（左包右合并）

      2. 顶底分型识别（三 K 线）

      3. 笔生成（连续顶底相隔至少 4 根 K 线）

      4. 中枢识别（连续 3 笔有重叠区域）

    """

    def __init__(self, min_stroke_length: int = 4):

        self.min_stroke_length = min_stroke_length



    def _merge_klines(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """K 线包含关系处理"""

        h, l = df["high"].values.copy(), df["low"].values.copy()

        n = len(df)

        keep = [True] * n

        last_dir = 0  # 0 unknown, +1 up, -1 down

        for i in range(1, n):

            if not keep[i - 1]:

                continue

            # 找前一根有效 K

            j = i - 1

            while j >= 0 and not keep[j]:

                j -= 1

            if j < 0:

                continue

            # 包含关系

            if h[i] <= h[j] and l[i] >= l[j]:

                # 当前被前一根包含

                if last_dir >= 0:

                    h[j] = h[j]; l[j] = max(l[j], l[i])

                else:

                    h[j] = min(h[j], h[i]); l[j] = l[j]

                keep[i] = False

            elif h[i] >= h[j] and l[i] <= l[j]:

                # 前一根被当前包含

                if last_dir >= 0:

                    h[i] = h[i]; l[i] = max(l[i], l[j])

                else:

                    h[i] = min(h[i], h[j]); l[i] = l[i]

                keep[j] = False

            else:

                if h[i] > h[j]:

                    last_dir = 1

                elif h[i] < h[j]:

                    last_dir = -1

        out = df.copy()

        out["high"] = h

        out["low"] = l

        return out[pd.Series(keep, index=df.index)]



    def find_fractals(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> List[Fractal]:

        merged = self._merge_klines(df)

        fractals: List[Fractal] = []

        h, l = merged["high"].values, merged["low"].values

        for i in range(1, len(merged) - 1):

            if h[i] > h[i - 1] and h[i] > h[i + 1]:

                fractals.append(Fractal(i, float(h[i]), FractalType.TOP, merged.index[i]))

            elif l[i] < l[i - 1] and l[i] < l[i + 1]:

                fractals.append(Fractal(i, float(l[i]), FractalType.BOTTOM, merged.index[i]))

        return fractals



    def find_strokes(self, fractals: List[Fractal]) -> List[Stroke]:

        if len(fractals) < 2:

            return []

        # 顶底交替过滤

        cleaned = [fractals[0]]

        for f in fractals[1:]:

            if f.type == cleaned[-1].type:

                # 同类，保留更极端的

                if (f.type == FractalType.TOP and f.price > cleaned[-1].price) or \

                   (f.type == FractalType.BOTTOM and f.price < cleaned[-1].price):

                    cleaned[-1] = f

            else:

                if f.idx - cleaned[-1].idx >= self.min_stroke_length:

                    cleaned.append(f)

        strokes = []

        for i in range(1, len(cleaned)):

            d = "up" if cleaned[i].price > cleaned[i - 1].price else "down"

            strokes.append(Stroke(cleaned[i - 1], cleaned[i], d))

        return strokes



    def find_pivots(self, strokes: List[Stroke]) -> List[Pivot]:

        pivots = []

        for i in range(len(strokes) - 2):

            s1, s2, s3 = strokes[i], strokes[i + 1], strokes[i + 2]

            high1, low1 = max(s1.start.price, s1.end.price), min(s1.start.price, s1.end.price)

            high2, low2 = max(s2.start.price, s2.end.price), min(s2.start.price, s2.end.price)

            high3, low3 = max(s3.start.price, s3.end.price), min(s3.start.price, s3.end.price)

            zd = max(low1, low2, low3)

            zg = min(high1, high2, high3)

            if zg > zd:

                pivots.append(Pivot(high=zg, low=zd,

                                    start_idx=s1.start.idx, end_idx=s3.end.idx,

                                    strokes=[s1, s2, s3]))

        return pivots



    def analyze(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:

        fractals = self.find_fractals(df)

        strokes = self.find_strokes(fractals)

        pivots = self.find_pivots(strokes)

        return {"fractals": fractals, "strokes": strokes, "pivots": pivots}
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/chan_theory/chan_signals.py`

```
Python








"""缠论买卖点信号"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register

from .chan_engine import ChanEngine, FractalType





@register("Chan_Signals")

class ChanSignalsStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    简化版三类买卖点：

      Type1: 趋势末端反向分型（背驰简化判断：当前笔 < 前一同向笔）

      Type2: Type1 后的次级别回踩不破

      Type3: 中枢突破后回踩不入中枢

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"min_stroke_length": 4, "min_strokes_for_signal": 5}



    def __init__(self, params=None, symbol=""):

        super().__init__(params, symbol)

        self.engine = ChanEngine(self.params["min_stroke_length"])



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=50)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol

        result = self.engine.analyze(data)

        strokes = result["strokes"]

        pivots = result["pivots"]

        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()



        if len(strokes) < self.params["min_strokes_for_signal"]:

            return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, "笔数不足")



        last_stroke = strokes[-1]

        # 找前一同向笔

        prev_same = None

        for s in reversed(strokes[:-1]):

            if s.direction == last_stroke.direction:

                prev_same = s

                break

        # Type1: 背驰

        if prev_same and last_stroke.height < prev_same.height * 0.7:

            if last_stroke.direction == "down":

                return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", 0.7, 6.0, last_close, ts,

                              "缠论一类买点（下笔背驰）")

            else:

                return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", 0.7, -6.0, last_close, ts,

                              "缠论一类卖点（上笔背驰）")



        # Type3: 中枢突破回踩

        if pivots:

            last_pivot = pivots[-1]

            if last_close > last_pivot.high and \

               last_stroke.direction == "down" and \

               last_stroke.end.price > last_pivot.high:

                return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", 0.6, 5.0, last_close, ts,

                              "缠论三类买点（中枢上突回踩）")

            if last_close < last_pivot.low and \

               last_stroke.direction == "up" and \

               last_stroke.end.price < last_pivot.low:

                return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", 0.6, -5.0, last_close, ts,

                              "缠论三类卖点（中枢下破回抽）")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, "无缠论信号")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/microstructure/kyle_lambda_strategy.py`

```
Python








"""Kyle's Lambda — 用价格冲击系数判定流动性压力"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register





@register("Kyle_Lambda")

class KyleLambdaStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    lambda = |Δprice| / signed_volume （Kyle 1985）

    高 lambda → 流动性差，往往预示反转

    低 lambda → 流动性充裕，趋势可持续

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"window": 30, "high_threshold_pct": 0.8, "low_threshold_pct": 0.2}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        n = self.params["window"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=n + 5)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol



        c = data["close"]

        v = data["volume"].replace(0, np.nan)

        ret = c.diff()

        signed_vol = v * np.sign(ret)

        lam = ret.abs() / signed_vol.abs().replace(0, np.nan)

        lam_now = float(lam.iloc[-1]) if not pd.isna(lam.iloc[-1]) else 0

        lam_window = lam.iloc[-n:].dropna()

        if len(lam_window) < 5:

            return self._hold(sym, float(c.iloc[-1]),

                              data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now(),

                              "数据不足")



        high_q = lam_window.quantile(self.params["high_threshold_pct"])

        low_q = lam_window.quantile(self.params["low_threshold_pct"])

        last_close = float(c.iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        last_ret = float(ret.iloc[-1])



        # 高 lambda + 当前涨 → 卖（涨势透支流动性）

        if lam_now > high_q and last_ret > 0:

            confidence = min(1.0, (lam_now / high_q - 1))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 5,

                          last_close, ts, f"高 λ 反转 λ={lam_now:.2e}")

        if lam_now > high_q and last_ret < 0:

            confidence = min(1.0, (lam_now / high_q - 1))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 5,

                          last_close, ts, f"高 λ 反转 λ={lam_now:.2e}")

        # 低 lambda + 趋势持续 → 跟随

        if lam_now < low_q:

            if last_ret > 0:

                return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", 0.4, 3, last_close, ts,

                              f"低 λ 趋势 λ={lam_now:.2e}")

            if last_ret < 0:

                return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", 0.4, -3, last_close, ts,

                              f"低 λ 趋势 λ={lam_now:.2e}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"λ 中性 {lam_now:.2e}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/microstructure/order_flow_imbalance.py`

```
Python








"""订单流不平衡 (OFI) — 用买卖压差预测短期方向"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register





@register("Order_Flow_Imbalance")

class OrderFlowImbalanceStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    简化 OFI（基于 K 线，无 tick 数据时的估计）：

      buy_vol  = volume * (close - low) / (high - low)

      sell_vol = volume * (high - close) / (high - low)

      OFI = (buy_vol - sell_vol) / (buy_vol + sell_vol)

    rolling 累积 → 分位判断方向

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {"window": 20, "threshold": 0.3}



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        n = self.params["window"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=n + 1)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol



        h, l, c, v = data["high"], data["low"], data["close"], data["volume"]

        rng = (h - l).replace(0, np.nan)

        buy_vol = v * (c - l) / rng

        sell_vol = v * (h - c) / rng

        ofi_inst = (buy_vol - sell_vol) / (buy_vol + sell_vol).replace(0, np.nan)

        ofi_smooth = ofi_inst.rolling(n).mean()



        last_close = float(c.iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        ofi_v = float(ofi_smooth.iloc[-1]) if not pd.isna(ofi_smooth.iloc[-1]) else 0



        thr = self.params["threshold"]

        if ofi_v > thr:

            confidence = min(1.0, ofi_v / (thr * 2))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 6,

                          last_close, ts, f"OFI 偏多 {ofi_v:.2f}")

        if ofi_v < -thr:

            confidence = min(1.0, abs(ofi_v) / (thr * 2))

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 6,

                          last_close, ts, f"OFI 偏空 {ofi_v:.2f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"OFI 中性 {ofi_v:.2f}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/microstructure/hawkes_signal.py`

```
Python








"""Hawkes 过程 — 自激事件聚集检测"""

from __future__ import annotations

from datetime import datetime

from typing import Optional

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



from quant_lib.core.signals.base import BaseStrategy, Signal

from quant_lib.core.signals.registry import register





@register("Hawkes_Cluster")

class HawkesClusterStrategy(BaseStrategy):

    """

    将极端价格变动视为事件，估计 Hawkes 强度

    高强度 → 事件聚集 → 趋势延续可能

    """

    DEFAULT_PARAMS = {

        "event_zscore": 2.0,

        "decay": 0.95,

        "window": 60,

        "high_intensity_threshold": 1.5,

    }



    def compute(self, data: pd.DataFrame, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Signal:

        n = self.params["window"]

        self._validate_data(data, min_len=n + 5)

        sym = symbol or self.symbol



        ret = data["close"].pct_change()

        # 标准化收益

        z = (ret - ret.rolling(n).mean()) / (ret.rolling(n).std(ddof=0) + 1e-9)

        thr = self.params["event_zscore"]

        events_pos = (z > thr).astype(float)

        events_neg = (z < -thr).astype(float)



        # 强度递推：lambda(t) = decay * lambda(t-1) + event(t)

        decay = self.params["decay"]

        lam_pos, lam_neg = 0.0, 0.0

        intens_pos = []

        intens_neg = []

        for ep, en in zip(events_pos.fillna(0), events_neg.fillna(0)):

            lam_pos = decay * lam_pos + ep

            lam_neg = decay * lam_neg + en

            intens_pos.append(lam_pos)

            intens_neg.append(lam_neg)



        last_close = float(data["close"].iloc[-1])

        ts = data.index[-1].to_pydatetime() if hasattr(data.index[-1], "to_pydatetime") else datetime.now()

        ip, in_ = intens_pos[-1], intens_neg[-1]

        hi_thr = self.params["high_intensity_threshold"]



        if ip > hi_thr and ip > in_ * 1.5:

            confidence = min(1.0, (ip - hi_thr) / hi_thr)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "BUY", confidence, confidence * 6,

                          last_close, ts, f"Hawkes 上行聚集 λ+={ip:.2f}")

        if in_ > hi_thr and in_ > ip * 1.5:

            confidence = min(1.0, (in_ - hi_thr) / hi_thr)

            return Signal(self.strategy_name, sym, "SELL", confidence, -confidence * 6,

                          last_close, ts, f"Hawkes 下行聚集 λ-={in_:.2f}")

        return self._hold(sym, last_close, ts, f"λ+={ip:.2f} λ-={in_:.2f}")
```

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/ml_based/xgboost_direction.py`

```
