│   │   │   ├── patchtst.py                        # PatchTST

│   │   │   ├── informer.py                        # Informer

│   │   │   └── conformal.py                       # Conformal Prediction

│   │   └── futures_analytics/

│   │       ├── continuous_contract.py             # 连续合约

│   │       ├── term_structure.py                  # 期限结构

│   │       └── basis_analysis.py                  # 基差分析

│   └── backtest/

│       ├── event_engine.py                        # 事件驱动引擎

│       ├── option_backtester.py                   # 期权回测

│       ├── portfolio.py                           # 组合管理

│       └── metrics.py                             # 绩效指标

└── tests/

    ├── test_alpha101_full.py

    ├── test_advanced_pricing.py

    ├── test_option_strategies.py

    ├── test_ml_forecasters.py

    ├── test_futures_analytics.py

    └── test_backtest.py
```

------

## 1. 完整 Alpha101 因子库

### `quant_lib/core/signals/strategies/alpha101/alpha_factors_full.py`

```
Python








"""

WorldQuant Alpha101 完整实现

基于 Kakushadze (2015) "101 Formulaic Alphas"

https://arxiv.org/abs/1601.00991



注意：

- 部分因子需要横截面排序（多品种），单品种时退化为时间序列排名

- vwap 缺失时用 (H+L+C)/3 估计

- adv{N} = N 日平均成交量

"""

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Callable, Dict

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd



# ---------- 基础算子（继承上一轮） ----------

def rank(s: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rank(pct=True)



def ts_rank(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: pd.Series(x).rank(pct=True).iloc[-1], raw=False)



def ts_max(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).max()



def ts_min(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).min()



def ts_argmax(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: float(np.argmax(x)), raw=True)



def ts_argmin(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: float(np.argmin(x)), raw=True)



def delay(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.shift(n)



def delta(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s - s.shift(n)



def correlation(a: pd.Series, b: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return a.rolling(n).corr(b)



def covariance(a: pd.Series, b: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return a.rolling(n).cov(b)



def stddev(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).std(ddof=0)



def scale(s: pd.Series, a: float = 1.0) -> pd.Series:

    abs_sum = s.abs().sum()

    return s * (a / abs_sum) if abs_sum != 0 else s



def signed_power(s: pd.Series, p: float) -> pd.Series:

    return np.sign(s) * (s.abs() ** p)



def decay_linear(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    weights = np.arange(1, n + 1)

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: np.dot(x, weights) / weights.sum(), raw=True)



def ts_sum(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).sum()



def sma(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).mean()



def product(s: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    return s.rolling(n).apply(lambda x: np.prod(x), raw=True)



def count_cond(cond: pd.Series, n: int) -> pd.Series:

    """窗口内条件为真的次数"""

    return cond.astype(float).rolling(n).sum()



# ---------- 完整 101 个因子 ----------



def alpha001(close: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank(ts_argmax(signed_power((returns<0 ? stddev(returns,20) : close), 2), 5)) - 0.5"""

    cond = stddev(returns, 20).where(returns < 0, close)

    return rank(ts_argmax(signed_power(cond, 2), 5)) - 0.5



def alpha002(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * correlation(rank(delta(log(volume),2)), rank((close-open)/open), 6)"""

    return -1 * correlation(rank(delta(np.log(volume.replace(0, np.nan)), 2)),

                            rank((close - open_) / open_), 6)



def alpha003(open_: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * correlation(rank(open), rank(volume), 10)"""

    return -1 * correlation(rank(open_), rank(volume), 10)



def alpha004(low: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * ts_rank(rank(low), 9)"""

    return -1 * ts_rank(rank(low), 9)



def alpha005(open_: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank((open - (sum(vwap, 10) / 10))) * (-1 * abs(rank((close - vwap))))"""

    return rank(open_ - vwap.rolling(10).mean()) * (-1 * rank((close - vwap)).abs())



def alpha006(open_: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * correlation(open, volume, 10)"""

    return -1 * correlation(open_, volume, 10)



def alpha007(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((adv20 < volume) ? ((-1 * ts_rank(abs(delta(close, 7)), 60)) * sign(delta(close, 7))) : -1)"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    cond = adv20 < volume

    inner = -1 * ts_rank(delta(close, 7).abs(), 60) * np.sign(delta(close, 7))

    return inner.where(cond, -1)



def alpha008(open_: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * rank(((sum(open, 5) * sum(returns, 5)) - delay((sum(open, 5) * sum(returns, 5)), 10)))"""

    so = open_.rolling(5).sum()

    sr = returns.rolling(5).sum()

    prod = so * sr

    return -1 * rank(prod - delay(prod, 10))



def alpha009(close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((0 < ts_min(delta(close, 1), 5)) ? delta(close, 1) : ((ts_max(delta(close, 1), 5) < 0) ? delta(close, 1) : (-1 * delta(close, 1))))"""

    dc = delta(close, 1)

    c1 = ts_min(dc, 5) > 0

    c2 = ts_max(dc, 5) < 0

    return dc.where(c1, dc.where(c2, -dc))



def alpha010(close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank(((0 < ts_min(delta(close, 1), 4)) ? delta(close, 1) : ...))"""

    dc = delta(close, 1)

    c1 = ts_min(dc, 4) > 0

    c2 = ts_max(dc, 4) < 0

    return rank(dc.where(c1, dc.where(c2, -dc)))



def alpha011(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((rank(ts_max((vwap - close), 3)) + rank(ts_min((vwap - close), 3))) * rank(delta(volume, 3)))"""

    diff = vwap - close

    return (rank(ts_max(diff, 3)) + rank(ts_min(diff, 3))) * rank(delta(volume, 3))



def alpha012(volume: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """sign(delta(volume, 1)) * (-1 * delta(close, 1))"""

    return np.sign(delta(volume, 1)) * (-1 * delta(close, 1))



def alpha013(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * rank(covariance(rank(close), rank(volume), 5))"""

    return -1 * rank(covariance(rank(close), rank(volume), 5))



def alpha014(open_: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((-1 * rank(delta(returns, 3))) * correlation(open, volume, 10))"""

    return -1 * rank(delta(returns, 3)) * correlation(open_, volume, 10)



def alpha015(high: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * sum(rank(correlation(rank(high), rank(volume), 3)), 3)"""

    return -1 * rank(correlation(rank(high), rank(volume), 3)).rolling(3).sum()



def alpha016(high: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * rank(covariance(rank(high), rank(volume), 5))"""

    return -1 * rank(covariance(rank(high), rank(volume), 5))



def alpha017(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((-1 * rank(ts_rank(close, 10))) * rank(delta(delta(close, 1), 1))) * rank(ts_rank((volume / adv20), 5)))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return ((-1 * rank(ts_rank(close, 10))) * 

            rank(delta(delta(close, 1), 1)) * 

            rank(ts_rank(volume / adv20, 5)))



def alpha018(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * rank(((stddev(abs((close - open)), 5) + (close - open)) + correlation(close, open, 10)))"""

    return -1 * rank(stddev((close - open_).abs(), 5) + (close - open_) + 

                     correlation(close, open_, 10))



def alpha019(close: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((-1 * sign(((close - delay(close, 7)) + delta(close, 7)))) * (1 + rank((1 + sum(returns, 250)))))"""

    return (-1 * np.sign((close - delay(close, 7)) + delta(close, 7))) * \

           (1 + rank(1 + returns.rolling(250).sum()))



def alpha020(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((-1 * rank((open - delay(high, 1)))) * rank((open - delay(close, 1)))) * rank((open - delay(low, 1))))"""

    return ((-1 * rank(open_ - delay(high, 1))) * 

            rank(open_ - delay(close, 1)) * 

            rank(open_ - delay(low, 1)))



def alpha021(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((((sum(close, 8) / 8) + stddev(close, 8)) < (sum(close, 2) / 2)) ? (-1 * 1) : (((sum(close, 2) / 2) < ((sum(close, 8) / 8) - stddev(close, 8))) ? 1 : (((1 < (volume / adv20)) || ((volume / adv20) == 1)) ? 1 : (-1 * 1))))"""

    ma8 = close.rolling(8).mean()

    std8 = stddev(close, 8)

    ma2 = close.rolling(2).mean()

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    c1 = (ma8 + std8) < ma2

    c2 = ma2 < (ma8 - std8)

    c3 = (volume / adv20) >= 1

    return np.where(c1, -1, np.where(c2, 1, np.where(c3, 1, -1)))



def alpha022(high: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * (delta(correlation(high, volume, 5), 5) * rank(stddev(close, 20)))"""

    return -1 * delta(correlation(high, volume, 5), 5) * rank(stddev(close, 20))



def alpha023(high: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((sum(high, 20) / 20) < high) ? (-1 * delta(high, 2)) : 0)"""

    cond = high.rolling(20).mean() < high

    return (-1 * delta(high, 2)).where(cond, 0)



def alpha024(close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((((delta((sum(close, 100) / 100), 100) / delay(close, 100)) < 0.05) || ((delta((sum(close, 100) / 100), 100) / delay(close, 100)) == 0.05)) ? (-1 * (close - ts_min(close, 100))) : (-1 * delta(close, 3)))"""

    ma100 = close.rolling(100).mean()

    cond = (delta(ma100, 100) / delay(close, 100)) <= 0.05

    return (-1 * (close - ts_min(close, 100))).where(cond, -1 * delta(close, 3))



def alpha025(high: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank(((((-1 * returns) * adv20) * vwap) * (high - close)))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return rank((-1 * returns) * adv20 * vwap * (high - close))



def alpha026(high: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """-1 * ts_max(correlation(ts_rank(volume, 5), ts_rank(high, 5), 5), 3)"""

    return -1 * ts_max(correlation(ts_rank(volume, 5), ts_rank(high, 5), 5), 3)



def alpha027(volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((0.5 < rank((sum(correlation(rank(volume), rank(vwap), 6), 2) / 2.0))) ? (-1 * 1) : 1)"""

    inner = rank(correlation(rank(volume), rank(vwap), 6).rolling(2).sum() / 2.0)

    return np.where(inner > 0.5, -1, 1)



def alpha028(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """scale(((correlation(adv20, low, 5) + ((high + low) / 2)) - close))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return scale(correlation(adv20, low, 5) + (high + low) / 2 - close)



def alpha029(close: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(min(product(rank(rank(scale(log(sum(ts_min(rank(rank((-1 * rank(delta((close - 1), 5))))), 2), 1))))), 1), 5) + ts_rank(delay((-1 * returns), 6), 5))"""

    inner = rank(rank(scale(np.log(ts_sum(ts_min(rank(rank(-1 * rank(delta(close - 1, 5)))), 2), 1).replace(0, np.nan)))))

    p = product(inner, 1).rolling(5).min()

    return p + ts_rank(delay(-1 * returns, 6), 5)



def alpha030(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((1.0 - rank(((sign((close - delay(close, 1))) + sign((delay(close, 1) - delay(close, 2)))) + sign((delay(close, 2) - delay(close, 3)))))) * sum(volume, 5)) / sum(volume, 20))"""

    s1 = np.sign(close - delay(close, 1))

    s2 = np.sign(delay(close, 1) - delay(close, 2))

    s3 = np.sign(delay(close, 2) - delay(close, 3))

    return (1.0 - rank(s1 + s2 + s3)) * volume.rolling(5).sum() / volume.rolling(20).sum()



def alpha031(close: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((rank(rank(rank(decay_linear((-1 * rank(rank(delta(close, 10)))), 10)))) + rank((-1 * delta(close, 3)))) + sign(scale(correlation(adv20, low, 12))))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return (rank(rank(rank(decay_linear(-1 * rank(rank(delta(close, 10))), 10)))) + 

            rank(-1 * delta(close, 3)) + 

            np.sign(scale(correlation(adv20, low, 12))))



def alpha032(close: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(scale(((sum(close, 7) / 7) - close)) + (20 * scale(correlation(vwap, delay(close, 5), 230))))"""

    return scale(close.rolling(7).mean() - close) + 20 * scale(correlation(vwap, delay(close, 5), 230))



def alpha033(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank((-1 * ((1 - (open / close))^1)))"""

    return rank(-1 * (1 - open_ / close))



def alpha034(close: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """rank(((1 - rank((stddev(returns, 2) / stddev(returns, 5)))) + (1 - rank(delta(close, 1)))))"""

    return rank((1 - rank(stddev(returns, 2) / stddev(returns, 5))) + (1 - rank(delta(close, 1))))



def alpha035(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((Ts_Rank(volume, 32) * (1 - Ts_Rank(((close + high) - low), 16))) * (1 - Ts_Rank(returns, 32)))"""

    high = close  # simplified if high not separately provided

    low = close

    return ts_rank(volume, 32) * (1 - ts_rank(close + high - low, 16)) * (1 - ts_rank(returns, 32))



def alpha036(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((((2.21 * rank(correlation((close - open), delay(volume, 1), 15))) + (0.7 * rank((open - close)))) + (0.73 * rank(Ts_Rank(delay((-1 * returns), 6), 5)))) + rank(abs(correlation(vwap, adv20, 6)))) + (0.6 * rank((((sum(close, 200) / 200) - open) * (close - open)))))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return (2.21 * rank(correlation(close - open_, delay(volume, 1), 15)) +

            0.7 * rank(open_ - close) +

            0.73 * rank(ts_rank(delay(-1 * returns, 6), 5)) +

            rank(correlation(vwap, adv20, 6).abs()) +

            0.6 * rank((close.rolling(200).mean() - open_) * (close - open_)))



def alpha037(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(rank(correlation(delay((open - close), 1), close, 200)) + rank((open - close)))"""

    return rank(correlation(delay(open_ - close, 1), close, 200)) + rank(open_ - close)



def alpha038(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((-1 * rank(Ts_Rank(close, 10))) * rank((close / open)))"""

    return -1 * rank(ts_rank(close, 10)) * rank(close / open_)



def alpha039(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((-1 * rank((delta(close, 7) * (1 - rank(decay_linear((volume / adv20), 9)))))) * (1 + rank(sum(returns, 250))))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return (-1 * rank(delta(close, 7) * (1 - rank(decay_linear(volume / adv20, 9))))) * \

           (1 + rank(returns.rolling(250).sum()))



def alpha040(high: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((-1 * rank(stddev(high, 10))) * correlation(high, volume, 10))"""

    return -1 * rank(stddev(high, 10)) * correlation(high, volume, 10)



def alpha041(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((high * low)^0.5) - vwap)"""

    return np.sqrt((high * low).clip(lower=0)) - vwap



def alpha042(close: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(rank((vwap - close)) / rank((vwap + close)))"""

    return rank(vwap - close) / rank(vwap + close).replace(0, np.nan)



def alpha043(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(ts_rank((volume / adv20), 20) * ts_rank((-1 * delta(close, 7)), 8))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return ts_rank(volume / adv20, 20) * ts_rank(-1 * delta(close, 7), 8)



def alpha044(high: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(-1 * correlation(high, rank(volume), 5))"""

    return -1 * correlation(high, rank(volume), 5)



def alpha045(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(-1 * ((rank((sum(delay(close, 5), 20) / 20)) * correlation(close, volume, 2)) * rank(correlation(sum(close, 5), sum(close, 20), 2))))"""

    return (-1 * rank(delay(close, 5).rolling(20).sum() / 20) * 

            correlation(close, volume, 2) * 

            rank(correlation(close.rolling(5).sum(), close.rolling(20).sum(), 2)))



def alpha046(close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((0.25 < (((delay(close, 20) - delay(close, 10)) / 10) - ((delay(close, 10) - close) / 10))) ? (-1 * 1) : (((((delay(close, 20) - delay(close, 10)) / 10) - ((delay(close, 10) - close) / 10)) < 0) ? 1 : ((-1 * 1) * (close - delay(close, 1))))))"""

    v = (delay(close, 20) - delay(close, 10)) / 10 - (delay(close, 10) - close) / 10

    return np.where(v > 0.25, -1, np.where(v < 0, 1, -1 * (close - delay(close, 1))))



def alpha047(high: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """((((rank((1 / close)) * volume) / adv20) * ((high * rank((high - close))) / (sum(high, 5) / 5))) - rank((vwap - delay(vwap, 5))))"""

    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

    return (rank(1 / close) * volume / adv20 * (high * rank(high - close)) / (high.rolling(5).mean())) - \

           rank(vwap - delay(vwap, 5))



def alpha048(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(indneutralize(((correlation(delta(close, 1), delta(delay(close, 1), 1), 250) * delta(close, 1)) / close), IndClass.subindustry) / sum(((delta(close, 1) / delay(close, 1))^2), 250))"""

    # indneutralize 需行业信息，简化为无中性化

    dc = delta(close, 1)

    corr_part = correlation(dc, delta(delay(close, 1), 1), 250) * dc / close

    denom = ((dc / delay(close, 1)) ** 2).rolling(250).sum()

    return corr_part / denom



def alpha049(close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(((((delay(close, 20) - delay(close, 10)) / 10) - ((delay(close, 10) - close) / 10)) < (-1 * 0.1)) ? 1 : ((-1 * 1) * (close - delay(close, 1))))"""

    v = (delay(close, 20) - delay(close, 10)) / 10 - (delay(close, 10) - close) / 10

    return np.where(v < -0.1, 1, -1 * (close - delay(close, 1)))



def alpha050(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

    """(-1 * ts_max(rank(correlation(rank(volume), rank(vwap), 5)), 5))"""

    return -1 * ts_max(rank(correlation(rank(volume), rank(vwap), 5)), 5)
```

def alpha051(close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(((((delay(close, 20) - delay(close, 10)) / 10) - ((delay(close, 10) - close) / 10)) < (-1 * 0.1)) ? 1 : ((-1 * 1) * (close - delay(close, 1))))"""

​    v = (delay(close, 20) - delay(close, 10)) / 10 - (delay(close, 10) - close) / 10

​    return np.where(v < -0.1, 1, -1 * (close - delay(close, 1)))

def alpha052(low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((((-1 * ts_min(low, 5)) + delay(ts_min(low, 5), 5)) * rank(((sum(returns, 240) - sum(returns, 20)) / 220))) * ts_rank(volume, 5))"""

​    return ((-1 * ts_min(low, 5) + delay(ts_min(low, 5), 5)) * 

​            rank((returns.rolling(240).sum() - returns.rolling(20).sum()) / 220) * 

​            ts_rank(volume, 5))

def alpha053(close: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(-1 * delta((((close - low) - (high - close)) / (close - low)), 9))"""

​    return -1 * delta(((close - low) - (high - close)) / (close - low).replace(0, np.nan), 9)

def alpha054(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((-1 * ((low - close) * (open^5))) / ((low - high) * (close^5)))"""

​    return -1 * ((low - close) * (open_ ** 5)) / ((low - high) * (close ** 5)).replace(0, np.nan)

def alpha055(close: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(-1 * correlation(rank(((close - ts_min(low, 12)) / (ts_max(high, 12) - ts_min(low, 12)))), rank(volume), 6))"""

​    return -1 * correlation(

​        rank((close - ts_min(low, 12)) / (ts_max(high, 12) - ts_min(low, 12)).replace(0, np.nan)),

​        rank(volume), 6)

def alpha056(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(0 - (1 * (rank((sum(returns, 10) / sum(sum(returns, 2), 3))) * rank((returns * cap)))))"""

​    *# cap = market cap, simplified as volume*

​    cap = volume

​    return -(rank(returns.rolling(10).sum() / returns.rolling(2).sum().rolling(3).sum()) * 

​             rank(returns * cap))

def alpha057(close: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(0 - (1 * ((close - vwap) / decay_linear(rank(ts_argmax(close, 30)), 2))))"""

​    return -(close - vwap) / decay_linear(rank(ts_argmax(close, 30)), 2).replace(0, np.nan)

def alpha058(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(-1 * Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(IndNeutral(vwap, IndClass.sector), volume, 3.92795), 7.89291), 5.50322))"""

​    *# IndNeutral 简化，直接用 vwap*

​    vwap_proxy = close

​    return -1 * ts_rank(decay_linear(correlation(vwap_proxy, volume, 4), 8), 6)

def alpha059(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(-1 * Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(IndNeutral(((vwap * 0.728317) + (vwap * (1 - 0.728317))), IndClass.industry), volume, 4.25197), 16.2289), 8.19648))"""

​    vwap_proxy = close

​    return -1 * ts_rank(decay_linear(correlation(vwap_proxy, volume, 4), 16), 8)

def alpha060(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(0 - (1 * ((2 * scale(rank(((((close - low) - (high - close)) / (high - low)) * volume)))) - scale(rank(ts_argmax(close, 10))))))"""

​    return -(2 * scale(rank(((close - low) - (high - close)) / (high - low).replace(0, np.nan) * volume)) - 

​             scale(rank(ts_argmax(close, 10))))

def alpha061(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(rank((vwap - ts_min(vwap, 16.1219))) < rank(correlation(vwap, adv180, 17.9282)))"""

​    adv180 = volume.rolling(180).mean()

​    return (rank(vwap - ts_min(vwap, 16)) < rank(correlation(vwap, adv180, 18))).astype(float)

def alpha062(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(correlation(vwap, sum(adv20, 22.4101), 9.91009)) < rank(((rank(open) + rank(open)) < (rank(((high + low) / 2)) + rank(high))))) * -1)"""

​    vwap_proxy = (high + low) / 2

​    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

​    c1 = rank(correlation(vwap_proxy, adv20.rolling(22).sum(), 10))

​    c2 = rank((rank(open_) + rank(open_)) < (rank((high + low) / 2) + rank(high)))

​    return -1 * (c1 < c2).astype(float)

def alpha063(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(decay_linear(delta(IndNeutral(close, IndClass.industry), 2.25164), 8.22237)) - rank(decay_linear(correlation(((vwap * 0.318108) + (open * (1 - 0.318108))), sum(adv180, 37.2467), 13.557), 12.2883))) * -1)"""

​    adv180 = volume.rolling(180).mean()

​    return -1 * (rank(decay_linear(delta(close, 2), 8)) - 

​                 rank(decay_linear(correlation(close, adv180.rolling(37).sum(), 14), 12)))

def alpha064(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(correlation(sum(((open * 0.178404) + (low * (1 - 0.178404))), 12.7054), sum(adv120, 12.7054), 16.6208)) < rank(delta(((((high + low) / 2) * 0.178404) + (vwap * (1 - 0.178404))), 3.69741))) * -1)"""

​    adv120 = volume.rolling(120).mean()

​    comp1 = (open_ * 0.178 + low * 0.822).rolling(13).sum()

​    comp2 = adv120.rolling(13).sum()

​    vwap_proxy = (high + low) / 2

​    return -1 * (rank(correlation(comp1, comp2, 17)) < rank(delta(vwap_proxy, 4))).astype(float)

def alpha065(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(correlation(((open * 0.00817205) + (vwap * (1 - 0.00817205))), sum(adv60, 8.6911), 6.40374)) < rank((open - ts_min(open, 13.635)))) * -1)"""

​    adv60 = volume.rolling(60).mean()

​    vwap_proxy = close

​    comp = open_ * 0.008 + vwap_proxy * 0.992

​    return -1 * (rank(correlation(comp, adv60.rolling(9).sum(), 6)) < 

​                 rank(open_ - ts_min(open_, 14))).astype(float)

def alpha066(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(decay_linear(delta(vwap, 3.51013), 7.23052)) + Ts_Rank(decay_linear(((((low * 0.96633) + (low * (1 - 0.96633))) - vwap) / (open - ((high + low) / 2))), 11.4157), 6.72611)) * -1)"""

​    return -1 * (rank(decay_linear(delta(vwap, 4), 7)) + 

​                 ts_rank(decay_linear((low - vwap) / (open_ - (high + low) / 2).replace(0, np.nan), 11), 7))

def alpha067(high: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank((high - ts_min(high, 2.14593)))^rank(correlation(IndNeutral(vwap, IndClass.sector), IndNeutral(adv20, IndClass.subindustry), 6.02936))) * -1)"""

​    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()

​    return -1 * (rank(high - ts_min(high, 2)) ** rank(correlation(vwap, adv20, 6)))

def alpha068(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((Ts_Rank(correlation(rank(high), rank(adv15), 8.91644), 13.9333) < rank(delta(((close * 0.518371) + (low * (1 - 0.518371))), 1.06157))) * -1)"""

​    adv15 = volume.rolling(15).mean()

​    comp = close * 0.518 + low * 0.482

​    return -1 * (ts_rank(correlation(rank(high), rank(adv15), 9), 14) < 

​                 rank(delta(comp, 1))).astype(float)

def alpha069(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(ts_max(delta(IndNeutral(vwap, IndClass.industry), 2.72412), 4.79344))^Ts_Rank(correlation(((close * 0.490655) + (vwap * (1 - 0.490655))), adv20, 4.92416), 9.0615)) * -1)"""

​                 ts_rank(correlation(comp, adv20, 5), 9))

def alpha070(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(delta(vwap, 1.29456))^Ts_Rank(correlation(IndNeutral(close, IndClass.industry), adv50, 17.8256), 17.9171)) * -1)"""

​    adv50 = volume.rolling(50).mean()

​    return -1 * (rank(delta(vwap, 1)) ** ts_rank(correlation(close, adv50, 18), 18))

def alpha071(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """max(Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(Ts_Rank(close, 3.43976), Ts_Rank(adv180, 12.0647), 18.0175), 4.20501), 15.6948), Ts_Rank(decay_linear((rank(((low + open) - (vwap + vwap)))^2), 16.4662), 4.4388))"""

​    adv180 = volume.rolling(180).mean()

​    part1 = ts_rank(decay_linear(correlation(ts_rank(close, 3), ts_rank(adv180, 12), 18), 4), 16)

​    part2 = ts_rank(decay_linear(rank((low + open_) - 2 * vwap) ** 2, 16), 4)

​    return pd.concat([part1, part2], axis=1).max(axis=1)

def alpha072(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(rank(decay_linear(correlation(((high + low) / 2), adv40, 8.93345), 10.1519)) / rank(decay_linear(correlation(Ts_Rank(vwap, 3.72469), Ts_Rank(volume, 18.5188), 6.86671), 2.95011)))"""

​    adv40 = volume.rolling(40).mean()

​    hl_mid = (high + low) / 2

​    num = rank(decay_linear(correlation(hl_mid, adv40, 9), 10))

​    denom = rank(decay_linear(correlation(ts_rank(vwap, 4), ts_rank(volume, 19), 7), 3))

​    return num / denom.replace(0, np.nan)

def alpha073(open_: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(max(rank(decay_linear(delta(vwap, 4.72775), 2.91864)), Ts_Rank(decay_linear(((delta(((open * 0.147155) + (low * (1 - 0.147155))), 2.03608) / ((open * 0.147155) + (low * (1 - 0.147155)))) * -1), 3.33829), 16.7411)) * -1)"""

​    comp = open_ * 0.147 + low * 0.853

​    part1 = rank(decay_linear(delta(vwap, 5), 3))

​    part2 = ts_rank(decay_linear(-1 * delta(comp, 2) / comp.replace(0, np.nan), 3), 17)

​    return -1 * pd.concat([part1, part2], axis=1).max(axis=1)

​    """(max(rank(decay_linear(delta(vwap, 1.24383), 11.8259)), Ts_Rank(decay_linear(Ts_Rank(correlation(IndNeutral(low, IndClass.sector), adv81, 8.14941), 19.569), 17.1543), 19.383)) * -1)"""

def alpha077(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """min(rank(decay_linear(((((high + low) / 2) + high) - (vwap + high)), 20.0451)), rank(decay_linear(correlation(((high + low) / 2), adv40, 3.1614), 5.64125)))"""

​    part1 = rank(decay_linear(hl_mid + high - vwap - high, 20))

​    part2 = rank(decay_linear(correlation(hl_mid, adv40, 3), 6))

​    return pd.concat([part1, part2], axis=1).min(axis=1)

def alpha078(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(rank(correlation(sum(((low * 0.352233) + (vwap * (1 - 0.352233))), 19.7428), sum(adv40, 19.7428), 6.83313))^rank(correlation(rank(vwap), rank(volume), 5.77492)))"""

​            rank(correlation(rank(vwap), rank(volume), 6)))

def alpha080(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(Sign(delta(IndNeutral(((open * 0.868128) + (high * (1 - 0.868128))), IndClass.industry), 4.04545)))^Ts_Rank(correlation(high, adv10, 5.11456), 5.53756)) * -1)"""

​    comp = open_ * 0.868 + high * 0.132

​                 ts_rank(correlation(high, adv10, 5), 6))

def alpha081(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(Log(product(rank((rank(correlation(vwap, sum(adv10, 49.6054), 8.47743))^4)), 14.9655))) < rank(correlation(rank(vwap), rank(volume), 5.07914))) * -1)"""

​    adv10 = volume.rolling(10).mean()

​    inner = rank(correlation(vwap, adv10.rolling(50).sum(), 8)) ** 4

​    part1 = rank(np.log(product(rank(inner), 15).replace(0, np.nan)))

​    part2 = rank(correlation(rank(vwap), rank(volume), 5))

​    return -1 * (part1 < part2).astype(float)

def alpha082(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(min(rank(decay_linear(delta(open, 1.46063), 14.8717)), Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(IndNeutral(volume, IndClass.sector), ((open * 0.634196) + (open * (1 - 0.634196))), 17.4842), 6.92131), 13.4283)) * -1)"""

​    part1 = rank(decay_linear(delta(open_, 1), 15))

​    part2 = ts_rank(decay_linear(correlation(volume, open_, 17), 7), 13)

​    return -1 * pd.concat([part1, part2], axis=1).min(axis=1)

def alpha083(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((rank(delay(((high - low) / (sum(close, 5) / 5)), 2)) * rank(rank(volume))) / (((high - low) / (sum(close, 5) / 5)) / (vwap - close)))"""

​    hl_range = (high - low) / (close.rolling(5).mean()).replace(0, np.nan)

​    num = rank(delay(hl_range, 2)) * rank(rank(volume))

​    denom = hl_range / (vwap - close).replace(0, np.nan)

​    return num / denom

def alpha084(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """SignedPower(Ts_Rank((vwap - ts_max(vwap, 15.3217)), 20.7127), delta(close, 4.96796))"""

​    return signed_power(ts_rank(vwap - ts_max(vwap, 15), 21), delta(close, 5))

def alpha085(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​            rank(correlation(ts_rank(comp2, 4), ts_rank(volume, 10), 7)))

​    """(max(rank(decay_linear(delta(((close * 0.369701) + (vwap * (1 - 0.369701))), 1.91233), 2.65461)), Ts_Rank(decay_linear(abs(correlation(IndNeutral(adv81, IndClass.industry), close, 13.4132)), 4.89768), 14.4535)) * -1)"""

def alpha088(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """min(rank(decay_linear(((rank(open) + rank(low)) - (rank(high) + rank(close))), 8.06882)), Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(Ts_Rank(close, 8.44728), Ts_Rank(adv60, 20.6966), 8.01266), 6.65053), 2.61957))"""

​    return pd.concat([part1, part2], axis=1).min(axis=1)

def alpha089(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """(Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(((low * 0.967285) + (low * (1 - 0.967285))), adv10, 6.94279), 5.51607), 3.79744) - Ts_Rank(decay_linear(delta(IndNeutral(vwap, IndClass.industry), 3.48158), 10.1466), 15.3012))"""

def alpha091(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """((Ts_Rank(decay_linear(decay_linear(correlation(IndNeutral(close, IndClass.industry), volume, 9.74928), 16.398), 3.83219), 4.8667) - rank(decay_linear(correlation(vwap, adv30, 4.01303), 2.6809))) * -1)"""
