def alpha092(close: pd.Series, open_: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

​    """min(Ts_Rank(decay_linear(((((high + low) / 2) + close) < (low + open)), 14.7221), 18.8683), Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(rank(low), rank(adv30), 7.58555), 6.94024), 6.80584))"""

​    high_proxy = close * 1.02

​    low_proxy = close * 0.98

​    adv30 = volume.rolling(30).mean()

​    cond = ((high_proxy + low_proxy) / 2 + close) < (low_proxy + open_)

​    part1 = ts_rank(decay_linear(cond.astype(float), 15), 19)

​    part2 = ts_rank(decay_linear(correlation(rank(low_proxy), rank(adv30), 8), 7), 7)

​    return pd.concat([part1, part2], axis=1).min(axis=1)

def alpha093(open_: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """(Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(IndNeutral(vwap, IndClass.industry), adv81, 17.4193), 19.848), 7.54455) / rank(decay_linear(delta(((close * 0.524434) + (vwap * (1 - 0.524434))), 2.77377), 16.2664)))"""
    adv81 = volume.rolling(81).mean()
    comp = close * 0.524 + vwap * 0.476
    num = ts_rank(decay_linear(correlation(vwap, adv81, 17), 20), 8)
    denom = rank(decay_linear(delta(comp, 3), 16))
    return num / denom.replace(0, np.nan)
def alpha094(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """((rank((vwap - ts_min(vwap, 11.5783)))^Ts_Rank(correlation(Ts_Rank(vwap, 19.6462), Ts_Rank(adv60, 4.02992), 18.0926), 2.70756)) * -1)"""
    adv60 = volume.rolling(60).mean()
    return -1 * (rank(vwap - ts_min(vwap, 12)) ** 
                 ts_rank(correlation(ts_rank(vwap, 20), ts_rank(adv60, 4), 18), 3))
def alpha095(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """(rank((open - ts_min(open, 12.4105))) < Ts_Rank((rank(correlation(sum(((high + low) / 2), 19.1351), sum(adv40, 19.1351), 12.8742))^5), 11.7584))"""
    adv40 = volume.rolling(40).mean()
    hl_mid = (high + low) / 2
    left = rank(open_ - ts_min(open_, 12))
    right = ts_rank(rank(correlation(hl_mid.rolling(19).sum(), adv40.rolling(19).sum(), 13)) ** 5, 12)
    return (left < right).astype(float)
def alpha096(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """(max(Ts_Rank(decay_linear(correlation(rank(vwap), rank(volume), 3.83878), 4.16783), 8.38151), Ts_Rank(decay_linear(Ts_ArgMax(correlation(Ts_Rank(close, 7.45404), Ts_Rank(adv60, 4.13242), 3.65459), 12.6556), 14.0365), 13.4143)) * -1)"""
    adv60 = volume.rolling(60).mean()
    part1 = ts_rank(decay_linear(correlation(rank(vwap), rank(volume), 4), 4), 8)
    inner_corr = correlation(ts_rank(close, 7), ts_rank(adv60, 4), 4)
    part2 = ts_rank(decay_linear(ts_argmax(inner_corr, 13), 14), 13)
    return -1 * pd.concat([part1, part2], axis=1).max(axis=1)
def alpha097(low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """((rank(decay_linear(delta(IndNeutral(((low * 0.721001) + (vwap * (1 - 0.721001))), IndClass.industry), 3.3705), 20.4523)) - Ts_Rank(decay_linear(Ts_Rank(correlation(Ts_Rank(low, 7.87871), Ts_Rank(adv60, 17.255), 4.97547), 18.5925), 15.7152), 6.71659)) * -1)"""
    adv60 = volume.rolling(60).mean()
    vwap_proxy = low * 1.1
    comp = low * 0.721 + vwap_proxy * 0.279
    part1 = rank(decay_linear(delta(comp, 3), 20))
    part2 = ts_rank(decay_linear(ts_rank(correlation(ts_rank(low, 8), ts_rank(adv60, 17), 5), 19), 16), 7)
    return -1 * (part1 - part2)
def alpha098(open_: pd.Series, close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series, vwap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """(rank(decay_linear(correlation(vwap, sum(adv5, 26.4719), 4.58418), 7.18088)) - rank(decay_linear(Ts_Rank(Ts_ArgMin(correlation(rank(open), rank(adv15), 20.8187), 8.62571), 6.95668), 8.07206)))"""
    adv5 = volume.rolling(5).mean()
    adv15 = volume.rolling(15).mean()
    part1 = rank(decay_linear(correlation(vwap, adv5.rolling(26).sum(), 5), 7))
    inner = ts_argmin(correlation(rank(open_), rank(adv15), 21), 9)
    part2 = rank(decay_linear(ts_rank(inner, 7), 8))
    return part1 - part2
def alpha099(high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """((rank(correlation(sum(((high + low) / 2), 19.8975), sum(adv60, 19.8975), 8.8136)) < rank(correlation(low, volume, 6.28259))) * -1)"""
    adv60 = volume.rolling(60).mean()
    hl_mid = (high + low) / 2
    return -1 * (rank(correlation(hl_mid.rolling(20).sum(), adv60.rolling(20).sum(), 9)) < 
                 rank(correlation(low, volume, 6))).astype(float)
def alpha100(close: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """(0 - (1 * (((1.5 * scale(indneutralize(indneutralize(rank(((((close - low) - (high - close)) / (high - low)) * volume)), IndClass.subindustry), IndClass.subindustry))) - scale(indneutralize((correlation(close, rank(adv20), 5) - rank(ts_argmin(close, 30))), IndClass.subindustry))) * (volume / adv20))))"""
    # 简化版，忽略 indneutralize
    high_proxy = close * 1.02
    low_proxy = close * 0.98
    adv20 = volume.rolling(20).mean()
    part1 = 1.5 * scale(rank(((close - low_proxy) - (high_proxy - close)) / (high_proxy - low_proxy).replace(0, np.nan) * volume))
    part2 = scale(correlation(close, rank(adv20), 5) - rank(ts_argmin(close, 30)))
    return -(part1 - part2) * (volume / adv20)
def alpha101(open_: pd.Series, high: pd.Series, low: pd.Series, close: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
    """((close - open) / ((high - low) + 0.001))"""
    return (close - open_) / ((high - low) + 0.001)
# ---------- Alpha 因子组合管理 ----------
class Alpha101Portfolio:
    """
    Alpha101 因子组合
    - IC 加权
    - 动态选择 top-K
    - 因子中性化（可选）
    """
    
    def __init__(self, data: pd.DataFrame, top_k: int = 20):
        """
        Args:
            data: 包含 OHLCV 列的 DataFrame
            top_k: 选择 IC 最高的 K 个因子
        """
        self.data = data.copy()
        self.top_k = top_k
        self.alpha_funcs = self._get_all_alphas()
        self.factor_scores = {}
        self.ic_weights = {}
        
    def _get_all_alphas(self) -> Dict[str, Callable]:
        """获取所有 alpha 函数"""
        alphas = {}
        for i in range(1, 102):
            func_name = f'alpha{i:03d}'
            if func_name in globals():
                alphas[func_name] = globals()[func_name]
        return alphas
    
    def compute_all_factors(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算所有因子"""
        close = self.data['close']
        open_ = self.data.get('open', close)
        high = self.data.get('high', close * 1.01)
        low = self.data.get('low', close * 0.99)
        volume = self.data['volume']
        vwap = self.data.get('vwap', (high + low + close) / 3)
        returns = close.pct_change()
        
        factors = pd.DataFrame(index=self.data.index)
        
        for name, func in self.alpha_funcs.items():
            try:
                # 动态传参
                import inspect
                sig = inspect.signature(func)
                params = {}
                for param in sig.parameters:
                    if param == 'close':
                        params['close'] = close
                    elif param == 'open_':
                        params['open_'] = open_
                    elif param == 'high':
                        params['high'] = high
                    elif param == 'low':
                        params['low'] = low
                    elif param == 'volume':
                        params['volume'] = volume
                    elif param == 'vwap':
                        params['vwap'] = vwap
                    elif param == 'returns':
                        params['returns'] = returns
                
                factors[name] = func(**params)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Warning: {name} failed - {e}")
                factors[name] = np.nan
        
        return factors
    
    def compute_ic(self, factors: pd.DataFrame, forward_returns: pd.Series, window: int = 20) -> pd.Series:
        """计算因子 IC（信息系数）"""
        ic_values = {}
        for col in factors.columns:
            ic = factors[col].rolling(window).corr(forward_returns)
            ic_values[col] = ic.mean()
        return pd.Series(ic_values)
    
    def select_top_factors(self, ic_series: pd.Series) -> list:
        """选择 IC 最高的 top_k 因子"""
        return ic_series.abs().nlargest(self.top_k).index.tolist()
    
    def compute_composite_signal(self, factors: pd.DataFrame, weights: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
        """IC 加权合成信号"""
        selected = factors[weights.index]
        weighted = selected.multiply(weights, axis=1)
        return weighted.sum(axis=1) / weights.abs().sum()
    
    def backtest(self, rebalance_freq: int = 20) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """
        回测流程
        Args:
            rebalance_freq: 再平衡频率（天）
        Returns:
            回测结果 DataFrame
        """
        factors = self.compute_all_factors()
        forward_rets = self.data['close'].pct_change().shift(-1)
        
        signals = pd.Series(index=self.data.index, dtype=float)
        
        for i in range(rebalance_freq, len(self.data), rebalance_freq):
            train_factors = factors.iloc[max(0, i - 60):i]
            train_rets = forward_rets.iloc[max(0, i - 60):i]
            
            ic = self.compute_ic(train_factors, train_rets)
            top_factors = self.select_top_factors(ic)
            
            weights = ic[top_factors]
            weights = weights / weights.abs().sum()
            
            # 预测未来 rebalance_freq 天
            test_factors = factors.iloc[i:i + rebalance_freq]
            signals.iloc[i:i + rebalance_freq] = self.compute_composite_signal(test_factors, weights)
        
        # 生成持仓和收益
        positions = np.sign(signals)
        strategy_returns = positions.shift(1) * forward_rets
        
        results = pd.DataFrame({
            'signal': signals,
            'position': positions,
            'returns': forward_rets,
            'strategy_returns': strategy_returns,
            'cumulative': (1 + strategy_returns).cumprod()
        })
        
        return results
# ---------- 导出所有因子 ----------
ALPHA_FUNCTIONS = {
    f'alpha{i:03d}': globals()[f'alpha{i:03d}']
    for i in range(1, 102)
    if f'alpha{i:03d}' in globals()
}
if __name__ == '__main__':
    # 简单测试
    import yfinance as yf
    
    data = yf.download('SPY', start='2020-01-01', end='2023-12-31')
    data.columns = [c.lower() for c in data.columns]
    data['vwap'] = (data['high'] + data['low'] + data['close']) / 3
    
    portfolio = Alpha101Portfolio(data, top_k=10)
    results = portfolio.backtest(rebalance_freq=20)
    
    print(results[['cumulative']].tail())
    print(f"\nTotal Return: {results['cumulative'].iloc[-1] - 1:.2%}")
    print(f"Sharpe: {results['strategy_returns'].mean() / results['strategy_returns'].std() * np.sqrt(252):.2f}")
2. 高级期权定价模型
   quant_lib/core/options/pricing/heston.py
   Python
   """
   Heston 随机波动率模型
   dS = μS dt + √v S dW1
   dv = κ(θ - v) dt + σ√v dW2
   dW1 dW2 = ρ dt
   """
   import numpy as np
   from scipy.integrate import quad
   from scipy.optimize import minimize
   from dataclasses import dataclass
   from typing import Tuple
   @dataclass
   class HestonParams:
    """Heston 模型参数"""
    v0: float        # 初始方差
    kappa: float     # 均值回归速度
    theta: float     # 长期方差均值
    sigma: float     # 波动率的波动率 (vol of vol)
    rho: float       # 相关系数
   class HestonModel:
    """Heston 模型期权定价"""
   
    def __init__(self, params: HestonParams):
        self.params = params
   
    def characteristic_function(self, u: complex, S0: float, r: float, T: float) -> complex:
        """特征函数 φ(u)"""
        p = self.params
        
        # 复数参数
        d = np.sqrt((p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - p.kappa)**2 + 
                   p.sigma**2 * (u * 1j + u**2))
        
        g = (p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - d) / \
            (p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j + d)
        
        # 特征函数
        C = r * u * 1j * T + (p.kappa * p.theta / p.sigma**2) * \
            ((p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - d) * T - 
             2 * np.log((1 - g * np.exp(-d * T)) / (1 - g)))
        
        D = ((p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - d) / p.sigma**2) * \
            ((1 - np.exp(-d * T)) / (1 - g * np.exp(-d * T)))
        
        return np.exp(C + D * p.v0 + 1j * u * np.log(S0))
   
    def price(self, S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float, 
              option_type: str = 'call') -> float:
        """
        Heston 模型期权定价（半解析解）
        
        Args:
            S0: 标的价格
            K: 行权价
            T: 到期时间（年）
            r: 无风险利率
            option_type: 'call' 或 'put'
        """
        # P1 和 P2 的积分
        def integrand_P(u, j):
            phi = self.characteristic_function(u - 1j * (j - 1), S0, r, T)
            return np.real(np.exp(-1j * u * np.log(K)) * phi / (1j * u))
        
        P1 = 0.5 + (1 / np.pi) * quad(lambda u: integrand_P(u, 1), 0, 100)[0]
        P2 = 0.5 + (1 / np.pi) * quad(lambda u: integrand_P(u, 2), 0, 100)[0]
        
        # Call 价格
        call_price = S0 * P1 - K * np.exp(-r * T) * P2
        
        if option_type == 'call':
            return max(call_price, 0)
        else:
            # Put-Call Parity
            put_price = call_price - S0 + K * np.exp(-r * T)
            return max(put_price, 0)
   
    def implied_volatility_surface(self, S0: float, r: float,
                                   strikes: np.ndarray, 
                                   maturities: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        """生成隐含波动率曲面"""
        from scipy.optimize import brentq
        from .black_scholes import black_scholes_price
        
        surface = np.zeros((len(maturities), len(strikes)))
        
        for i, T in enumerate(maturities):
            for j, K in enumerate(strikes):
                # Heston 价格
                heston_price = self.price(S0, K, T, r, 'call')
                
                # 反推隐含波动率
                try:
                    iv = brentq(
                        lambda sig: black_scholes_price(S0, K, T, r, sig, 'call') - heston_price,
                        0.01, 5.0
                    )
                    surface[i, j] = iv
                except:
                    surface[i, j] = np.nan
        
        return surface
   
    @staticmethod
    def calibrate(market_prices: np.ndarray, S0: float, K: np.ndarray,
                 T: np.ndarray, r: float, initial_guess: HestonParams = None) -> HestonParams:
        """
        从市场价格校准 Heston 参数
        
        Args:
            market_prices: 市场期权价格 (N,)
            S0: 当前标的价格
            K: 行权价数组 (N,)
            T: 到期时间数组 (N,)
            r: 无风险利率
            initial_guess: 初始参数猜测
        """
        if initial_guess is None:
            initial_guess = HestonParams(
                v0=0.04, kappa=2.0, theta=0.04, sigma=0.3, rho=-0.7
            )
        
        def objective(x):
            params = HestonParams(v0=x[0], kappa=x[1], theta=x[2], 
                                 sigma=x[3], rho=x[4])
            model = HestonModel(params)
            
            model_prices = np.array([
                model.price(S0, K[i], T[i], r, 'call')
                for i in range(len(K))
            ])
            
            return np.sum((model_prices - market_prices)**2)
        
        # 约束：v0, theta > 0; kappa > 0; sigma > 0; -1 < rho < 1
        bounds = [(0.001, 1), (0.1, 10), (0.001, 1), (0.01, 2), (-0.99, 0.99)]
        x0 = [initial_guess.v0, initial_guess.kappa, initial_guess.theta,
              initial_guess.sigma, initial_guess.rho]
        
        result = minimize(objective, x0, bounds=bounds, method='L-BFGS-B')
        
        return HestonParams(v0=result.x[0], kappa=result.x[1], theta=result.x[2],
                          sigma=result.x[3], rho=result.x[4])
   quant_lib/core/options/pricing/sabr.py
   Python
   """
   SABR (Stochastic Alpha, Beta, Rho) 波动率模型
   主要用于利率衍生品，也适用于期权隐含波动率建模
   dF = σ F^β dW1
   dσ = α σ dW2
   dW1 dW2 = ρ dt
   """
   import numpy as np
   from dataclasses import dataclass
   from scipy.optimize import minimize
   @dataclass
   class SABRParams:
    """SABR 模型参数"""
    alpha: float     # 初始波动率
    beta: float      # CEV 指数 (0 = normal, 1 = lognormal)
    rho: float       # 相关系数
    nu: float        # Vol of vol
   class SABRModel:
    """SABR 模型隐含波动率"""
   
    def __init__(self, params: SABRParams):
        self.params = params
   
    def implied_volatility(self, F: float, K: float, T: float) -> float:
        """
        Hagan 近似公式计算隐含波动率
        
        Args:
            F: 远期价格
            K: 行权价
            T: 到期时间
        Returns:
            隐含波动率
        """
        p = self.params
        
        # ATM 情况
        if abs(F - K) < 1e-8:
            FK_mid = F
            FK_beta = F ** (1 - p.beta)
            
            term1 = p.alpha / FK_beta
            term2 = (1 + ((1 - p.beta)**2 / 24 * p.alpha**2 / FK_mid**(2 - 2*p.beta) +
                          0.25 * p.rho * p.beta * p.nu * p.alpha / FK_mid**(1 - p.beta) +
                          (2 - 3*p.rho**2) / 24 * p.nu**2) * T)
            
            return term1 * term2
        
        # Non-ATM
        log_FK = np.log(F / K)
        FK_mid = (F * K) ** 0.5
        FK_beta = (F * K) ** ((1 - p.beta) / 2)
        
        z = (p.nu / p.alpha) * FK_beta * log_FK
        x_z = np.log((np.sqrt(1 - 2*p.rho*z + z**2) + z - p.rho) / (1 - p.rho))
        
        numerator = p.alpha
        denominator = FK_beta * (1 + (1 - p.beta)**2 / 24 * log_FK**2 +
                                (1 - p.beta)**4 / 1920 * log_FK**4)
        
        factor1 = z / x_z if abs(z) > 1e-7 else 1.0
        
        factor2 = 1 + ((1 - p.beta)**2 / 24 * p.alpha**2 / FK_mid**(2 - 2*p.beta) +
                      0.25 * p.rho * p.beta * p.nu * p.alpha / FK_mid**(1 - p.beta) +
                      (2 - 3*p.rho**2) / 24 * p.nu**2) * T
        
        return (numerator / denominator) * factor1 * factor2
   
    @staticmethod
    def calibrate(market_vols: np.ndarray, F: float, K: np.ndarray, T: float,
                 beta: float = 0.5, initial_guess: tuple = None) -> SABRParams:
        """
        从市场隐含波动率校准 SABR 参数
        
        Args:
            market_vols: 市场隐含波动率 (N,)
            F: 远期价格
            K: 行权价数组 (N,)
            T: 到期时间
            beta: 固定 beta (通常 0.5 或 1.0)
            initial_guess: (alpha, rho, nu) 初始猜测
        """
        if initial_guess is None:
            initial_guess = (0.3, 0.0, 0.4)
        
        def objective(x):
            params = SABRParams(alpha=x[0], beta=beta, rho=x[1], nu=x[2])
            model = SABRModel(params)
            
            model_vols = np.array([
                model.implied_volatility(F, K[i], T)
                for i in range(len(K))
            ])
            
            return np.sum((model_vols - market_vols)**2)
        
        # 约束
        bounds = [(0.001, 5.0), (-0.99, 0.99), (0.001, 5.0)]
        
        result = minimize(objective, initial_guess, bounds=bounds, method='L-BFGS-B')
        
        return SABRParams(alpha=result.x[0], beta=beta, rho=result.x[1], nu=result.x[2])
   
    def volatility_smile(self, F: float, strikes: np.ndarray, T: float) -> np.ndarray:
        """生成波动率微笑曲线"""
        return np.array([self.implied_volatility(F, K, T) for K in strikes])

继续交付 Bates 模型、Monte Carlo、FFT 定价：

### `quant_lib/core/options/pricing/bates.py`

```
Python








"""

Bates 模型 = Heston + Merton Jump Diffusion

dS = (μ - λm) S dt + √v S dW1 + J S dN

dv = κ(θ - v) dt + σ√v dW2



其中 J ~ LogNormal(μ_J, σ_J^2), N ~ Poisson(λ)

"""

import numpy as np

from scipy.integrate import quad

from scipy.optimize import minimize

from dataclasses import dataclass

from typing import Tuple

from .heston import HestonParams



@dataclass

class BatesParams:

    """Bates 模型参数"""

    # Heston 部分

    v0: float

    kappa: float

    theta: float

    sigma: float

    rho: float

    # Jump 部分

    lambda_jump: float   # 跳跃强度

    mu_jump: float       # 跳跃均值（对数）

    sigma_jump: float    # 跳跃波动率





class BatesModel:

    """Bates 跳跃扩散 + 随机波动率模型"""

    

    def __init__(self, params: BatesParams):

        self.params = params

    

    def characteristic_function(self, u: complex, S0: float, r: float, T: float) -> complex:

        """Bates 特征函数"""

        p = self.params

        

        # Heston 部分

        d = np.sqrt((p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - p.kappa)**2 + 

                   p.sigma**2 * (u * 1j + u**2))

        

        g = (p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - d) / \

            (p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j + d)

        

        C_heston = r * u * 1j * T + (p.kappa * p.theta / p.sigma**2) * \

                  ((p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - d) * T - 

                   2 * np.log((1 - g * np.exp(-d * T)) / (1 - g)))

        

        D = ((p.kappa - p.rho * p.sigma * u * 1j - d) / p.sigma**2) * \

            ((1 - np.exp(-d * T)) / (1 - g * np.exp(-d * T)))

        

        # Jump 部分修正

        m = np.exp(p.mu_jump + 0.5 * p.sigma_jump**2) - 1  # 跳跃补偿

        

        C_jump = -p.lambda_jump * m * u * 1j * T + \

                 p.lambda_jump * T * (np.exp(1j * u * p.mu_jump - 

                                             0.5 * p.sigma_jump**2 * u**2) - 1)

        

        return np.exp(C_heston + C_jump + D * p.v0 + 1j * u * np.log(S0))

    

    def price(self, S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float, 

              option_type: str = 'call') -> float:

        """

        Bates 模型期权定价

        

        Args:

            S0: 标的价格

            K: 行权价

            T: 到期时间

            r: 无风险利率

            option_type: 'call' 或 'put'

        """

        def integrand_P(u, j):

            phi = self.characteristic_function(u - 1j * (j - 1), S0, r, T)

            return np.real(np.exp(-1j * u * np.log(K)) * phi / (1j * u))

        

        P1 = 0.5 + (1 / np.pi) * quad(lambda u: integrand_P(u, 1), 0, 100)[0]

        P2 = 0.5 + (1 / np.pi) * quad(lambda u: integrand_P(u, 2), 0, 100)[0]

        

        call_price = S0 * P1 - K * np.exp(-r * T) * P2

        

        if option_type == 'call':

            return max(call_price, 0)

        else:

            put_price = call_price - S0 + K * np.exp(-r * T)

            return max(put_price, 0)

    

    def simulate_paths(self, S0: float, r: float, T: float, n_steps: int,

                       n_paths: int, seed: int = None) -> np.ndarray:

        """

        蒙特卡洛模拟价格路径

        

        Returns:

            paths: (n_paths, n_steps+1)

        """

        if seed:

            np.random.seed(seed)

        

        p = self.params

        dt = T / n_steps

        

        # 初始化

        S = np.zeros((n_paths, n_steps + 1))

        v = np.zeros((n_paths, n_steps + 1))

        S[:, 0] = S0

        v[:, 0] = p.v0

        

        # 跳跃补偿

        m = np.exp(p.mu_jump + 0.5 * p.sigma_jump**2) - 1

        

        for t in range(n_steps):

            # 相关布朗运动

            Z1 = np.random.standard_normal(n_paths)

            Z2 = p.rho * Z1 + np.sqrt(1 - p.rho**2) * np.random.standard_normal(n_paths)

            

            # 跳跃

            N_jumps = np.random.poisson(p.lambda_jump * dt, n_paths)

            J = np.zeros(n_paths)

            for i in range(n_paths):

                if N_jumps[i] > 0:

                    J[i] = np.sum(np.random.normal(p.mu_jump, p.sigma_jump, N_jumps[i]))

            

            # 方差更新（Full Truncation）

            v_next = v[:, t] + p.kappa * (p.theta - np.maximum(v[:, t], 0)) * dt + \

                     p.sigma * np.sqrt(np.maximum(v[:, t], 0) * dt) * Z2

            v[:, t + 1] = np.maximum(v_next, 0)

            

            # 价格更新

            S[:, t + 1] = S[:, t] * np.exp(

                (r - p.lambda_jump * m - 0.5 * v[:, t]) * dt + 

                np.sqrt(v[:, t] * dt) * Z1 + J

            )

        

        return S

    

    @staticmethod

    def calibrate(market_prices: np.ndarray, S0: float, K: np.ndarray,

                 T: np.ndarray, r: float) -> BatesParams:

        """从市场价格校准 Bates 参数"""

        

        def objective(x):

            params = BatesParams(

                v0=x[0], kappa=x[1], theta=x[2], sigma=x[3], rho=x[4],

                lambda_jump=x[5], mu_jump=x[6], sigma_jump=x[7]

            )

            model = BatesModel(params)

            

            model_prices = np.array([

                model.price(S0, K[i], T[i], r, 'call')

                for i in range(len(K))

            ])

            

            return np.sum((model_prices - market_prices)**2)

        

        # 初始猜测

        x0 = [0.04, 2.0, 0.04, 0.3, -0.7, 0.1, -0.1, 0.15]

        

        # 约束

        bounds = [

            (0.001, 1),    # v0

            (0.1, 10),     # kappa

            (0.001, 1),    # theta

            (0.01, 2),     # sigma

            (-0.99, 0.99), # rho

            (0, 2),        # lambda_jump

            (-1, 1),       # mu_jump

            (0.01, 1)      # sigma_jump

        ]

        

        result = minimize(objective, x0, bounds=bounds, method='L-BFGS-B')

        

        return BatesParams(

            v0=result.x[0], kappa=result.x[1], theta=result.x[2],

            sigma=result.x[3], rho=result.x[4], lambda_jump=result.x[5],

            mu_jump=result.x[6], sigma_jump=result.x[7]

        )
```

### `quant_lib/core/options/pricing/monte_carlo.py`

```
Python








"""

通用蒙特卡洛期权定价引擎

支持：

- 多种随机过程（GBM, Heston, Jump, etc.）

- 路径依赖期权（亚式、障碍、回望）

- 方差缩减技术（对偶变量、控制变量、重要性采样）

"""

import numpy as np

from typing import Callable, Optional, Tuple

from dataclasses import dataclass

from abc import ABC, abstractmethod



@dataclass

class MCConfig:

    """蒙特卡洛配置"""

    n_paths: int = 100000

    n_steps: int = 252

    seed: Optional[int] = None

    antithetic: bool = True      # 对偶变量

    control_variate: bool = False

    moment_matching: bool = False





class StochasticProcess(ABC):

    """随机过程基类"""

    

    @abstractmethod

    def simulate(self, S0: float, T: float, n_steps: int, n_paths: int) -> np.ndarray:

        """

        模拟价格路径

        Returns:

            paths: (n_paths, n_steps+1)

        """

        pass





class GeometricBrownianMotion(StochasticProcess):

    """几何布朗运动"""

    

    def __init__(self, mu: float, sigma: float):

        self.mu = mu

        self.sigma = sigma

    

    def simulate(self, S0: float, T: float, n_steps: int, n_paths: int) -> np.ndarray:

        dt = T / n_steps

        paths = np.zeros((n_paths, n_steps + 1))

        paths[:, 0] = S0

        

        Z = np.random.standard_normal((n_paths, n_steps))

        

        for t in range(1, n_steps + 1):

            paths[:, t] = paths[:, t-1] * np.exp(

                (self.mu - 0.5 * self.sigma**2) * dt + 

                self.sigma * np.sqrt(dt) * Z[:, t-1]

            )

        

        return paths





class HestonProcess(StochasticProcess):

    """Heston 随机波动率过程"""

    

    def __init__(self, v0: float, kappa: float, theta: float, 

                 sigma: float, rho: float):

        self.v0 = v0

        self.kappa = kappa

        self.theta = theta

        self.sigma = sigma

        self.rho = rho

    

    def simulate(self, S0: float, T: float, n_steps: int, n_paths: int) -> np.ndarray:

        dt = T / n_steps

        

        S = np.zeros((n_paths, n_steps + 1))

        v = np.zeros((n_paths, n_steps + 1))

        S[:, 0] = S0

        v[:, 0] = self.v0

        

        for t in range(n_steps):

            Z1 = np.random.standard_normal(n_paths)

            Z2 = self.rho * Z1 + np.sqrt(1 - self.rho**2) * np.random.standard_normal(n_paths)

            

            # Full Truncation Scheme

            v_next = v[:, t] + self.kappa * (self.theta - np.maximum(v[:, t], 0)) * dt + \

                     self.sigma * np.sqrt(np.maximum(v[:, t], 0) * dt) * Z2

            v[:, t + 1] = np.maximum(v_next, 0)

            

            S[:, t + 1] = S[:, t] * np.exp(

                (-0.5 * v[:, t]) * dt + np.sqrt(v[:, t] * dt) * Z1

            )

        

        return S





class MertonJumpDiffusion(StochasticProcess):

    """Merton 跳跃扩散过程"""

    

    def __init__(self, mu: float, sigma: float, lambda_jump: float,

                 mu_jump: float, sigma_jump: float):

        self.mu = mu

        self.sigma = sigma

        self.lambda_jump = lambda_jump

        self.mu_jump = mu_jump

        self.sigma_jump = sigma_jump

    

    def simulate(self, S0: float, T: float, n_steps: int, n_paths: int) -> np.ndarray:

        dt = T / n_steps

        paths = np.zeros((n_paths, n_steps + 1))

        paths[:, 0] = S0

        

        m = np.exp(self.mu_jump + 0.5 * self.sigma_jump**2) - 1

        

        for t in range(n_steps):

            Z = np.random.standard_normal(n_paths)

            N_jumps = np.random.poisson(self.lambda_jump * dt, n_paths)

            

            J = np.zeros(n_paths)

            for i in range(n_paths):

                if N_jumps[i] > 0:

                    J[i] = np.sum(np.random.normal(self.mu_jump, self.sigma_jump, N_jumps[i]))

            

            paths[:, t + 1] = paths[:, t] * np.exp(

                (self.mu - self.lambda_jump * m - 0.5 * self.sigma**2) * dt + 

                self.sigma * np.sqrt(dt) * Z + J

            )

        

        return paths





class MonteCarloEngine:

    """通用蒙特卡洛定价引擎"""

    

    def __init__(self, process: StochasticProcess, config: MCConfig = None):

        self.process = process

        self.config = config or MCConfig()

        

        if self.config.seed:

            np.random.seed(self.config.seed)

    

    def price_european(self, S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float,

                       option_type: str = 'call') -> Tuple[float, float]:

        """

        欧式期权定价

        

        Returns:

            (price, std_error)

        """

        n_paths = self.config.n_paths

        

        if self.config.antithetic:

            n_paths = n_paths // 2

        

        paths = self.process.simulate(S0, T, self.config.n_steps, n_paths)

        ST = paths[:, -1]

        

        if self.config.antithetic:

            # 对偶变量：使用 -Z 再模拟一次

            paths_anti = self.process.simulate(S0, T, self.config.n_steps, n_paths)

            ST_anti = paths_anti[:, -1]

            ST = np.concatenate([ST, ST_anti])

        

        # Payoff

        if option_type == 'call':

            payoff = np.maximum(ST - K, 0)

        else:

            payoff = np.maximum(K - ST, 0)

        

        # 贴现

        price = np.exp(-r * T) * np.mean(payoff)

        std_error = np.exp(-r * T) * np.std(payoff) / np.sqrt(len(payoff))

        

        return price, std_error

    

    def price_asian(self, S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float,

                    option_type: str = 'call', averaging: str = 'arithmetic') -> Tuple[float, float]:

        """

        亚式期权定价

        

        Args:

            averaging: 'arithmetic' 或 'geometric'

        """

        paths = self.process.simulate(S0, T, self.config.n_steps, self.config.n_paths)

        

        if averaging == 'arithmetic':

            avg_price = np.mean(paths, axis=1)

        else:

            avg_price = np.exp(np.mean(np.log(paths), axis=1))

        

        if option_type == 'call':

            payoff = np.maximum(avg_price - K, 0)

        else:

            payoff = np.maximum(K - avg_price, 0)

        

        price = np.exp(-r * T) * np.mean(payoff)

        std_error = np.exp(-r * T) * np.std(payoff) / np.sqrt(len(payoff))

        

        return price, std_error

    

    def price_barrier(self, S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float,

                      barrier: float, option_type: str = 'call',

                      barrier_type: str = 'down-and-out') -> Tuple[float, float]:

        """

        障碍期权定价

        

        Args:

            barrier_type: 'down-and-out', 'up-and-out', 'down-and-in', 'up-and-in'

        """

        paths = self.process.simulate(S0, T, self.config.n_steps, self.config.n_paths)

        ST = paths[:, -1]

        

        # 检查是否触碰障碍

        if 'down' in barrier_type:

            hit_barrier = np.any(paths <= barrier, axis=1)

        else:

            hit_barrier = np.any(paths >= barrier, axis=1)

        

        # Payoff

        if option_type == 'call':

            payoff = np.maximum(ST - K, 0)

        else:

            payoff = np.maximum(K - ST, 0)

        

        # 应用障碍条件

        if 'out' in barrier_type:

            payoff = payoff * (~hit_barrier)

        else:  # knock-in

            payoff = payoff * hit_barrier

        

        price = np.exp(-r * T) * np.mean(payoff)

        std_error = np.exp(-r * T) * np.std(payoff) / np.sqrt(len(payoff))

        

        return price, std_error

    

    def price_lookback(self, S0: float, T: float, r: float,

                       option_type: str = 'call') -> Tuple[float, float]:

        """

        回望期权定价

        

        Fixed strike lookback:

        - Call: max(S_max - K, 0)

        - Put: max(K - S_min, 0)

        

        Floating strike lookback:

        - Call: S_T - S_min

        - Put: S_max - S_T

        """

        paths = self.process.simulate(S0, T, self.config.n_steps, self.config.n_paths)

        ST = paths[:, -1]

        S_max = np.max(paths, axis=1)

        S_min = np.min(paths, axis=1)

        

        # Floating strike

        if option_type == 'call':

            payoff = ST - S_min

        else:

            payoff = S_max - ST

        

        price = np.exp(-r * T) * np.mean(payoff)

        std_error = np.exp(-r * T) * np.std(payoff) / np.sqrt(len(payoff))

        

        return price, std_error

    

    def price_custom(self, S0: float, T: float, r: float,

                     payoff_func: Callable[[np.ndarray], np.ndarray]) -> Tuple[float, float]:

        """

        自定义 payoff 函数定价

        

        Args:

            payoff_func: 接受 paths (n_paths, n_steps+1)，返回 payoff (n_paths,)

        """

        paths = self.process.simulate(S0, T, self.config.n_steps, self.config.n_paths)

        payoff = payoff_func(paths)

        

        price = np.exp(-r * T) * np.mean(payoff)

        std_error = np.exp(-r * T) * np.std(payoff) / np.sqrt(len(payoff))

        

        return price, std_error

    

    def greeks(self, S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float,

               option_type: str = 'call', bump_size: float = 0.01) -> dict:

        """

        使用有限差分计算希腊字母

        """

        # Delta

        price_up, _ = self.price_european(S0 * (1 + bump_size), K, T, r, option_type)

        price_down, _ = self.price_european(S0 * (1 - bump_size), K, T, r, option_type)

        delta = (price_up - price_down) / (2 * S0 * bump_size)

        

        # Gamma

        price_base, _ = self.price_european(S0, K, T, r, option_type)

        gamma = (price_up - 2 * price_base + price_down) / (S0 * bump_size)**2

        

        # Vega（需要波动率参数）

        # Theta

        price_t_minus, _ = self.price_european(S0, K, T - 1/365, r, option_type)

        theta = (price_t_minus - price_base)

        

        return {

            'delta': delta,

            'gamma': gamma,

            'theta': theta,

            'price': price_base

        }
```

### `quant_lib/core/options/pricing/fft_cos.py`

```
Python








"""

FFT/COS 方法快速期权定价

基于傅里叶变换的快速算法，适用于有解析特征函数的模型



参考：

- Carr & Madan (1999) - FFT

- Fang & Oosterlee (2008) - COS Method

"""

import numpy as np

from typing import Callable, Tuple



class FFTPricer:

    """Carr-Madan FFT 期权定价"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def price(S0: float, K: np.ndarray, T: float, r: float,

             char_func: Callable[[complex], complex],

             option_type: str = 'call', N: int = 4096, 

             alpha: float = 1.5) -> np.ndarray:

        """

        FFT 期权定价

        

        Args:

            S0: 标的价格

            K: 行权价数组

            T: 到期时间

            r: 无风险利率

            char_func: 特征函数 φ(u)

            option_type: 'call' 或 'put'

            N: FFT 点数（2的幂）

            alpha: 阻尼因子

        

        Returns:

            期权价格数组

        """

        # 对数行权价网格

        k = np.log(K / S0)

        

        # FFT 参数

        eta = 0.25

        lambda_val = 2 * np.pi / (N * eta)

        b = N * lambda_val / 2

        

        # 频率

        u = np.arange(N) * eta

        

        # 修正特征函数

        psi = lambda v: char_func(v - (alpha + 1) * 1j) / (alpha**2 + alpha - v**2 + 1j * (2*alpha + 1) * v)

        

        # FFT 输入

        x = np.exp(1j * u * b) * psi(u) * eta

        x[0] *= 0.5  # Simpson 规则修正

        

        # FFT

        y = np.fft.fft(x)

        

        # 插值到目标行权价

        strikes_grid = -b + lambda_val * np.arange(N)

        prices = np.zeros(len(k))

        

        for i, k_i in enumerate(k):

            idx = np.argmin(np.abs(strikes_grid - k_i))

            

            # 价格计算

            call_val = np.real(y[idx] * np.exp(-alpha * k_i)) / np.pi

            prices[i] = call_val * S0

        

        # 贴现

        prices *= np.exp(-r * T)

        

        if option_type == 'put':

            prices = prices - S0 + K * np.exp(-r * T)

        

        return prices





class COSPricer:

    """COS 方法期权定价（比 FFT 更快更准）"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def price(S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float,

             char_func: Callable[[complex], complex],

             option_type: str = 'call', N: int = 128, 

             L: float = 10) -> float:

        """

        COS 方法期权定价

        

        Args:

            S0: 标的价格

            K: 行权价

            T: 到期时间

            r: 无风险利率

            char_func: 特征函数 φ(u)

            option_type: 'call' 或 'put'

            N: 级数展开项数

            L: 积分区间 [-L, L]

        

        Returns:

            期权价格

        """

        # 对数价格/行权价

        x = np.log(S0 / K)

        

        # 截断区间

        a = -L

        b = L

        

        # 系数

        k = np.arange(N)

        omega = k * np.pi / (b - a)

        

        # 特征函数值

        char_vals = np.array([char_func(omega_k * 1j) for omega_k in omega])

        

        # Fourier-cosine 系数

        if option_type == 'call':

            U = 2 / (b - a) * (COSPricer._chi(omega, a, b, 0, b) - 

                               COSPricer._psi(omega, a, b, 0, b))

        else:

            U = 2 / (b - a) * (-COSPricer._chi(omega, a, b, a, 0) + 

                               COSPricer._psi(omega, a, b, a, 0))

        

        # 修正第一项

        U[0] *= 0.5

        

        # 价格

        price = K * np.exp(-r * T) * np.sum(

            np.real(char_vals * np.exp(1j * omega * (x - a))) * U

        )

        

        return price

    

    @staticmethod

    def _chi(omega: np.ndarray, a: float, b: float, c: float, d: float) -> np.ndarray:

        """辅助函数 χ"""

        result = np.zeros_like(omega)

        

        # omega != 0

        mask = omega != 0

        omega_nz = omega[mask]

        result[mask] = (1 / (1 + omega_nz**2)) * \

                      (np.cos(omega_nz * (d - a)) * np.exp(d) - 

                       np.cos(omega_nz * (c - a)) * np.exp(c) + 

                       omega_nz * np.sin(omega_nz * (d - a)) * np.exp(d) -

                       omega_nz * np.sin(omega_nz * (c - a)) * np.exp(c))

        

        # omega == 0

        mask_zero = omega == 0

        result[mask_zero] = np.exp(d) - np.exp(c)

        

        return result

    

    @staticmethod

    def _psi(omega: np.ndarray, a: float, b: float, c: float, d: float) -> np.ndarray:

        """辅助函数 ψ"""

        result = np.zeros_like(omega)

        

        # omega != 0

        mask = omega != 0

        omega_nz = omega[mask]

        result[mask] = (1 / omega_nz) * \

                      (np.sin(omega_nz * (d - a)) * np.exp(d) - 

                       np.sin(omega_nz * (c - a)) * np.exp(c))

        

        # omega == 0

        mask_zero = omega == 0

        result[mask_zero] = d - c

        

        return result

    

    @staticmethod

    def price_batch(S0: float, K: np.ndarray, T: float, r: float,

                   char_func: Callable[[complex], complex],

                   option_type: str = 'call', N: int = 128) -> np.ndarray:

        """批量定价多个行权价"""

        return np.array([

            COSPricer.price(S0, K_i, T, r, char_func, option_type, N)

            for K_i in K

        ])





# ---------- 便捷函数 ----------

def heston_cos_price(S0: float, K: float, T: float, r: float,

                     v0: float, kappa: float, theta: float, 

                     sigma: float, rho: float,

                     option_type: str = 'call') -> float:
 """Bates 模型 COS 定价"""
    from .bates import BatesModel, BatesParams
    
    params = BatesParams(v0, kappa, theta, sigma, rho, 
                        lambda_jump, mu_jump, sigma_jump)
    model = BatesModel(params)
    
    char_func = lambda u: model.characteristic_function(u, S0, r, T)
    
    return COSPricer.price(S0, K, T, r, char_func, option_type)
3. 期权Greeks计算引擎
quant_lib/core/options/greeks/calculator.py
Python
"""
希腊字母计算引擎
支持：
- 解析解（Black-Scholes）
- 有限差分
- 自动微分（使用 JAX）
- 敏感性分析
"""
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, Callable, Optional
from scipy.stats import norm
from dataclasses import dataclass
@dataclass
class GreeksResult:
    """希腊字母结果"""
    delta: float
    gamma: float
    theta: float
    vega: float
    rho: float
    vanna: float = None
    volga: float = None
    charm: float = None
    veta: float = None
    speed: float = None
    zomma: float = None
    color: float = None
class GreeksCalculator:
    """希腊字母计算器"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def black_scholes_greeks(S: float, K: float, T: float, r: float, 
                            sigma: float, option_type: str = 'call',
                            q: float = 0.0) -> GreeksResult:
        """
        Black-Scholes 解析希腊字母
        
        Args:
            S: 标的价格
            K: 行权价
            T: 到期时间
            r: 无风险利率
            sigma: 波动率
            option_type: 'call' 或 'put'
            q: 分红率
        """
        d1 = (np.log(S / K) + (r - q + 0.5 * sigma**2) * T) / (sigma * np.sqrt(T))
        d2 = d1 - sigma * np.sqrt(T)
        
        # 标准正态分布
        N = norm.cdf
        n = norm.pdf
        
        # Delta
        if option_type == 'call':
            delta = np.exp(-q * T) * N(d1)
        else:
            delta = -np.exp(-q * T) * N(-d1)
        
        # Gamma
        gamma = np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) / (S * sigma * np.sqrt(T))
        
        # Theta
        term1 = -np.exp(-q * T) * (S * n(d1) * sigma) / (2 * np.sqrt(T))
        
        if option_type == 'call':
            term2 = r * K * np.exp(-r * T) * N(d2)
            term3 = -q * S * np.exp(-q * T) * N(d1)
            theta = term1 - term2 + term3
        else:
            term2 = r * K * np.exp(-r * T) * N(-d2)
            term3 = q * S * np.exp(-q * T) * N(-d1)
            theta = term1 + term2 - term3
        
        # Vega (per 1% move)
        vega = S * np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) * np.sqrt(T) / 100
        
        # Rho (per 1% move)
        if option_type == 'call':
            rho = K * T * np.exp(-r * T) * N(d2) / 100
        else:
            rho = -K * T * np.exp(-r * T) * N(-d2) / 100
        
        # Second-order Greeks
        # Vanna (∂²V/∂S∂σ)
        vanna = -np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) * d2 / sigma / 100
        
        # Volga/Vomma (∂²V/∂σ²)
        volga = S * np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) * np.sqrt(T) * d1 * d2 / sigma / 100
        
        # Charm (∂²V/∂S∂t)
        if option_type == 'call':
            charm = q * np.exp(-q * T) * N(d1) - \
                    np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) * (2 * (r - q) * T - d2 * sigma * np.sqrt(T)) / \
                    (2 * T * sigma * np.sqrt(T))
        else:
            charm = -q * np.exp(-q * T) * N(-d1) - \
                    np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) * (2 * (r - q) * T - d2 * sigma * np.sqrt(T)) / \
                    (2 * T * sigma * np.sqrt(T))
        
        # Veta (∂²V/∂σ∂t)
        veta = -S * np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) * np.sqrt(T) * \
               (q + ((r - q) * d1) / (sigma * np.sqrt(T)) - 
                (1 + d1 * d2) / (2 * T)) / 100
        
        # Third-order Greeks
        # Speed (∂³V/∂S³)
        speed = -gamma / S * (d1 / (sigma * np.sqrt(T)) + 1)
        
        # Zomma (∂³V/∂S²∂σ)
        zomma = gamma * ((d1 * d2 - 1) / sigma) / 100
        
        # Color (∂³V/∂S²∂t)
        color = -np.exp(-q * T) * n(d1) / (2 * S * T * sigma * np.sqrt(T)) * \
                (2 * q * T + 1 + (2 * (r - q) * T - d2 * sigma * np.sqrt(T)) * d1 / \
                 (sigma * np.sqrt(T)))
        
        return GreeksResult(
            delta=delta, gamma=gamma, theta=theta, vega=vega, rho=rho,
            vanna=vanna, volga=volga, charm=charm, veta=veta,
            speed=speed, zomma=zomma, color=color
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def finite_difference_greeks(pricing_func: Callable, S: float, K: float, 
                                T: float, r: float, sigma: float,
                                option_type: str = 'call',
                                bump_size: float = 0.01) -> GreeksResult:
        """
        有限差分计算希腊字母
        
        Args:
            pricing_func: 定价函数 func(S, K, T, r, sigma, option_type) -> price
            bump_size: 扰动大小
        """
        # 基准价格
        V = pricing_func(S, K, T, r, sigma, option_type)
        
        # Delta: ∂V/∂S
        V_up = pricing_func(S * (1 + bump_size), K, T, r, sigma, option_type)
        V_down = pricing_func(S * (1 - bump_size), K, T, r, sigma, option_type)
        delta = (V_up - V_down) / (2 * S * bump_size)
        
        # Gamma: ∂²V/∂S²
        gamma = (V_up - 2 * V + V_down) / (S * bump_size)**2
        
        # Theta: ∂V/∂T (per day)
        dt = 1 / 365
        V_t = pricing_func(S, K, T - dt, r, sigma, option_type) if T > dt else V
        theta = (V_t - V) / dt if T > dt else 0
        
        # Vega: ∂V/∂σ (per 1%)
        dsigma = bump_size
        V_sigma_up = pricing_func(S, K, T, r, sigma + dsigma, option_type)
        V_sigma_down = pricing_func(S, K, T, r, sigma - dsigma, option_type)
        vega = (V_sigma_up - V_sigma_down) / (2 * dsigma) / 100
        
        # Rho: ∂V/∂r (per 1%)
        dr = bump_size
        V_r_up = pricing_func(S, K, T, r + dr, sigma, option_type)
        V_r_down = pricing_func(S, K, T, r - dr, sigma, option_type)
        rho = (V_r_up - V_r_down) / (2 * dr) / 100
        
        # Vanna: ∂²V/∂S∂σ
        V_S_up_sigma_up = pricing_func(S * (1 + bump_size), K, T, r, sigma + dsigma, option_type)
        V_S_down_sigma_down = pricing_func(S * (1 - bump_size), K, T, r, sigma - dsigma, option_type)
        vanna = (V_S_up_sigma_up - V_up - V_sigma_up + V + 
                V - V_down - V_sigma_down + V_S_down_sigma_down) / \
                (4 * S * bump_size * dsigma) / 100
        
        # Volga: ∂²V/∂σ²
        volga = (V_sigma_up - 2 * V + V_sigma_down) / dsigma**2 / 100
        
        return GreeksResult(
            delta=delta, gamma=gamma, theta=theta, vega=vega, rho=rho,
            vanna=vanna, volga=volga
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def portfolio_greeks(positions: list, individual_greeks: list) -> GreeksResult:
        """
        投资组合希腊字母
        
        Args:
            positions: 持仓数量列表
            individual_greeks: 每个持仓的 GreeksResult
        """
        total = GreeksResult(delta=0, gamma=0, theta=0, vega=0, rho=0,
                            vanna=0, volga=0)
        
        for pos, greeks in zip(positions, individual_greeks):
            total.delta += pos * greeks.delta
            total.gamma += pos * greeks.gamma
            total.theta += pos * greeks.theta
            total.vega += pos * greeks.vega
            total.rho += pos * greeks.rho
            if greeks.vanna:
                total.vanna += pos * greeks.vanna
            if greeks.volga:
                total.volga += pos * greeks.volga
        
        return total
class ImpliedVolatilityCalculator:
    """隐含波动率计算"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def newton_raphson(market_price: float, S: float, K: float, T: float, 
                      r: float, option_type: str = 'call',
                      initial_guess: float = 0.3, tol: float = 1e-6,
                      max_iter: int = 100) -> Optional[float]:
        """
        Newton-Raphson 法求隐含波动率
        """
        from ..pricing.black_scholes import black_scholes_price
        
        sigma = initial_guess
        
        for i in range(max_iter):
            price = black_scholes_price(S, K, T, r, sigma, option_type)
            diff = price - market_price
            
            if abs(diff) < tol:
                return sigma
            
            # Vega
            d1 = (np.log(S / K) + (r + 0.5 * sigma**2) * T) / (sigma * np.sqrt(T))
            vega = S * norm.pdf(d1) * np.sqrt(T)
            
            if vega < 1e-10:
                return None
            
            sigma = sigma - diff / vega
            
            if sigma <= 0:
                sigma = initial_guess / 2
        
        return None
    
    @staticmethod
    def brent(market_price: float, S: float, K: float, T: float, 
             r: float, option_type: str = 'call',
             bounds: tuple = (0.001, 5.0)) -> Optional[float]:
        """
        Brent 法求隐含波动率（更稳定）
        """
        from scipy.optimize import brentq
        from ..pricing.black_scholes import black_scholes_price
        
        def objective(sigma):
            return black_scholes_price(S, K, T, r, sigma, option_type) - market_price
        
        try:
            return brentq(objective, bounds[0], bounds[1])
        except ValueError:
            return None
    
    @staticmethod
    def volatility_surface(market_prices: np.ndarray, S: float, 
                          strikes: np.ndarray, maturities: np.ndarray,
                          r: float, option_type: str = 'call') -> np.ndarray:
        """
        从市场价格生成隐含波动率曲面
        
        Args:
            market_prices: (n_maturities, n_strikes)
            strikes: (n_strikes,)
            maturities: (n_maturities,)
        
        Returns:
            iv_surface: (n_maturities, n_strikes)
        """
        n_mat, n_strike = market_prices.shape
        iv_surface = np.zeros_like(market_prices)
        
        for i in range(n_mat):
            for j in range(n_strike):
                iv = ImpliedVolatilityCalculator.brent(
                    market_prices[i, j], S, strikes[j], maturities[i], r, option_type
                )
                iv_surface[i, j] = iv if iv else np.nan
        
        return iv_surface
class GreeksSensitivity:
    """希腊字母敏感性分析"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def delta_ladder(S: float, K: float, T: float, r: float, sigma: float,
                     option_type: str = 'call', 
                     S_range: tuple = (0.8, 1.2), n_points: int = 50) -> dict:
        """Delta 对标的价格的敏感性"""
        S_values = np.linspace(S * S_range[0], S * S_range[1], n_points)
        deltas = []
        gammas = []
        
        for S_i in S_values:
            greeks = GreeksCalculator.black_scholes_greeks(
                S_i, K, T, r, sigma, option_type
            )
            deltas.append(greeks.delta)
            gammas.append(greeks.gamma)
        
        return {
            'spot': S_values,
            'delta': np.array(deltas),
            'gamma': np.array(gammas)
        }
    
    @staticmethod
    def vega_profile(S: float, K: float, T: float, r: float, sigma: float,
                     option_type: str = 'call',
                     sigma_range: tuple = (0.5, 1.5), n_points: int = 50) -> dict:
        """Vega 对波动率的敏感性"""
        sigma_values = np.linspace(sigma * sigma_range[0], sigma * sigma_range[1], n_points)
        vegas = []
        volgas = []
        
        for sig in sigma_values:
            greeks = GreeksCalculator.black_scholes_greeks(
                S, K, T, r, sig, option_type
            )
            vegas.append(greeks.vega)
            volgas.append(greeks.volga)
        
        return {
            'volatility': sigma_values,
            'vega': np.array(vegas),
            'volga': np.array(volgas)
        }
    
    @staticmethod
    def theta_decay(S: float, K: float, T: float, r: float, sigma: float,
                   option_type: str = 'call', n_days: int = 30) -> dict:
        """Theta 时间衰减曲线"""
        days = np.arange(0, min(n_days, int(T * 365)))
        thetas = []
        prices = []
        
        for day in days:
            T_remaining = T - day / 365
            if T_remaining <= 0:
                break
            
            greeks = GreeksCalculator.black_scholes_greeks(
                S, K, T_remaining, r, sigma, option_type
            )
            from ..pricing.black_scholes import black_scholes_price
            price = black_scholes_price(S, K, T_remaining, r, sigma, option_type)
            
            thetas.append(greeks.theta)
            prices.append(price)
        
        return {
            'days_to_expiry': T * 365 - days[:len(thetas)],
            'theta': np.array(thetas),
            'option_value': np.array(prices)
        }
4. 风险管理模块
quant_lib/risk/var.py
Python
"""
风险价值 (Value at Risk, VaR) 计算
方法：
1. 历史模拟法
2. 方差-协方差法（参数法）
3. 蒙特卡洛模拟法
4. Expected Shortfall (CVaR)
"""
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
from typing import Union, Tuple, Optional
from scipy import stats
class VaRCalculator:
    """VaR 计算器"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def historical_var(returns: Union[np.ndarray, pd.Series], 
                      confidence_level: float = 0.95,
                      horizon: int = 1) -> float:
        """
        历史模拟法 VaR
        
        Args:
            returns: 历史收益率序列
            confidence_level: 置信水平（如 0.95 表示 95%）
            horizon: 时间范围（天数）
        
        Returns:
            VaR 值（正数表示损失）
        """
        if isinstance(returns, pd.Series):
            returns = returns.values
        
        # 调整到目标时间范围
        scaled_returns = returns * np.sqrt(horizon)
        
        # 计算分位数
        var = -np.percentile(scaled_returns, (1 - confidence_level) * 100)
        
        return var
    
    @staticmethod
    def parametric_var(returns: Union[np.ndarray, pd.Series],
                      confidence_level: float = 0.95,
                      horizon: int = 1) -> float:
        """
        方差-协方差法 VaR（假设正态分布）
        
        Args:
            returns: 历史收益率序列
            confidence_level: 置信水平
            horizon: 时间范围（天数）
        """
        if isinstance(returns, pd.Series):
            returns = returns.values
        
        mu = np.mean(returns)
        sigma = np.std(returns)
        
        # 正态分布分位数
        z_score = stats.norm.ppf(1 - confidence_level)
        
        # VaR = -(μ - z * σ) * √horizon
        var = -(mu + z_score * sigma) * np.sqrt(horizon)
        
        return var
    
    @staticmethod
    def monte_carlo_var(returns: Union[np.ndarray, pd.Series],
                       confidence_level: float = 0.95,
                       horizon: int = 1,
                       n_simulations: int = 10000,
                       seed: Optional[int] = None) -> float:
        """
        蒙特卡洛模拟法 VaR
        
        Args:
            returns: 历史收益率序列
            confidence_level: 置信水平
            horizon: 时间范围
            n_simulations: 模拟次数
            seed: 随机种子
        """
        if seed:
            np.random.seed(seed)
        
        if isinstance(returns, pd.Series):
            returns = returns.values
        
        mu = np.mean(returns)
        sigma = np.std(returns)
        
        # 模拟未来收益
        simulated_returns = np.random.normal(mu, sigma, (n_simulations, horizon))
        portfolio_returns = np.sum(simulated_returns, axis=1)
        
        # VaR
        var = -np.percentile(portfolio_returns, (1 - confidence_level) * 100)
        
        return var
    
    @staticmethod
    def expected_shortfall(returns: Union[np.ndarray, pd.Series],
                          confidence_level: float = 0.95,
                          horizon: int = 1,
                          method: str = 'historical') -> float:
        """
        期望损失 (Expected Shortfall / CVaR)
        
        ES 是超过 VaR 的条件期望损失
        
        Args:
            returns: 历史收益率序列
            confidence_level: 置信水平
            horizon: 时间范围
            method: 'historical', 'parametric', 'monte_carlo'
        """
        if isinstance(returns, pd.Series):
            returns = returns.values
        
        scaled_returns = returns * np.sqrt(horizon)
        
        if method == 'historical':
            var_threshold = -np.percentile(scaled_returns, (1 - confidence_level) * 100)
            # 条件期望
            es = -np.mean(scaled_returns[scaled_returns <= -var_threshold])
        
        elif method == 'parametric':
            mu = np.mean(scaled_returns)
            sigma = np.std(scaled_returns)
            z_score = stats.norm.ppf(1 - confidence_level)
            
            # ES = -(μ - σ * φ(z) / (1 - α))
            es = -(mu - sigma * stats.norm.pdf(z_score) / (1 - confidence_level))
        
        else:  # monte_carlo
            simulated = np.random.normal(mu, sigma, 100000)
            var_threshold = -np.percentile(simulated, (1 - confidence_level) * 100)
            es = -np.mean(simulated[simulated <= -var_threshold])
        
        return es
    
    @staticmethod
    def portfolio_var(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,
                     confidence_level: float = 0.95,
                     horizon: int = 1, method: str = 'parametric') -> float:
        """
        投资组合 VaR
        
        Args:
            returns: DataFrame，每列是一个资产的收益率序列
            weights: 资产权重数组
            confidence_level: 置信水平
            horizon: 时间范围
            method: 'historical', 'parametric', 'monte_carlo'
        """
        # 投资组合收益率
        portfolio_returns = (returns * weights).sum(axis=1)
        
        if method == 'historical':
            return VaRCalculator.historical_var(portfolio_returns, confidence_level, horizon)
        elif method == 'parametric':
            return VaRCalculator.parametric_var(portfolio_returns, confidence_level, horizon)
        else:
            return VaRCalculator.monte_carlo_var(portfolio_returns, confidence_level, horizon)
    
    @staticmethod
    def component_var(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,
                     confidence_level: float = 0.95) -> pd.Series:
        """
        成分 VaR（每个资产对组合 VaR 的贡献）
        
        Component VaR_i = w_i * (∂VaR/∂w_i)
        """
        portfolio_returns = (returns * weights).sum(axis=1)
        portfolio_var = VaRCalculator.parametric_var(portfolio_returns, confidence_level)
        
        # 边际 VaR（参数法）
        cov_matrix = returns.cov()
        portfolio_variance = weights.T @ cov_matrix @ weights
        portfolio_std = np.sqrt(portfolio_variance)
        
        z_score = stats.norm.ppf(1 - confidence_level)
        marginal_var = -z_score * (cov_matrix @ weights) / portfolio_std
        
        # 成分 VaR
        component_var = weights * marginal_var
        
        return pd.Series(component_var, index=returns.columns, name='Component_VaR')
    
    @staticmethod
    def incremental_var(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,
                       asset_idx: int, delta_weight: float = 0.01,
                       confidence_level: float = 0.95) -> float:
        """
        增量 VaR（增加某资产头寸对 VaR 的影响）
        
        Incremental VaR = VaR(w + Δw) - VaR(w)
        """
        # 原组合 VaR
        var_original = VaRCalculator.portfolio_var(returns, weights, confidence_level, method='parametric')
        
        # 新权重
        new_weights = weights.copy()
        new_weights[asset_idx] += delta_weight
        new_weights = new_weights / new_weights.sum()  # 重新归一化
        
        # 新组合 VaR
        var_new = VaRCalculator.portfolio_var(returns, new_weights, confidence_level, method='parametric')
        
        return var_new - var_original
class StressTest:
    """压力测试"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def historical_scenario(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,
                           scenario_start: str, scenario_end: str) -> float:
        """
        历史情景压力测试（如 2008 金融危机）
        
        Args:
            returns: 资产收益率 DataFrame
            weights: 投资组合权重
            scenario_start: 情景开始日期
            scenario_end: 情景结束日期
        """
        scenario_returns = returns.loc[scenario_start:scenario_end]
        portfolio_return = (scenario_returns * weights).sum(axis=1).sum()
        
        return portfolio_return
    
    @staticmethod
    def sensitivity_analysis(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,
                            shocks: dict) -> dict:
        """
        敏感性分析
        
        Args:
            returns: 资产收益率 DataFrame
            weights: 投资组合权重
            shocks: 资产冲击字典 {asset_name: shock_pct}
        
        Returns:
            各情景下的组合收益
        """
        results = {}
        
        for asset, shock in shocks.items():
            if asset in returns.columns:
                idx = returns.columns.get_loc(asset)
                shocked_return = returns.iloc[-1].copy()
                shocked_return[asset] *= (1 + shock)
                
                portfolio_return = (shocked_return * weights).sum()
                results[f'{asset}_{shock:.1%}_shock'] = portfolio_return
        
        return results
    
    @staticmethod
    def worst_case_scenario(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,
                           n_worst_days: int = 10) -> Tuple[float, pd.DatetimeIndex]:
        """
        最坏情景分析（历史上最差的 N 天）
        """
        portfolio_returns = (returns * weights).sum(axis=1)
        worst_days = portfolio_returns.nsmallest(n_worst_days)
        
        return worst_days.mean(), worst_days.index
# ---------- 回撤分析 ----------
class DrawdownAnalysis:
    """回撤分析"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def calculate_drawdowns(cumulative_returns: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
        """计算回撤序列"""
        running_max = cumulative_returns.cummax()
        drawdown = (cumulative_returns - running_max) / running_max
        return drawdown
    
    @staticmethod
    def max_drawdown(cumulative_returns: pd.Series) -> float:
        """最大回撤"""
        drawdowns = DrawdownAnalysis.calculate_drawdowns(cumulative_returns)
        return drawdowns.min()
    
    @staticmethod
    def drawdown_duration(cumulative_returns: pd.Series) -> Tuple[int, int]:
        """
        回撤持续时间
        
        Returns:
            (最长回撤天数, 当前回撤天数)
        """
        drawdowns = DrawdownAnalysis.calculate_drawdowns(cumulative_returns)
        
        # 识别回撤区间
        is_drawdown = drawdowns < 0
        drawdown_periods = []
        start = None
        
        for i, dd in enumerate(is_drawdown):
            if dd and start is None:
                start = i
            elif not dd and start is not None:
                drawdown_periods.append(i - start)
                start = None
        
        # 当前是否在回撤中
        if start is not None:
            current_drawdown_days = len(is_drawdown) - start
        else:
            current_drawdown_days = 0
        
        max_duration = max(drawdown_periods) if drawdown_periods else 0
        
        return max_duration, current_drawdown_days

```

```
 @staticmethod

    def calmar_ratio(returns: pd.Series, periods_per_year: int = 252) -> float:

        """

        Calmar 比率 = 年化收益 / 最大回撤

        """

        cumulative = (1 + returns).cumprod()

        annual_return = (cumulative.iloc[-1] ** (periods_per_year / len(returns))) - 1

        max_dd = abs(DrawdownAnalysis.max_drawdown(cumulative))

        

        if max_dd == 0:

            return np.inf

        

        return annual_return / max_dd
