### `quant_lib/risk/portfolio_risk.py`

```
Python








"""

投资组合风险度量

- 波动率

- 相关性

- Beta

- 追踪误差

- 信息比率

"""

import numpy as np

import pandas as pd

from typing import Union, Tuple, Optional



class PortfolioRisk:

    """投资组合风险分析"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def portfolio_volatility(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,

                            annualize: bool = True, 

                            periods_per_year: int = 252) -> float:

        """

        投资组合波动率

        

        σ_p = √(w^T Σ w)

        """

        cov_matrix = returns.cov()

        portfolio_variance = weights.T @ cov_matrix @ weights

        portfolio_vol = np.sqrt(portfolio_variance)

        

        if annualize:

            portfolio_vol *= np.sqrt(periods_per_year)

        

        return portfolio_vol

    

    @staticmethod

    def marginal_volatility(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray) -> pd.Series:

        """

        边际波动率贡献 (∂σ_p / ∂w_i)

        """

        cov_matrix = returns.cov()

        portfolio_variance = weights.T @ cov_matrix @ weights

        portfolio_vol = np.sqrt(portfolio_variance)

        

        marginal_vol = (cov_matrix @ weights) / portfolio_vol

        

        return pd.Series(marginal_vol, index=returns.columns, name='Marginal_Vol')

    

    @staticmethod

    def component_volatility(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray) -> pd.Series:

        """

        成分波动率 (w_i * ∂σ_p / ∂w_i)

        """

        marginal_vol = PortfolioRisk.marginal_volatility(returns, weights)

        component_vol = weights * marginal_vol.values

        

        return pd.Series(component_vol, index=returns.columns, name='Component_Vol')

    

    @staticmethod

    def correlation_matrix(returns: pd.DataFrame, method: str = 'pearson') -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        资产相关性矩阵

        

        Args:

            method: 'pearson', 'spearman', 'kendall'

        """

        return returns.corr(method=method)

    

    @staticmethod

    def rolling_correlation(returns1: pd.Series, returns2: pd.Series,

                           window: int = 60) -> pd.Series:

        """滚动相关系数"""

        return returns1.rolling(window).corr(returns2)

    

    @staticmethod

    def beta(asset_returns: pd.Series, market_returns: pd.Series) -> float:

        """

        Beta = Cov(R_a, R_m) / Var(R_m)

        """

        covariance = asset_returns.cov(market_returns)

        market_variance = market_returns.var()

        

        return covariance / market_variance

    

    @staticmethod

    def portfolio_beta(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,

                      market_returns: pd.Series) -> float:

        """投资组合 Beta"""

        portfolio_returns = (returns * weights).sum(axis=1)

        return PortfolioRisk.beta(portfolio_returns, market_returns)

    

    @staticmethod

    def tracking_error(portfolio_returns: pd.Series, benchmark_returns: pd.Series,

                      annualize: bool = True, periods_per_year: int = 252) -> float:

        """

        追踪误差（相对基准的波动率）

        

        TE = σ(R_p - R_b)

        """

        active_returns = portfolio_returns - benchmark_returns

        te = active_returns.std()

        

        if annualize:

            te *= np.sqrt(periods_per_year)

        

        return te

    

    @staticmethod

    def information_ratio(portfolio_returns: pd.Series, benchmark_returns: pd.Series,

                         periods_per_year: int = 252) -> float:

        """

        信息比率 = 超额收益 / 追踪误差

        

        IR = E(R_p - R_b) / σ(R_p - R_b)

        """

        active_returns = portfolio_returns - benchmark_returns

        excess_return = active_returns.mean() * periods_per_year

        te = PortfolioRisk.tracking_error(portfolio_returns, benchmark_returns, 

                                         annualize=True, periods_per_year=periods_per_year)

        

        if te == 0:

            return np.inf if excess_return > 0 else -np.inf

        

        return excess_return / te

    

    @staticmethod

    def sharpe_ratio(returns: pd.Series, risk_free_rate: float = 0.0,

                    periods_per_year: int = 252) -> float:

        """

        Sharpe 比率 = (收益率 - 无风险利率) / 波动率

        """

        excess_returns = returns - risk_free_rate / periods_per_year

        sharpe = excess_returns.mean() / excess_returns.std() * np.sqrt(periods_per_year)

        

        return sharpe

    

    @staticmethod

    def sortino_ratio(returns: pd.Series, risk_free_rate: float = 0.0,

                     target_return: float = 0.0,

                     periods_per_year: int = 252) -> float:

        """

        Sortino 比率（只考虑下行波动率）

        

        Sortino = (收益率 - 目标收益) / 下行标准差

        """

        excess_returns = returns - risk_free_rate / periods_per_year

        downside_returns = excess_returns[excess_returns < target_return]

        downside_std = downside_returns.std()

        

        if downside_std == 0:

            return np.inf if excess_returns.mean() > 0 else -np.inf

        

        sortino = excess_returns.mean() / downside_std * np.sqrt(periods_per_year)

        

        return sortino

    

    @staticmethod

    def maximum_loss(returns: pd.Series, confidence_level: float = 0.95) -> float:

        """

        最大损失（历史分位数）

        """

        return -np.percentile(returns, (1 - confidence_level) * 100)

    

    @staticmethod

    def tail_ratio(returns: pd.Series, percentile: float = 0.95) -> float:

        """

        尾部比率 = 右尾 / 左尾

        

        衡量正收益尾部相对于负收益尾部的大小

        """

        right_tail = np.percentile(returns, percentile * 100)

        left_tail = abs(np.percentile(returns, (1 - percentile) * 100))

        

        if left_tail == 0:

            return np.inf

        

        return right_tail / left_tail

    

    @staticmethod

    def omega_ratio(returns: pd.Series, threshold: float = 0.0) -> float:

        """

        Omega 比率 = 高于阈值的收益期望 / 低于阈值的损失期望

        """

        gains = returns[returns > threshold] - threshold

        losses = threshold - returns[returns < threshold]

        

        if losses.sum() == 0:

            return np.inf

        

        return gains.sum() / losses.sum()





class RiskDecomposition:

    """风险分解"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def factor_risk_attribution(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,

                                factor_exposures: pd.DataFrame,

                                factor_covariance: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:

        """

        因子风险归因

        

        σ_p^2 = β^T Σ_f β + σ_ε^2

        

        Args:

            returns: 资产收益率

            weights: 投资组合权重

            factor_exposures: 因子暴露矩阵 (n_assets, n_factors)

            factor_covariance: 因子协方差矩阵 (n_factors, n_factors)

        """

        # 组合因子暴露

        portfolio_factor_exposure = weights @ factor_exposures.values

        

        # 因子风险

        factor_risk = np.sqrt(

            portfolio_factor_exposure.T @ factor_covariance.values @ portfolio_factor_exposure

        )

        

        # 特异性风险

        residual_returns = returns - (factor_exposures @ factor_covariance).sum(axis=1)

        specific_risk = np.sqrt((weights ** 2 * residual_returns.var()).sum())

        

        # 总风险

        total_risk = PortfolioRisk.portfolio_volatility(returns, weights, annualize=False)

        

        return {

            'total_risk': total_risk,

            'factor_risk': factor_risk,

            'specific_risk': specific_risk,

            'factor_contribution_pct': (factor_risk / total_risk) * 100,

            'specific_contribution_pct': (specific_risk / total_risk) * 100

        }

    

    @staticmethod

    def sector_risk_attribution(returns: pd.DataFrame, weights: np.ndarray,

                                sector_mapping: dict) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        行业风险归因

        

        Args:

            returns: 资产收益率

            weights: 投资组合权重

            sector_mapping: {asset_name: sector_name}

        """

        results = []

        

        for sector in set(sector_mapping.values()):

            # 该行业的资产

            sector_assets = [asset for asset, s in sector_mapping.items() if s == sector]

            sector_idx = [returns.columns.get_loc(asset) for asset in sector_assets]

            

            # 行业权重和收益

            sector_weights = weights[sector_idx]

            sector_returns = returns[sector_assets]

            

            # 行业风险贡献

            sector_vol = PortfolioRisk.portfolio_volatility(

                sector_returns, sector_weights / sector_weights.sum(), annualize=False

            )

            

            results.append({

                'sector': sector,

                'weight': sector_weights.sum(),

                'volatility': sector_vol,

                'contribution': sector_weights.sum() * sector_vol

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(results)





class LiquidityRisk:

    """流动性风险"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def bid_ask_spread(bid: pd.Series, ask: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """买卖价差"""

        return (ask - bid) / ((ask + bid) / 2)

    

    @staticmethod

    def amihud_illiquidity(returns: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series) -> float:

        """

        Amihud 非流动性指标

        

        ILLIQ = (1/N) * Σ |R_t| / Volume_t

        """

        illiquidity = (returns.abs() / volume).mean()

        return illiquidity

    

    @staticmethod

    def turnover_ratio(volume: pd.Series, shares_outstanding: float,

                      window: int = 20) -> pd.Series:

        """

        换手率 = 成交量 / 流通股本

        """

        return (volume / shares_outstanding).rolling(window).mean()

    

    @staticmethod

    def liquidity_adjusted_var(returns: pd.Series, volume: pd.Series,

                              confidence_level: float = 0.95,

                              lambda_liquidity: float = 0.1) -> float:

        """

        流动性调整的 VaR

        

        VaR_adj = VaR * (1 + λ * ILLIQ)

        """

        from .var import VaRCalculator

        

        base_var = VaRCalculator.historical_var(returns, confidence_level)

        illiquidity = LiquidityRisk.amihud_illiquidity(returns, volume)

        

        adjusted_var = base_var * (1 + lambda_liquidity * illiquidity)

        

        return adjusted_var
```

------

## 5. 高级回测引擎

### `quant_lib/backtest/engine.py`

```
Python








"""

高级回测引擎

特性：

- 多资产、多策略支持

- 滑点、交易成本、冲击成本模型

- 分钟级/日级数据

- 事件驱动架构

- 详细的性能分析

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Callable

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

from datetime import datetime

from collections import defaultdict

from abc import ABC, abstractmethod



@dataclass

class Trade:

    """交易记录"""

    timestamp: datetime

    symbol: str

    side: str  # 'buy' or 'sell'

    quantity: float

    price: float

    commission: float = 0.0

    slippage: float = 0.0

    

    @property

    def value(self) -> float:

        """交易金额"""

        return self.quantity * self.price





@dataclass

class Position:

    """持仓"""

    symbol: str

    quantity: float = 0.0

    avg_price: float = 0.0

    

    @property

    def market_value(self) -> float:

        """市值"""

        return self.quantity * self.avg_price

    

    def update(self, trade: Trade):

        """更新持仓"""

        if trade.side == 'buy':

            total_cost = self.quantity * self.avg_price + trade.quantity * trade.price

            self.quantity += trade.quantity

            self.avg_price = total_cost / self.quantity if self.quantity > 0 else 0

        else:  # sell

            self.quantity -= trade.quantity

            if self.quantity <= 0:

                self.quantity = 0

                self.avg_price = 0





@dataclass

class Portfolio:

    """投资组合"""

    cash: float

    positions: Dict[str, Position] = field(default_factory=dict)

    trades: List[Trade] = field(default_factory=list)

    

    def get_position(self, symbol: str) -> Position:

        """获取持仓"""

        if symbol not in self.positions:

            self.positions[symbol] = Position(symbol)

        return self.positions[symbol]

    

    def execute_trade(self, trade: Trade):

        """执行交易"""

        # 扣除交易成本

        total_cost = trade.value + trade.commission + trade.slippage

        

        if trade.side == 'buy':

            if total_cost > self.cash:

                raise ValueError(f"Insufficient cash: {self.cash} < {total_cost}")

            self.cash -= total_cost

        else:  # sell

            self.cash += trade.value - trade.commission - trade.slippage

        

        # 更新持仓

        position = self.get_position(trade.symbol)

        position.update(trade)

        

        # 记录交易

        self.trades.append(trade)

    

    def market_value(self, prices: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

        """组合市值"""

        total = self.cash

        for symbol, position in self.positions.items():

            if symbol in prices:

                total += position.quantity * prices[symbol]

        return total

    

    def equity_curve(self, prices: Dict[datetime, Dict[str, float]]) -> pd.Series:

        """权益曲线"""

        equity = []

        timestamps = []

        

        for timestamp, price_dict in prices.items():

            timestamps.append(timestamp)

            equity.append(self.market_value(price_dict))

        

        return pd.Series(equity, index=timestamps)





class CostModel(ABC):

    """交易成本模型基类"""

    

    @abstractmethod

    def calculate_commission(self, trade: Trade) -> float:

        """计算佣金"""

        pass

    

    @abstractmethod

    def calculate_slippage(self, trade: Trade, market_data: dict) -> float:

        """计算滑点"""

        pass





class FixedCostModel(CostModel):

    """固定费率成本模型"""

    

    def __init__(self, commission_rate: float = 0.001, 

                 slippage_bps: float = 5.0):

        """

        Args:

            commission_rate: 佣金费率（如 0.001 = 0.1%）

            slippage_bps: 滑点（基点，1 bps = 0.01%）

        """

        self.commission_rate = commission_rate

        self.slippage_bps = slippage_bps

    

    def calculate_commission(self, trade: Trade) -> float:

        return trade.value * self.commission_rate

    

    def calculate_slippage(self, trade: Trade, market_data: dict) -> float:

        return trade.value * (self.slippage_bps / 10000)





class MarketImpactModel(CostModel):

    """市场冲击成本模型（根据成交量）"""

    

    def __init__(self, commission_rate: float = 0.001,

                 impact_coefficient: float = 0.1):

        """

        Args:

            impact_coefficient: 冲击系数

        """

        self.commission_rate = commission_rate

        self.impact_coefficient = impact_coefficient

    

    def calculate_commission(self, trade: Trade) -> float:

        return trade.value * self.commission_rate

    

    def calculate_slippage(self, trade: Trade, market_data: dict) -> float:

        """

        冲击成本 ∝ √(交易量 / 日均成交量)

        """

        avg_volume = market_data.get('avg_volume', 1e6)

        impact = self.impact_coefficient * np.sqrt(trade.quantity / avg_volume)

        return trade.value * impact





class Strategy(ABC):

    """策略基类"""

    

    def __init__(self, name: str):

        self.name = name

    

    @abstractmethod

    def generate_signals(self, data: pd.DataFrame, 

                        portfolio: Portfolio) -> Dict[str, float]:

        """

        生成交易信号

        

        Args:

            data: 市场数据

            portfolio: 当前组合

        

        Returns:

            {symbol: target_weight} 目标权重字典

        """

        pass

    

    def on_bar(self, timestamp: datetime, data: dict):

        """Bar 数据回调（可选）"""

        pass

    

    def on_trade(self, trade: Trade):

        """交易执行回调（可选）"""

        pass





class BacktestEngine:

    """回测引擎"""

    

    def __init__(self, initial_capital: float = 1000000,

                 cost_model: Optional[CostModel] = None,

                 benchmark: Optional[pd.Series] = None):

        """

        Args:

            initial_capital: 初始资金

            cost_model: 交易成本模型

            benchmark: 基准收益序列

        """

        self.initial_capital = initial_capital

        self.cost_model = cost_model or FixedCostModel()

        self.benchmark = benchmark

        

        self.portfolio = Portfolio(cash=initial_capital)

        self.performance_history = []

        

    def run(self, strategy: Strategy, data: pd.DataFrame,

            rebalance_freq: str = 'D') -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        运行回测

        

        Args:

            strategy: 交易策略

            data: 市场数据（MultiIndex: (timestamp, symbol)）

            rebalance_freq: 再平衡频率 ('D', 'W', 'M')

        

        Returns:

            回测结果 DataFrame

        """

        # 按时间戳分组

        timestamps = data.index.get_level_values(0).unique()

        

        # 再平衡时间点

        if rebalance_freq == 'D':

            rebalance_dates = timestamps

        elif rebalance_freq == 'W':

            rebalance_dates = pd.DatetimeIndex(timestamps).to_period('W').to_timestamp().unique()

        elif rebalance_freq == 'M':

            rebalance_dates = pd.DatetimeIndex(timestamps).to_period('M').to_timestamp().unique()

        else:

            rebalance_dates = timestamps

        

        for timestamp in timestamps:

            # 当前时刻的数据

            current_data = data.loc[timestamp]

            

            # 再平衡

            if timestamp in rebalance_dates:

                signals = strategy.generate_signals(current_data, self.portfolio)

                self._rebalance(timestamp, signals, current_data)

            

            # 记录组合价值

            prices = current_data['close'].to_dict()

            portfolio_value = self.portfolio.market_value(prices)

            

            self.performance_history.append({

                'timestamp': timestamp,

                'portfolio_value': portfolio_value,

                'cash': self.portfolio.cash,

                'positions_value': portfolio_value - self.portfolio.cash

            })

            

            # 策略回调

            strategy.on_bar(timestamp, current_data.to_dict())

        

        return self._generate_report()

    

    def _rebalance(self, timestamp: datetime, target_weights: Dict[str, float],

                   market_data: pd.DataFrame):

        """执行再平衡"""

        prices = market_data['close'].to_dict()

        portfolio_value = self.portfolio.market_value(prices)

        

        # 目标持仓

        target_positions = {

            symbol: (weight * portfolio_value) / prices[symbol]

            for symbol, weight in target_weights.items()

            if symbol in prices

        }

        

        # 生成交易

        for symbol, target_qty in target_positions.items():

            current_position = self.portfolio.get_position(symbol)

            delta_qty = target_qty - current_position.quantity

            

            if abs(delta_qty) < 1e-6:

                continue

            

            side = 'buy' if delta_qty > 0 else 'sell'

            price = prices[symbol]

            

            # 创建交易

            trade = Trade(

                timestamp=timestamp,

                symbol=symbol,

                side=side,

                quantity=abs(delta_qty),

                price=price

            )

            

            # 计算成本

            market_info = market_data.loc[symbol].to_dict()

            trade.commission = self.cost_model.calculate_commission(trade)

            trade.slippage = self.cost_model.calculate_slippage(trade, market_info)

            

            # 执行

            try:

                self.portfolio.execute_trade(trade)

                strategy.on_trade(trade)

            except ValueError as e:

                print(f"Trade failed: {e}")

    

    def _generate_report(self) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """生成回测报告"""

        df = pd.DataFrame(self.performance_history)

        df.set_index('timestamp', inplace=True)

        

        # 计算收益率

        df['returns'] = df['portfolio_value'].pct_change()

        df['cumulative_returns'] = (1 + df['returns']).cumprod() - 1

        

        # 如果有基准，计算超额收益

        if self.benchmark is not None:

            df = df.join(self.benchmark.rename('benchmark_returns'))

            df['excess_returns'] = df['returns'] - df['benchmark_returns']

        

        return df

    

    def performance_metrics(self) -> dict:

        """计算性能指标"""

        df = pd.DataFrame(self.performance_history)

        returns = df['portfolio_value'].pct_change().dropna()

        

        from ..risk.portfolio_risk import PortfolioRisk, DrawdownAnalysis

        

        metrics = {

            'total_return': (df['portfolio_value'].iloc[-1] / self.initial_capital - 1),

            'annualized_return': (df['portfolio_value'].iloc[-1] / self.initial_capital) ** \

                                (252 / len(df)) - 1,

            'volatility': returns.std() * np.sqrt(252),

            'sharpe_ratio': PortfolioRisk.sharpe_ratio(returns),

            'sortino_ratio': PortfolioRisk.sortino_ratio(returns),

            'max_drawdown': DrawdownAnalysis.max_drawdown((1 + returns).cumprod()),

            'calmar_ratio': DrawdownAnalysis.calmar_ratio(returns),

            'win_rate': (returns > 0).sum() / len(returns),

            'num_trades': len(self.portfolio.trades)

        }

        

        # 如果有基准

        if self.benchmark is not None:

            portfolio_returns = returns

            benchmark_returns = self.benchmark.loc[portfolio_returns.index]

            

            metrics['tracking_error'] = PortfolioRisk.tracking_error(

                portfolio_returns, benchmark_returns

            )

            metrics['information_ratio'] = PortfolioRisk.information_ratio(

                portfolio_returns, benchmark_returns

            )

            metrics['beta'] = PortfolioRisk.beta(portfolio_returns, benchmark_returns)

        

        return metrics





# ---------- 示例策略 ----------

class MomentumStrategy(Strategy):

    """动量策略"""

    

    def __init__(self, lookback: int = 20, top_n: int = 5):

        super().__init__("Momentum")

        self.lookback = lookback

        self.top_n = top_n

    

    def generate_signals(self, data: pd.DataFrame, 

                        portfolio: Portfolio) -> Dict[str, float]:

        """选择动量最强的 top_n 个资产"""

        if 'close' not in data.columns:

            return {}

        

        # 计算收益率（需要历史数据，这里简化）

        returns = data['close'].pct_change(self.lookback)

        

        # 选择 top N

        top_symbols = returns.nlargest(self.top_n).index.tolist()

        

        # 等权重

        weight = 1.0 / self.top_n if self.top_n > 0 else 0

        

        return {symbol: weight for symbol in top_symbols}





class MeanReversionStrategy(Strategy):

    """均值回归策略"""

    

    def __init__(self, lookback: int = 20, threshold: float = 2.0):

        super().__init__("MeanReversion")

        self.lookback = lookback

        self.threshold = threshold

    

    def generate_signals(self, data: pd.DataFrame,

                        portfolio: Portfolio) -> Dict[str, float]:

        """买入超卖资产，卖出超买资产"""

        if 'close' not in data.columns:

            return {}

        

        # Z-score（需要历史数据）

        mean = data['close'].rolling(self.lookback).mean()

        std = data['close'].rolling(self.lookback).std()

        z_score = (data['close'] - mean) / std

        

        signals = {}

        for symbol in data.index:

            z = z_score.loc[symbol]

            if z < -self.threshold:

                signals[symbol] = 0.2  # 超卖，买入

            elif z > self.threshold:

                signals[symbol] = 0.0  # 超买，卖出

        

        # 归一化

        total_weight = sum(signals.values())

        if total_weight > 0:

            signals = {k: v / total_weight for k, v in signals.items()}

        

        return signals
```

## 6. 多因子模型

### `quant_lib/factor/factor_model.py`

```
Python








"""

多因子模型

- Fama-French 三因子/五因子

- 风格因子（价值、动量、质量等）

- 因子测试和回归分析

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import List, Dict, Optional, Tuple

from sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression

from scipy import stats

import statsmodels.api as sm



class FactorLibrary:

    """因子库"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def momentum(prices: pd.DataFrame, lookback: int = 12, 

                skip: int = 1) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        动量因子

        

        Args:

            prices: 价格数据 (时间 x 资产)

            lookback: 回看期（月）

            skip: 跳过最近 N 个月（避免短期反转）

        

        Returns:

            动量得分 DataFrame

        """

        if skip > 0:

            momentum = prices.pct_change(lookback).shift(skip)

        else:

            momentum = prices.pct_change(lookback)

        

        return momentum

    

    @staticmethod

    def value(market_cap: pd.DataFrame, book_value: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        价值因子（Book-to-Market）

        

        Args:

            market_cap: 市值

            book_value: 账面价值

        """

        return book_value / market_cap

    

    @staticmethod

    def size(market_cap: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        规模因子（对数市值）

        """

        return np.log(market_cap)

    

    @staticmethod

    def volatility(returns: pd.DataFrame, window: int = 60) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        波动率因子

        """

        return returns.rolling(window).std() * np.sqrt(252)

    

    @staticmethod

    def quality(roe: pd.DataFrame, debt_to_equity: pd.DataFrame,

               earnings_variability: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        质量因子（综合指标）

        

        Quality = ROE - Debt/Equity - Earnings_Volatility

        """

        quality = roe - debt_to_equity - earnings_variability

        return quality

    

    @staticmethod

    def liquidity(volume: pd.DataFrame, market_cap: pd.DataFrame,

                 window: int = 20) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        流动性因子（成交额占比）

        """

        turnover = volume / market_cap

        avg_turnover = turnover.rolling(window).mean()

        return avg_turnover

    

    @staticmethod

    def low_volatility(returns: pd.DataFrame, window: int = 252) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        低波动因子（负的波动率）

        """

        vol = returns.rolling(window).std() * np.sqrt(252)

        return -vol

    

    @staticmethod

    def dividend_yield(dividends: pd.DataFrame, prices: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        股息率因子

        """

        return dividends / prices

    

    @staticmethod

    def earnings_yield(earnings: pd.DataFrame, market_cap: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        盈利收益率 (E/P)

        """

        return earnings / market_cap

    

    @staticmethod

    def accruals(net_income: pd.DataFrame, cash_flow: pd.DataFrame,

                total_assets: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        应计项目因子（Sloan 1996）

        

        Accruals = (Net_Income - Cash_Flow) / Total_Assets

        负相关：高应计项目 → 未来收益低

        """

        return (net_income - cash_flow) / total_assets

    

    @staticmethod

    def investment(total_assets: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        投资因子（资产增长率）

        

        Investment = ΔTotal_Assets / Total_Assets

        负相关：高投资 → 未来收益低

        """

        return total_assets.pct_change(12)

    

    @staticmethod

    def profitability(operating_profit: pd.DataFrame, 

                     book_equity: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        盈利能力因子 (Operating_Profit / Book_Equity)

        """

        return operating_profit / book_equity





class FamaFrenchModel:

    """Fama-French 因子模型"""

    

    def __init__(self, risk_free_rate: pd.Series):

        self.risk_free_rate = risk_free_rate

        self.model_results = None

    

    def three_factor_regression(self, asset_returns: pd.Series,

                                market_returns: pd.Series,

                                smb: pd.Series, hml: pd.Series) -> dict:

        """

        三因子模型回归

        

        R_i - R_f = α + β_mkt(R_m - R_f) + β_smb SMB + β_hml HML + ε

        

        Args:

            asset_returns: 资产收益率

            market_returns: 市场收益率

            smb: Small Minus Big (规模因子)

            hml: High Minus Low (价值因子)

        

        Returns:

            回归结果字典

        """

        # 超额收益

        excess_returns = asset_returns - self.risk_free_rate

        market_excess = market_returns - self.risk_free_rate

        

        # 构造回归矩阵

        X = pd.DataFrame({

            'Market': market_excess,

            'SMB': smb,

            'HML': hml

        })

        

        # 对齐时间

        X, y = X.align(excess_returns, join='inner')

        

        # 回归

        X_with_const = sm.add_constant(X)

        model = sm.OLS(y, X_with_const).fit()

        

        return {

            'alpha': model.params['const'],

            'beta_market': model.params['Market'],

            'beta_smb': model.params['SMB'],

            'beta_hml': model.params['HML'],

            'r_squared': model.rsquared,

            'alpha_tstat': model.tvalues['const'],

            'alpha_pvalue': model.pvalues['const'],

            'model': model

        }

    

    def five_factor_regression(self, asset_returns: pd.Series,

                              market_returns: pd.Series,

                              smb: pd.Series, hml: pd.Series,

                              rmw: pd.Series, cma: pd.Series) -> dict:

        """

        五因子模型回归

        

        增加：

        - RMW (Robust Minus Weak): 盈利能力因子

        - CMA (Conservative Minus Aggressive): 投资因子

        """

        excess_returns = asset_returns - self.risk_free_rate

        market_excess = market_returns - self.risk_free_rate

        

        X = pd.DataFrame({

            'Market': market_excess,

            'SMB': smb,

            'HML': hml,

            'RMW': rmw,

            'CMA': cma

        })

        

        X, y = X.align(excess_returns, join='inner')

        X_with_const = sm.add_constant(X)

        model = sm.OLS(y, X_with_const).fit()

        

        return {

            'alpha': model.params['const'],

            'beta_market': model.params['Market'],

            'beta_smb': model.params['SMB'],

            'beta_hml': model.params['HML'],

            'beta_rmw': model.params['RMW'],

            'beta_cma': model.params['CMA'],

            'r_squared': model.rsquared,

            'alpha_tstat': model.tvalues['const'],

            'alpha_pvalue': model.pvalues['const'],

            'model': model

        }

    

    @staticmethod

    def construct_smb_hml(returns: pd.DataFrame, market_cap: pd.DataFrame,

                         book_to_market: pd.DataFrame,

                         rebalance_freq: str = 'Y') -> Tuple[pd.Series, pd.Series]:

        """

        构造 SMB 和 HML 因子

        

        方法：

        1. 按市值分为 Small (S) 和 Big (B)

        2. 按 B/M 分为 High (H), Medium (M), Low (L)

        3. 构造 6 个组合：SH, SM, SL, BH, BM, BL

        4. SMB = (SH + SM + SL)/3 - (BH + BM + BL)/3

        5. HML = (SH + BH)/2 - (SL + BL)/2

        """

        # 这里简化实现，实际需要按时间动态重组

        median_cap = market_cap.median(axis=1)

        

        # 分组

        is_small = market_cap.lt(median_cap, axis=0)

        

        # B/M 三分位

        btm_30 = book_to_market.quantile(0.3, axis=1)

        btm_70 = book_to_market.quantile(0.7, axis=1)

        

        is_low = book_to_market.lt(btm_30, axis=0)

        is_high = book_to_market.gt(btm_70, axis=0)

        

        # 6 个组合

        portfolios = {

            'SL': returns[is_small & is_low].mean(axis=1),

            'SM': returns[is_small & ~is_low & ~is_high].mean(axis=1),

            'SH': returns[is_small & is_high].mean(axis=1),

            'BL': returns[~is_small & is_low].mean(axis=1),

            'BM': returns[~is_small & ~is_low & ~is_high].mean(axis=1),

            'BH': returns[~is_small & is_high].mean(axis=1)

        }

        

        # SMB 和 HML

        smb = (portfolios['SL'] + portfolios['SM'] + portfolios['SH']) / 3 - \

              (portfolios['BL'] + portfolios['BM'] + portfolios['BH']) / 3

        

        hml = (portfolios['SH'] + portfolios['BH']) / 2 - \

              (portfolios['SL'] + portfolios['BL']) / 2

        

        return smb, hml





class FactorTester:

    """因子有效性测试"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def information_coefficient(factor_values: pd.DataFrame,

                               forward_returns: pd.DataFrame,

                               method: str = 'spearman') -> pd.Series:

        """

        信息系数 (IC)：因子值与未来收益的相关性

        

        Args:

            factor_values: 因子值 (时间 x 资产)

            forward_returns: 未来收益 (时间 x 资产)

            method: 'pearson' 或 'spearman'

        

        Returns:

            每个时间点的 IC

        """

        ic_series = []

        

        for date in factor_values.index:

            if date in forward_returns.index:

                factor_slice = factor_values.loc[date].dropna()

                returns_slice = forward_returns.loc[date].dropna()

                

                common_assets = factor_slice.index.intersection(returns_slice.index)

                

                if len(common_assets) > 2:

                    if method == 'pearson':

                        ic = factor_slice[common_assets].corr(returns_slice[common_assets])

                    else:

                        ic = factor_slice[common_assets].corr(

                            returns_slice[common_assets], method='spearman'

                        )

                    ic_series.append({'date': date, 'IC': ic})

        

        return pd.DataFrame(ic_series).set_index('date')['IC']

    

    @staticmethod

    def ic_statistics(ic_series: pd.Series) -> dict:

        """IC 统计指标"""

        return {

            'IC_mean': ic_series.mean(),

            'IC_std': ic_series.std(),

            'IC_IR': ic_series.mean() / ic_series.std() if ic_series.std() > 0 else 0,

            'IC_positive_rate': (ic_series > 0).sum() / len(ic_series),

            'IC_tstat': stats.ttest_1samp(ic_series, 0)[0],

            'IC_pvalue': stats.ttest_1samp(ic_series, 0)[1]

        }

    

    @staticmethod

    def quantile_analysis(factor_values: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series,

                         n_quantiles: int = 5) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        分位数分析：按因子值分组，比较各组收益

        

        Returns:

            各分位数组合的统计数据

        """

        # 分组

        quantiles = pd.qcut(factor_values, n_quantiles, labels=False, duplicates='drop')

        

        results = []

        for q in range(n_quantiles):

            group_returns = returns[quantiles == q]

            

            results.append({

                'quantile': q + 1,

                'mean_return': group_returns.mean(),

                'std': group_returns.std(),

                'sharpe': group_returns.mean() / group_returns.std() if group_returns.std() > 0 else 0,

                'count': len(group_returns)

            })

        

        df = pd.DataFrame(results)

        

        # Long-Short 组合

        if len(df) > 0:

            df.loc[len(df)] = {

                'quantile': 'Long-Short',

                'mean_return': df.iloc[-1]['mean_return'] - df.iloc[0]['mean_return'],

                'std': np.nan,

                'sharpe': np.nan,

                'count': np.nan

            }

        

        return df

    

    @staticmethod

    def turnover_analysis(factor_values: pd.DataFrame, 

                         n_quantiles: int = 5) -> pd.Series:

        """

        因子换手率：组合成分变动频率

        """

        quantiles = factor_values.apply(

            lambda x: pd.qcut(x, n_quantiles, labels=False, duplicates='drop'), axis=1

        )

        

        turnover = []

        for i in range(1, len(quantiles)):

            prev = quantiles.iloc[i-1]

            curr = quantiles.iloc[i]

            

            # 重叠度

            overlap = (prev == curr).sum()

            turnover.append(1 - overlap / len(prev))

        

        return pd.Series(turnover, index=quantiles.index[1:], name='Turnover')

    

    @staticmethod

    def factor_return_decomposition(returns: pd.DataFrame, 

                                   factor_exposures: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """

        收益归因：将收益分解到各因子

        

        R_i = Σ β_ik * F_k + ε_i

        """

        # 横截面回归

        factor_returns = []

        

        for date in returns.index:

            y = returns.loc[date].dropna()

            X = factor_exposures.loc[date].reindex(y.index).dropna()

            

            common_assets = y.index.intersection(X.index)

            

            if len(common_assets) > len(factor_exposures.columns):

                model = LinearRegression()

                model.fit(X.loc[common_assets], y.loc[common_assets])

                

                factor_returns.append({

                    'date': date,

                    **dict(zip(factor_exposures.columns, model.coef_))

                })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(factor_returns).set_index('date')





class FactorPortfolio:

    """因子组合构建"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def equal_weight(factor_scores: pd.Series, top_n: int = 20) -> pd.Series:

        """等权重选股"""

        top_stocks = factor_scores.nlargest(top_n)

        weights = pd.Series(1.0 / top_n, index=top_stocks.index)

        return weights

    

    @staticmethod

    def score_weight(factor_scores: pd.Series, top_pct: float = 0.2) -> pd.Series:

        """按因子得分加权"""

        n_select = int(len(factor_scores) * top_pct)

        top_stocks = factor_scores.nlargest(n_select)

        

        # 归一化得分

        normalized = (top_stocks - top_stocks.min()) / (top_stocks.max() - top_stocks.min())

        weights = normalized / normalized.sum()

        

        return weights

    

    @staticmethod

    def long_short(factor_scores: pd.Series, top_pct: float = 0.2,

                  bottom_pct: float = 0.2) -> pd.Series:

        """多空组合"""

        n_long = int(len(factor_scores) * top_pct)

        n_short = int(len(factor_scores) * bottom_pct)

        

        long_stocks = factor_scores.nlargest(n_long)

        short_stocks = factor_scores.nsmallest(n_short)

        

        weights = pd.Series(dtype=float)

        weights[long_stocks.index] = 1.0 / n_long

        weights[short_stocks.index] = -1.0 / n_short

        

        return weights

    

    @staticmethod

    def risk_parity(factor_scores: pd.Series, 

                   covariance_matrix: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """

        风险平价：每个资产贡献相同风险

        

        w_i ∝ 1 / (Σw)_i

        """

        from scipy.optimize import minimize

        

        n = len(factor_scores)

        

        def risk_budget_objective(weights, cov):

            portfolio_vol = np.sqrt(weights @ cov @ weights)

            marginal_contrib = cov @ weights

            contrib = weights * marginal_contrib / portfolio_vol

            

            # 最小化风险贡献的方差

            return np.sum((contrib - contrib.mean())**2)

        

        constraints = [{'type': 'eq', 'fun': lambda w: np.sum(w) - 1}]

        bounds = [(0, 1) for _ in range(n)]

        x0 = np.ones(n) / n

        

        result = minimize(

            risk_budget_objective, x0,

            args=(covariance_matrix.values,),

            method='SLSQP',

            bounds=bounds,

            constraints=constraints

        )

        

        return pd.Series(result.x, index=factor_scores.index)
```

## 7. 机器学习集成

### `quant_lib/ml/feature_engineering.py`

"""

机器学习特征工程

- 技术指标特征

- 因子特征

- 时序特征

- 特征选择

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import List, Optional

from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler, RobustScaler

from sklearn.feature_selection import SelectKBest, f_classif, mutual_info_classif



class TechnicalFeatures:

    """技术指标特征"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def momentum_features(prices: pd.Series, windows: List[int] = [5, 10, 20, 60]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """动量特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index)

        

        for w in windows:

            features[f'returns_{w}d'] = prices.pct_change(w)

            features[f'log_returns_{w}d'] = np.log(prices / prices.shift(w))

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def volatility_features(returns: pd.Series, windows: List[int] = [5, 10, 20, 60]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """波动率特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=returns.index)

        

        for w in windows:

            features[f'vol_{w}d'] = returns.rolling(w).std()

            features[f'vol_ratio_{w}d'] = features[f'vol_{w}d'] / returns.rolling(252).std()

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def price_features(prices: pd.Series, windows: List[int] = [5, 10, 20, 60]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """价格位置特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index)

        

        for w in windows:

            rolling_max = prices.rolling(w).max()

            rolling_min = prices.rolling(w).min()

            

            features[f'price_position_{w}d'] = (prices - rolling_min) / (rolling_max - rolling_min)

            features[f'dist_from_high_{w}d'] = (rolling_max - prices) / rolling_max

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def moving_average_features(prices: pd.Series, 

                               windows: List[int] = [5, 10, 20, 60, 120]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """移动平均特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index)

        

        for w in windows:

            ma = prices.rolling(w).mean()

            features[f'ma_{w}'] = ma

            features[f'price_to_ma_{w}'] = prices / ma - 1

        

        # 均线交叉

        features['ma_cross_5_20'] = (features['ma_5'] > features['ma_20']).astype(int)

        features['ma_cross_10_60'] = (features['ma_10'] > features['ma_60']).astype(int)

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def rsi_features(prices: pd.Series, windows: List[int] = [6, 12, 24]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """RSI 特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index)

        returns = prices.diff()

        

        for w in windows:

            gain = returns.where(returns > 0, 0).rolling(w).mean()

            loss = -returns.where(returns < 0, 0).rolling(w).mean()

            

            rs = gain / loss

            rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))

            

            features[f'rsi_{w}'] = rsi

            features[f'rsi_oversold_{w}'] = (rsi < 30).astype(int)

            features[f'rsi_overbought_{w}'] = (rsi > 70).astype(int)

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def volume_features(volume: pd.Series, prices: pd.Series,

                       windows: List[int] = [5, 10, 20]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """成交量特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=volume.index)

        

        for w in windows:

            features[f'volume_ma_{w}'] = volume.rolling(w).mean()

            features[f'volume_ratio_{w}'] = volume / features[f'volume_ma_{w}']

            features[f'volume_std_{w}'] = volume.rolling(w).std()

        

        # 量价关系

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        features['volume_price_corr'] = volume.rolling(20).corr(returns)

        features['obv'] = (np.sign(returns) * volume).cumsum()  # On-Balance Volume

        

        return features





class TimeSeriesFeatures:

    """时间序列特征"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def lag_features(data: pd.Series, lags: List[int] = [1, 2, 3, 5, 10]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """滞后特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=data.index)

        

        for lag in lags:

            features[f'lag_{lag}'] = data.shift(lag)

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def diff_features(data: pd.Series, periods: List[int] = [1, 5, 10]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """差分特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=data.index)

        

        for p in periods:

            features[f'diff_{p}'] = data.diff(p)

            features[f'pct_change_{p}'] = data.pct_change(p)

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def rolling_stats(data: pd.Series, windows: List[int] = [5, 10, 20]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """滚动统计特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=data.index)

        

        for w in windows:

            features[f'mean_{w}'] = data.rolling(w).mean()

            features[f'std_{w}'] = data.rolling(w).std()

            features[f'min_{w}'] = data.rolling(w).min()

            features[f'max_{w}'] = data.rolling(w).max()

            features[f'median_{w}'] = data.rolling(w).median()

            features[f'skew_{w}'] = data.rolling(w).skew()

            features[f'kurt_{w}'] = data.rolling(w).kurt()

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def expanding_stats(data: pd.Series, min_periods: int = 20) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """累积统计特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=data.index)

        

        features['expanding_mean'] = data.expanding(min_periods).mean()

        features['expanding_std'] = data.expanding(min_periods).std()

        features['expanding_min'] = data.expanding(min_periods).min()

        features['expanding_max'] = data.expanding(min_periods).max()

        

        return features

    

    @staticmethod

    def date_features(dates: pd.DatetimeIndex) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """日期特征"""

        features = pd.DataFrame(index=dates)

        

        features['day_of_week'] = dates.dayofweek

        features['day_of_month'] = dates.day

        features['week_of_year'] = dates.isocalendar().week

        features['month'] = dates.month

        features['quarter'] = dates.quarter

        features['is_month_start'] = dates.is_month_start.astype(int)

        features['is_month_end'] = dates.is_month_end.astype(int)

        features['is_quarter_start'] = dates.is_quarter_start.astype(int)

        features['is_quarter_end'] = dates.is_quarter_end.astype(int)

        

        return features





class FeatureTransformer:

    """特征变换"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def winsorize(data: pd.DataFrame, limits: tuple = (0.01, 0.99)) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """Winsorize（限制极端值）"""

        return data.clip(

            lower=data.quantile(limits[0]),

            upper=data.quantile(limits[1]),

            axis=1

        )

    

    @staticmethod

    def standardize(data: pd.DataFrame, method: str = 'standard') -> pd.DataFrame:

        """标准化"""

        if method == 'standard':

            scaler = StandardScaler()

        elif method == 'robust':

            scaler = RobustScaler()

        else:

            raise ValueError(f"Unknown method: {method}")

        

        scaled = scaler.fit_transform(data)

        return pd.DataFrame(scaled, index=data.index, columns=data.columns)

    

    @staticmethod

    def rank_transform(data: pd.DataFrame, axis: int = 1) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """排名变换（横截面排名）"""

        if axis == 1:

            return data.rank(axis=1, pct=True)

        else:

            return data.rank(axis=0, pct=True)

    

    @staticmethod

    def zscore_neutralize(data: pd.DataFrame, group_by: pd.Series) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """分组中性化"""

        neutralized = data.copy()

        

        for group in group_by.unique():

            mask = group_by == group

            group_data = data[mask]

            

            neutralized[mask] = (group_data - group_data.mean()) / group_data.std()

        

        return neutralized





class FeatureSelector:

    """特征选择"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def correlation_filter(features: pd.DataFrame, threshold: float = 0.95) -> List[str]:

        """

        相关性过滤：移除高度相关的特征

        """

        corr_matrix = features.corr().abs()

        upper = corr_matrix.where(np.triu(np.ones(corr_matrix.shape), k=1).astype(bool))

        

        to_drop = [column for column in upper.columns if any(upper[column] > threshold)]

        

        return [col for col in features.columns if col not in to_drop]

    

    @staticmethod

    def variance_filter(features: pd.DataFrame, threshold: float = 0.01) -> List[str]:

        """方差过滤：移除低方差特征"""

        variances = features.var()

        return variances[variances > threshold].index.tolist()

    

    @staticmethod

    def univariate_selection(features: pd.DataFrame, target: pd.Series,

                            k: int = 20, score_func=f_classif) -> List[str]:

        """单变量特征选择"""

        selector = SelectKBest(score_func=score_func, k=k)

        selector.fit(features, target)

        

        selected_indices = selector.get_support(indices=True)

        return features.columns[selected_indices].tolist()

    

    @staticmethod

    def mutual_information_selection(features: pd.DataFrame, target: pd.Series,

                                    k: int = 20) -> List[str]:

        """互信息特征选择"""

        selector = SelectKBest(score_func=mutual_info_classif, k=k)

        selector.fit(features, target)

        

        selected_indices = selector.get_support(indices=True)

        return features.columns[selected_indices].tolist()

    


```

```
 @staticmethod

    def feature_importance_selection(features: pd.DataFrame, target: pd.Series,

                                    model, k: int = 20) -> List[str]:

        """

        基于模型特征重要性选择

        

        Args:

            features: 特征矩阵

            target: 目标变量

            model: 具有 feature_importances_ 的模型 (如 RandomForest, XGBoost)

            k: 选择特征数量

        """

        model.fit(features, target)

        importances = pd.Series(model.feature_importances_, index=features.columns)

        

        return importances.nlargest(k).index.tolist()

### `quant_lib/ml/models.py`

```
Python








"""

机器学习模型封装

- 分类模型（方向预测）

- 回归模型（收益预测）

- 时间序列交叉验证

- 模型集成

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple

from sklearn.model_selection import TimeSeriesSplit

from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier, RandomForestRegressor

from sklearn.ensemble import GradientBoostingClassifier, GradientBoostingRegressor

from sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression, Ridge, Lasso

from sklearn.metrics import (accuracy_score, precision_score, recall_score, 

                            f1_score, roc_auc_score, mean_squared_error, 

                            mean_absolute_error, r2_score)



class MLPredictor:

    """机器学习预测器基类"""

    

    def __init__(self, model, features: List[str]):

        self.model = model

        self.features = features

        self.is_fitted = False

    

    def fit(self, X: pd.DataFrame, y: pd.Series):

        """训练模型"""

        X_train = X[self.features]

        self.model.fit(X_train, y)

        self.is_fitted = True

    

    def predict(self, X: pd.DataFrame) -> np.ndarray:

        """预测"""

        if not self.is_fitted:

            raise ValueError("Model not fitted yet")

        

        X_pred = X[self.features]

        return self.model.predict(X_pred)

    

    def predict_proba(self, X: pd.DataFrame) -> np.ndarray:

        """预测概率（分类模型）"""

        if not self.is_fitted:

            raise ValueError("Model not fitted yet")

        

        if not hasattr(self.model, 'predict_proba'):

            raise AttributeError("Model does not support predict_proba")

        

        X_pred = X[self.features]

        return self.model.predict_proba(X_pred)





class DirectionClassifier(MLPredictor):

    """方向分类器（预测涨跌）"""

    

    def __init__(self, model_type: str = 'random_forest', **kwargs):

        """

        Args:

            model_type: 'random_forest', 'gradient_boosting', 'logistic'

        """

        if model_type == 'random_forest':

            model = RandomForestClassifier(**kwargs)

        elif model_type == 'gradient_boosting':

            model = GradientBoostingClassifier(**kwargs)

        elif model_type == 'logistic':

            model = LogisticRegression(**kwargs)

        else:

            raise ValueError(f"Unknown model type: {model_type}")

        

        super().__init__(model, [])

    

    def evaluate(self, X: pd.DataFrame, y: pd.Series) -> Dict[str, float]:

        """评估分类性能"""

        y_pred = self.predict(X)

        y_proba = self.predict_proba(X)[:, 1] if hasattr(self.model, 'predict_proba') else None

        

        metrics = {

            'accuracy': accuracy_score(y, y_pred),

            'precision': precision_score(y, y_pred, average='weighted'),

            'recall': recall_score(y, y_pred, average='weighted'),

            'f1': f1_score(y, y_pred, average='weighted')

        }

        

        if y_proba is not None:
			 metrics['auc'] = roc_auc_score(y, y_proba)
        
        return metrics
class ReturnRegressor(MLPredictor):
    """收益率回归器"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_type: str = 'random_forest', **kwargs):
        """
        Args:
            model_type: 'random_forest', 'gradient_boosting', 'ridge', 'lasso'
        """
        if model_type == 'random_forest':
            model = RandomForestRegressor(**kwargs)
        elif model_type == 'gradient_boosting':
            model = GradientBoostingRegressor(**kwargs)
        elif model_type == 'ridge':
            model = Ridge(**kwargs)
        elif model_type == 'lasso':
            model = Lasso(**kwargs)
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unknown model type: {model_type}")
        
        super().__init__(model, [])
    
    def evaluate(self, X: pd.DataFrame, y: pd.Series) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """评估回归性能"""
        y_pred = self.predict(X)
        
        metrics = {
            'mse': mean_squared_error(y, y_pred),
            'rmse': np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(y, y_pred)),
            'mae': mean_absolute_error(y, y_pred),
            'r2': r2_score(y, y_pred)
        }
        
        # 方向准确率
        direction_correct = np.sign(y) == np.sign(y_pred)
        metrics['direction_accuracy'] = direction_correct.sum() / len(y)
        
        return metrics
class TimeSeriesCV:
    """时间序列交叉验证"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def walk_forward_split(data: pd.DataFrame, n_splits: int = 5,
                          train_size: Optional[int] = None) -> List[Tuple]:
        """
        滚动窗口分割
        
        Args:
            data: 时间序列数据
            n_splits: 分割数量
            train_size: 训练集大小（None = 扩展窗口）
        
        Returns:
            [(train_idx, test_idx), ...]
        """
        tscv = TimeSeriesSplit(n_splits=n_splits, max_train_size=train_size)
        splits = []
        
        for train_idx, test_idx in tscv.split(data):
            splits.append((train_idx, test_idx))
        
        return splits
    
    @staticmethod
    def purged_split(data: pd.DataFrame, test_times: pd.DatetimeIndex,
                    embargo_period: int = 5) -> List[Tuple]:
        """
        Purged cross-validation (避免数据泄漏)
        
        Args:
            data: 时间序列数据
            test_times: 测试集时间点
            embargo_period: 禁止期（天数）
        """
        splits = []
        
        for test_time in test_times:
            # 训练集：测试时间之前（排除禁止期）
            train_mask = data.index < (test_time - pd.Timedelta(days=embargo_period))
            
            # 测试集：当前时间点
            test_mask = data.index == test_time
            
            train_idx = np.where(train_mask)[0]
            test_idx = np.where(test_mask)[0]
            
            if len(train_idx) > 0 and len(test_idx) > 0:
                splits.append((train_idx, test_idx))
        
        return splits
    
    @staticmethod
    def evaluate_model(model: MLPredictor, X: pd.DataFrame, y: pd.Series,
                      splits: List[Tuple], metric_func: callable) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """
        交叉验证评估
        
        Returns:
            每折的指标 DataFrame
        """
        results = []
        
        for fold, (train_idx, test_idx) in enumerate(splits):
            X_train, X_test = X.iloc[train_idx], X.iloc[test_idx]
            y_train, y_test = y.iloc[train_idx], y.iloc[test_idx]
            
            model.fit(X_train, y_train)
            
            if hasattr(model, 'evaluate'):
                metrics = model.evaluate(X_test, y_test)
            else:
                y_pred = model.predict(X_test)
                metrics = {'score': metric_func(y_test, y_pred)}
            
            metrics['fold'] = fold
            metrics['train_size'] = len(train_idx)
            metrics['test_size'] = len(test_idx)
            
            results.append(metrics)
        
        return pd.DataFrame(results)
class EnsembleModel:
    """集成模型"""
    
    def __init__(self, models: List[MLPredictor], weights: Optional[List[float]] = None):
        """
        Args:
            models: 模型列表
            weights: 模型权重（None = 等权）
        """
        self.models = models
        self.weights = weights if weights else [1.0 / len(models)] * len(models)
        
        if len(self.weights) != len(self.models):
            raise ValueError("Number of weights must match number of models")
        
        if not np.isclose(sum(self.weights), 1.0):
            raise ValueError("Weights must sum to 1")
    
    def fit(self, X: pd.DataFrame, y: pd.Series):
        """训练所有模型"""
        for model in self.models:
            model.fit(X, y)
    
    def predict(self, X: pd.DataFrame) -> np.ndarray:
        """加权平均预测"""
        predictions = np.array([model.predict(X) for model in self.models])
        weighted_pred = np.average(predictions, axis=0, weights=self.weights)
        
        return weighted_pred
    
    def predict_proba(self, X: pd.DataFrame) -> np.ndarray:
        """加权平均预测概率"""
        probas = np.array([model.predict_proba(X) for model in self.models])
        weighted_proba = np.average(probas, axis=0, weights=self.weights)
        
        return weighted_proba
class FeatureImportanceAnalyzer:
    """特征重要性分析"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def get_importance(model, feature_names: List[str]) -> pd.Series:
        """获取特征重要性"""
        if hasattr(model, 'feature_importances_'):
            importances = model.feature_importances_
        elif hasattr(model, 'coef_'):
            importances = np.abs(model.coef_)
        else:
            raise ValueError("Model does not have feature_importances_ or coef_")
        
        return pd.Series(importances, index=feature_names, name='importance').sort_values(ascending=False)
    
    @staticmethod
    def permutation_importance(model: MLPredictor, X: pd.DataFrame, y: pd.Series,
                             metric_func: callable, n_repeats: int = 10) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """
        Permutation importance（排列重要性）
        
        通过打乱特征值并观察性能下降来衡量重要性
        """
        baseline_score = metric_func(y, model.predict(X))
        
        importances = []
        
        for feature in X.columns:
            scores = []
            
            for _ in range(n_repeats):
                X_permuted = X.copy()
                X_permuted[feature] = np.random.permutation(X_permuted[feature].values)
                
                score = metric_func(y, model.predict(X_permuted))
                scores.append(baseline_score - score)
            
            importances.append({
                'feature': feature,
                'importance_mean': np.mean(scores),
                'importance_std': np.std(scores)
            })
        
        df = pd.DataFrame(importances).sort_values('importance_mean', ascending=False)
        return df
class MLSignalGenerator:
    """机器学习信号生成器"""
    
    def __init__(self, model: MLPredictor, feature_cols: List[str],
                 signal_type: str = 'classification'):
        """
        Args:
            signal_type: 'classification' (方向) 或 'regression' (收益率)
        """
        self.model = model
        self.feature_cols = feature_cols
        self.signal_type = signal_type
    
    def generate_signals(self, features: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:
        """生成交易信号"""
        if self.signal_type == 'classification':
            # 预测方向（1=上涨，0=下跌）
            predictions = self.model.predict(features[self.feature_cols])
            signals = pd.Series(predictions, index=features.index)
            signals = signals.replace({0: -1})  # 转换为 -1/1
        
        elif self.signal_type == 'regression':
            # 预测收益率
            predictions = self.model.predict(features[self.feature_cols])
            signals = pd.Series(predictions, index=features.index)
            
            # 归一化为信号强度
            signals = (signals - signals.mean()) / signals.std()
        
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unknown signal type: {self.signal_type}")
        
        return signals
    
    def backtest_signals(self, signals: pd.Series, returns: pd.Series,
                        transaction_cost: float = 0.001) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """回测信号"""
        # 持仓（基于信号）
        positions = signals.shift(1)  # T日信号 → T+1日持仓
        
        # 策略收益
        strategy_returns = positions * returns
        
        # 扣除交易成本
        position_changes = positions.diff().abs()
        costs = position_changes * transaction_cost
        strategy_returns -= costs
        
        # 累积收益
        cumulative_returns = (1 + strategy_returns).cumprod()
        
        results = pd.DataFrame({
            'signal': signals,
            'position': positions,
            'returns': strategy_returns,
            'cumulative_returns': cumulative_returns
        })
        
        return results
8. 可视化模块
quant_lib/visualization/plot_utils.py
