"""

完整的自我进化量化交易系统

整合所有模块：策略库、自动ML、信号合成、策略进化

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from datetime import datetime, timedelta

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

import seaborn as sns



from quant_lib.strategy.strategy_library import (

    StrategyLibrary, StrategyBacktester, 

    StrategyPortfolioOptimizer, StrategyMonitor

)

from quant_lib.ml.auto_ml import (

    AutoMLPipeline, ModelRegistry, PerformanceMonitor,

    StrategyEvolution

)

from quant_lib.strategy.signal_composer import (

    MultiStrategyPortfolio, ResonanceDetector, AdaptiveSignalWeighting

)



# 设置绘图风格

sns.set_style("whitegrid")

plt.rcParams['font.sans-serif'] = ['Arial Unicode MS', 'SimHei']

plt.rcParams['axes.unicode_minus'] = False





def generate_realistic_market_data(n_days: int = 1000) -> Tuple[pd.DataFrame, pd.DataFrame]:

    """生成更真实的市场数据"""

    dates = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=n_days, freq='D')

    n_assets = 10

    

    # 生成具有不同特征的资产

    prices = pd.DataFrame(index=dates)

    

    for i in range(n_assets):

        # 趋势项

        trend = 0.0003 + np.random.normal(0, 0.0001)

        

        # 波动率

        volatility = 0.015 + np.random.normal(0, 0.005)

        

        # 均值回归强度

        mean_reversion = 0.05 + np.random.uniform(0, 0.1)

        

        # 生成价格

        returns = []

        for t in range(n_days):

            # 随机游走 + 均值回归

            if t == 0:

                ret = np.random.normal(trend, volatility)

            else:

                prev_ret = returns[-1]

                # 均值回归项

                mr_component = -mean_reversion * prev_ret

                # 随机项

                random_component = np.random.normal(trend, volatility)

                ret = mr_component + random_component

            

            returns.append(ret)

        

        price = 100 * np.exp(np.cumsum(returns))

        prices[f'Asset_{i}'] = price

    

    returns = prices.pct_change().dropna()

    

    return prices, returns





def create_advanced_strategies():

    """创建高级策略"""

    

    def dual_momentum_strategy(data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """双动量策略（绝对动量 + 相对动量）"""

        lookback_short = 20

        lookback_long = 60

        

        if len(data) < lookback_long:

            return pd.DataFrame()

        

        signals = []

        latest_date = data.index[-1]

        

        for asset in data.columns:

            # 绝对动量

            abs_momentum = data[asset].iloc[-1] / data[asset].iloc[-lookback_short] - 1

            

            # 相对动量（vs 其他资产）

            all_momentums = {}

            for other_asset in data.columns:

                all_momentums[other_asset] = data[other_asset].iloc[-1] / data[other_asset].iloc[-lookback_long] - 1

            

            relative_rank = sorted(all_momentums.values(), reverse=True).index(all_momentums[asset]) + 1

            relative_score = 1 - (relative_rank / len(data.columns))

            

            # 组合信号

            strength = np.tanh(abs_momentum * 5) * relative_score

            

            signals.append({

                'timestamp': latest_date,

                'asset': asset,

                'strength': strength,

                'source': 'dual_momentum'

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(signals)

    

    def bollinger_mean_reversion(data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """布林带均值回归策略"""

        lookback = 20

        num_std = 2

        

        if len(data) < lookback:

            return pd.DataFrame()

        

        signals = []

        latest_date = data.index[-1]

        

        for asset in data.columns:

            recent = data[asset].iloc[-lookback:]

            mean = recent.mean()

            std = recent.std()

            current = recent.iloc[-1]

            

            # 布林带

            upper_band = mean + num_std * std

            lower_band = mean - num_std * std

            

            # 信号：价格偏离均值的程度

            if current > upper_band:

                strength = -min((current - upper_band) / std, 1)

            elif current < lower_band:

                strength = min((lower_band - current) / std, 1)

            else:

                strength = -(current - mean) / std * 0.5

            

            signals.append({

                'timestamp': latest_date,

                'asset': asset,

                'strength': strength,

                'source': 'bollinger_mr'

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(signals)

    

    def volume_weighted_momentum(data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """成交量加权动量策略"""

        lookback = 30

        

        if len(data) < lookback:

            return pd.DataFrame()

        

        signals = []

        latest_date = data.index[-1]

        

        for asset in data.columns:

            # 模拟成交量（基于波动率）

            returns = data[asset].pct_change().iloc[-lookback:]

            volume_proxy = returns.abs()

            

            # 加权动量

            weighted_returns = returns * volume_proxy

            momentum = weighted_returns.sum()

            

            strength = np.tanh(momentum * 20)

            

            signals.append({

                'timestamp': latest_date,

                'asset': asset,

                'strength': strength,

                'source': 'volume_momentum'

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(signals)

    

    def rsi_contrarian(data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """RSI逆向策略"""

        lookback = 14

        

        if len(data) < lookback + 1:

            return pd.DataFrame()

        

        signals = []

        latest_date = data.index[-1]

        

        for asset in data.columns:

            returns = data[asset].pct_change().iloc[-lookback-1:]

            

            # 计算RSI

            gains = returns.clip(lower=0)

            losses = -returns.clip(upper=0)

            

            avg_gain = gains.mean()

            avg_loss = losses.mean()

            

            if avg_loss > 0:

                rs = avg_gain / avg_loss

                rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))

            else:

                rsi = 100

            

            # 逆向信号

            if rsi > 70:

                strength = -(rsi - 70) / 30

            elif rsi < 30:

                strength = (30 - rsi) / 30

            else:

                strength = 0

            

            signals.append({

                'timestamp': latest_date,

                'asset': asset,

                'strength': strength,

                'source': 'rsi_contrarian'

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(signals)

    

    return {

        'dual_momentum': dual_momentum_strategy,

        'bollinger_mr': bollinger_mean_reversion,

        'volume_momentum': volume_weighted_momentum,

        'rsi_contrarian': rsi_contrarian

    }





def run_complete_system():

    """运行完整系统"""

    print("=" * 100)

    print("完整自我进化量化交易系统")

    print("=" * 100)

    

    # ========== 第1阶段：数据准备 ==========

    print("\n[阶段 1/5] 数据准备")

    print("-" * 100)

    

    prices, returns = generate_realistic_market_data(n_days=1000)

    print(f"✓ 生成 {len(prices)} 天，{len(prices.columns)} 个资产的市场数据")

    print(f"  日期范围: {prices.index[0].date()} 至 {prices.index[-1].date()}")

    

    # 分割数据

    train_size = int(len(prices) * 0.6)

    val_size = int(len(prices) * 0.2)

    

    prices_train = prices.iloc[:train_size]

    prices_val = prices.iloc[train_size:train_size+val_size]

    prices_test = prices.iloc[train_size+val_size:]

    

    returns_train = returns.iloc[:train_size]

    returns_val = returns.iloc[train_size:train_size+val_size]

    returns_test = returns.iloc[train_size+val_size:]

    

    print(f"  训练集: {len(prices_train)} 天")

    print(f"  验证集: {len(prices_val)} 天")

    print(f"  测试集: {len(prices_test)} 天")

    

    # ========== 第2阶段：策略库初始化 ==========

    print("\n[阶段 2/5] 初始化策略库")

    print("-" * 100)

    

    strategy_lib = StrategyLibrary(library_path='./strategy_library_v2')

    

    # 注册策略

    strategies = create_advanced_strategies()

    

    for name, strategy_func in strategies.items():

        strategy_id, version = strategy_lib.register_strategy(

            name=name,

            strategy_func=strategy_func,

            description=f"{name} 策略",

            author="System",

            tags=['momentum', 'mean_reversion', 'technical'],

            parameters={}

        )

        print(f"  ✓ 注册策略: {name} (ID: {strategy_id[:8]}, v{version})")

    

    # ========== 第3阶段：回测与优化 ==========

    print("\n[阶段 3/5] 策略回测与组合优化")

    print("-" * 100)

    

    backtester = StrategyBacktester(strategy_lib)

    

    # 回测所有策略

    all_strategies = strategy_lib.list_strategies()

    strategy_specs = [(row['strategy_id'], row['version']) 

                     for _, row in all_strategies.iterrows()]

    

    print(f"  回测 {len(strategy_specs)} 个策略...")

    backtest_results = backtester.backtest_multiple(

        strategy_specs, 

        prices_train, 

        returns_train

    )

    

    print("\n  策略回测结果:")

    print(backtest_results[['name', 'total_return', 'sharpe_ratio', 'max_drawdown', 'win_rate']].to_string(index=False))

    

    # 组合优化

    print("\n  优化策略组合权重...")

    optimizer = StrategyPortfolioOptimizer(strategy_lib)

    

    optimal_weights = optimizer.optimize_weights(

        strategy_specs,

        prices_train,

        returns_train,

        method='sharpe'

    )

    

    print("\n  优化后的权重分配:")

    for strategy_key, weight in sorted(optimal_weights.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):

        strategy_id = strategy_key.split('_')[0]

        metadata = [m for m in strategy_lib.strategies.values() if m.strategy_id == strategy_id][0]

        print(f"    {metadata.name}: {weight:.2%}")

    

    # ========== 第4阶段：策略进化 ==========

    print("\n[阶段 4/5] 策略进化")

    print("-" * 100)

    

    # 使用验证集进行进化

    evolution = StrategyEvolution(strategies)

    

    n_generations = 5

    window_size = len(prices_val) // n_generations

    

    for gen in range(n_generations):

        start_idx = gen * window_size

        end_idx = min(start_idx + window_size, len(prices_val))

        

        data_window = prices_val.iloc[start_idx:end_idx]

        returns_window = returns_val.iloc[start_idx:end_idx]

        

        fitness_scores = evolution.evaluate_generation(data_window, returns_window)

        

        print(f"\n  第 {gen + 1} 代进化:")

        for strategy, score in sorted(fitness_scores.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:3]:

            print(f"    {strategy}: Fitness = {score:.4f}")

        

        if gen < n_generations - 1:

            evolution.evolve(fitness_scores, survival_rate=0.6, mutation_rate=0.15)

    

    # 获取最优策略

    best_evolved = evolution.get_best_strategies(top_n=5)

    print("\n  进化后的最佳策略:")

    for rank, (strategy, fitness) in enumerate(best_evolved, 1):

        print(f"    {rank}. {strategy}: {fitness:.4f}")

    

    # ========== 第5阶段：实时监控与测试 ==========

    print("\n[阶段 5/5] 测试集验证与监控")

    print("-" * 100)

    

    # 构建最终组合

    final_strategies = {name: func for name, func in evolution.strategy_pool.items() 

                       if name in [s[0] for s in best_evolved[:3]]}

    

    portfolio = MultiStrategyPortfolio(final_strategies)

    monitor = StrategyMonitor(strategy_lib)

    

    # 在测试集上运行

    print(f"  在测试集({len(prices_test)}天)上运行组合...")

    

    # 滚动窗口测试

    window = 30

    test_results = []

    

    for i in range(0, len(prices_test) - window, window // 2):

        test_window = prices_test.iloc[i:i+window]

        returns_window = returns_test.iloc[i:i+window]

        

        # 生成信号

        signals = portfolio.generate_portfolio_signals(

            test_window,

            use_resonance=True,

            resonance_threshold=2

        )

        

        # 计算收益

        if not signals.empty:

            window_returns = []

            for _, signal in signals.iterrows():

                timestamp = signal['timestamp']

                asset = signal['asset']

                strength = signal['strength']

                

                if timestamp in returns_window.index and asset in returns_window.columns:

                    ret = returns_window.loc[timestamp, asset]

                    window_returns.append(strength * ret)

            

            if window_returns:

                test_results.append({

                    'window_start': test_window.index[0],

                    'window_end': test_window.index[-1],

                    'mean_return': np.mean(window_returns),

                    'sharpe': np.mean(window_returns) / np.std(window_returns) * np.sqrt(252) if np.std(window_returns) > 0 else 0,

                    'num_signals': len(signals)

                })

    

    test_results_df = pd.DataFrame(test_results)

    

    print("\n  测试集表现:")

    print(f"    平均收益: {test_results_df['mean_return'].mean():.4%}")

    print(f"    平均Sharpe: {test_results_df['sharpe'].mean():.2f}")

    print(f"    总信号数: {test_results_df['num_signals'].sum()}")

    

    # ========== 可视化 ==========

    print("\n[生成可视化报告]")

    print("-" * 100)

    

    fig = plt.figure(figsize=(20, 12))

    gs = fig.add_gridspec(3, 3, hspace=0.3, wspace=0.3)

    

    # 1. 策略回测表现对比

    ax1 = fig.add_subplot(gs[0, :2])

    backtest_sorted = backtest_results.sort_values('sharpe_ratio', ascending=False)

    bars = ax1.barh(range(len(backtest_sorted)), backtest_sorted['sharpe_ratio'])

    ax1.set_yticks(range(len(backtest_sorted)))

    ax1.set_yticklabels(backtest_sorted['name'])

    ax1.set_xlabel('Sharpe Ratio')

    ax1.set_title('策略回测表现 (训练集)', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')

    ax1.axvline(x=0, color='black', linestyle='-', linewidth=0.5)

    ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3, axis='x')

    

    # 颜色编码

    for i, bar in enumerate(bars):

        if backtest_sorted.iloc[i]['sharpe_ratio'] > 1:

            bar.set_color('green')

        elif backtest_sorted.iloc[i]['sharpe_ratio'] > 0:

            bar.set_color('lightgreen')

        else:

            bar.set_color('red')

    

    # 2. 最优权重分配

    ax2 = fig.add_subplot(gs[0, 2])

    weights_df = pd.DataFrame(list(optimal_weights.items()), columns=['strategy', 'weight'])

    weights_df['name'] = weights_df['strategy'].apply(lambda x: 

        [m.name for m in strategy_lib.strategies.values() if m.strategy_id == x.split('_')[0]][0]

    )

    ax2.pie(weights_df['weight'], labels=weights_df['name'], autopct='%1.1f%%', startangle=90)

    ax2.set_title('优化权重分配', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')

    

    # 3. 策略进化历史

    ax3 = fig.add_subplot(gs[1, :2])

    evolution_history = evolution.get_evolution_history()

    for strategy in best_evolved[:3]:

        strategy_name = strategy[0]

        strategy_data = evolution_history[evolution_history['strategy'] == strategy_name]

        if not strategy_data.empty:

            ax3.plot(strategy_data['generation'], strategy_data['fitness'], 

                    marker='o', linewidth=2, label=strategy_name)

    ax3.set_xlabel('代数')

    ax3.set_ylabel('适应度')

    ax3.set_title('策略适应度进化', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')

    ax3.legend()

    ax3.grid(True, alpha=0.3)

    

    # 4. 测试集滚动Sharpe

    ax4 = fig.add_subplot(gs[1, 2])

    ax4.plot(range(len(test_results_df)), test_results_df['sharpe'], 

            marker='o', linestyle='-', color='blue')

    ax4.axhline(y=0, color='red', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)

    ax4.axhline(y=test_results_df['sharpe'].mean(), color='green', 

                linestyle='--', alpha=0.5, label=f'平均: {test_results_df["sharpe"].mean():.2f}')

    ax4.set_xlabel('测试窗口')

    ax4.set_ylabel('Sharpe Ratio')

    ax4.set_title('测试集滚动Sharpe', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')

    ax4.legend()

    ax4.grid(True, alpha=0.3)

    

    # 5. 累积收益对比

    ax5 = fig.add_subplot(gs[2, :])

    

    # 买入持有基准

    buy_hold_cumret = (prices_test.mean(axis=1) / prices_test.mean(axis=1).iloc[0] - 1) * 100

    ax5.plot(prices_test.index, buy_hold_cumret, label='买入持有 (等权)', 

            linestyle='--', color='gray', linewidth=2)

    

    # 策略组合累积收益

    if not test_results_df.empty:

        strategy_cumret = test_results_df['mean_return'].cumsum() * 100

        # 对齐日期

        dates = [test_results_df.iloc[i]['window_end'] for i in range(len(test_results_df))]

        ax5.plot(dates, strategy_cumret, label='进化策略组合', 

                color='blue', linewidth=2)

    

    ax5.set_xlabel('日期')

    ax5.set_ylabel('累积收益 (%)')

    ax5.set_title('策略组合 vs 基准', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')

    ax5.legend()

    ax5.grid(True, alpha=0.3)

    

    plt.savefig('complete_evolution_system.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')

    print("  ✓ 已保存: complete_evolution_system.png")

    

    # ========== 保存结果 ==========

    print("\n[保存分析结果]")

    print("-" * 100)

    

    # 保存策略列表

    strategy_lib.list_strategies().to_csv('final_strategy_library.csv', index=False)

    print("  ✓ 已保存: final_strategy_library.csv")

    

    # 保存回测结果
```

    # 保存进化历史

    evolution_history.to_csv('evolution_history.csv', index=False)

    print("  ✓ 已保存: evolution_history.csv")

    

    # 保存测试结果

    test_results_df.to_csv('test_results.csv', index=False)

    # ========== 最终报告 ==========

    print("\n" + "=" * 100)

    print("\n📊 训练阶段 (回测):")

    print(f"  • 策略总数: {len(backtest_results)}")

    print(f"  • 最佳Sharpe: {backtest_results['sharpe_ratio'].max():.2f} ({backtest_results.loc[backtest_results['sharpe_ratio'].idxmax(), 'name']})")

    print(f"  • 平均Sharpe: {backtest_results['sharpe_ratio'].mean():.2f}")

    print(f"  • 最大回撤: {backtest_results['max_drawdown'].min():.2%}")

    

    print("\n🧬 进化阶段:")

    print(f"  • 进化代数: {n_generations}")

    print(f"  • 存活策略: {len(best_evolved)}")

    print(f"  • 最佳适应度: {best_evolved[0][1]:.4f}")

    

    print("\n✅ 测试阶段:")

    print(f"  • 测试窗口数: {len(test_results_df)}")

    print(f"  • 平均收益: {test_results_df['mean_return'].mean():.4%}")

    print(f"  • 平均Sharpe: {test_results_df['sharpe'].mean():.2f}")

    print(f"  • 胜率: {(test_results_df['mean_return'] > 0).mean():.1%}")

    

    # 与基准对比

    bh_final_ret = (prices_test.mean(axis=1).iloc[-1] / prices_test.mean(axis=1).iloc[0] - 1)

    strategy_final_ret = test_results_df['mean_return'].sum()

    

    print(f"\n📈 相对基准表现:")

    print(f"  • 买入持有收益: {bh_final_ret:.2%}")

    print(f"  • 策略组合收益: {strategy_final_ret:.2%}")

    print(f"  • 超额收益: {strategy_final_ret - bh_final_ret:.2%}")

    

    print("\n" + "=" * 100)

    print("🎉 自我进化量化交易系统演示完成！")

    print("=" * 100)

    

    return {

        'strategy_lib': strategy_lib,

        'backtest_results': backtest_results,

        'optimal_weights': optimal_weights,

        'evolution': evolution,

        'test_results': test_results_df

    }

from quant_lib.strategy.strategy_library import StrategyLibrary, StrategyBacktester

from quant_lib.ml.auto_ml import AutoMLPipeline, ModelRegistry, PerformanceMonitor



# 1. 初始化系统

strategy_lib = StrategyLibrary('./my_strategies')

model_registry = ModelRegistry('./my_models')

performance_monitor = PerformanceMonitor()



# 2. 注册策略

def my_momentum_strategy(data):

    # 你的策略逻辑

    signals = []

    # ... 生成信号

    return pd.DataFrame(signals)



strategy_lib.register_strategy(

    name='momentum_v1',

    strategy_func=my_momentum_strategy,

    description='简单动量策略',

    tags=['momentum', 'trend_following']

)



# 3. 回测

backtester = StrategyBacktester(strategy_lib)

results = backtester.backtest_strategy(

    strategy_id='your_strategy_id',

    version='1.0.0',

    prices=price_data,

    returns=return_data

)



print(results['metrics'])
```

## 核心模块

### 1. 策略库管理 (`StrategyLibrary`)

**功能:**

- 策略版本控制
- 策略元数据管理
- 策略搜索与过滤
- 策略性能追踪

**关键方法:**

```
Python








# 注册策略

strategy_id, version = lib.register_strategy(

    name='my_strategy',

    strategy_func=strategy_function,

    description='策略描述',

    parameters={'param1': value1},

    tags=['tag1', 'tag2']

)



# 获取策略

strategy_func, metadata = lib.get_strategy(strategy_id, version)



# 搜索策略

results = lib.search_strategies('momentum')



# 比较策略

comparison = lib.compare_strategies(

    [(id1, v1), (id2, v2)],

    metric='sharpe_ratio'

)
```

### 2. 自动化回测 (`StrategyBacktester`)

**功能:**

- 单策略回测
- 多策略并行回测
- 性能指标计算
- 风险分析

**回测指标:**

- 总收益率
- 年化收益率
- 波动率
- Sharpe比率
- 最大回撤
- 胜率

**示例:**

```
Python








backtester = StrategyBacktester(strategy_lib)



# 回测单个策略

result = backtester.backtest_strategy(

    strategy_id='abc123',

    version='1.0.0',

    prices=prices,

    returns=returns,

    initial_capital=1000000

)



# 回测多个策略

results = backtester.backtest_multiple(

    [('id1', 'v1'), ('id2', 'v2')],

    prices=prices,

    returns=returns

)
```

### 3. 组合优化 (`StrategyPortfolioOptimizer`)

**优化方法:**

- `sharpe`: 最大化Sharpe比率
- `min_variance`: 最小方差
- `risk_parity`: 风险平价

**示例:**

```
Python








optimizer = StrategyPortfolioOptimizer(strategy_lib)



optimal_weights = optimizer.optimize_weights(

    strategy_specs=[('id1', 'v1'), ('id2', 'v2')],

    prices=prices,

    returns=returns,

    method='sharpe'

)



# {'id1_v1': 0.6, 'id2_v2': 0.4}
```

### 4. 策略进化 (`StrategyEvolution`)

**进化机制:**

- **选择**: 保留适应度高的策略
- **变异**: 随机调整策略参数
- **交叉**: 组合两个策略的特征
- **淘汰**: 移除表现差的策略

**示例:**

```
Python








evolution = StrategyEvolution(strategy_pool)



# 评估当代

fitness_scores = evolution.evaluate_generation(data, returns)



# 进化下一代

evolution.evolve(

    fitness_scores,

    survival_rate=0.7,

    mutation_rate=0.1

)



# 获取最佳策略

best_strategies = evolution.get_best_strategies(top_n=5)
```

### 5. 机器学习管道 (`AutoMLPipeline`)

**功能:**

- 自动超参数优化
- 在线学习
- 模型版本管理
- 性能退化检测

**示例:**

```
Python








auto_ml = AutoMLPipeline(model_registry, performance_monitor)



# 初始化

auto_ml.initialize(

    X_train, y_train,

    model_class=RandomForestClassifier,

    param_grid={'n_estimators': [50, 100], 'max_depth': [3, 5]}

)



# 在线预测与学习

predictions = auto_ml.predict_and_update(X_new, y_new, current_date)



# 获取状态

status = auto_ml.get_status()
```

### 6. 信号合成 (`SignalComposer`)

**聚合方法:**

- `weighted_average`: 加权平均
- `max_strength`: 最强信号
- `consensus`: 一致性信号
- `adaptive`: 自适应权重

**示例:**

```
Python








composer = SignalComposer(aggregation_method='weighted_average')



# 添加信号源

composer.add_signal_source('momentum', momentum_strategy, weight=1.0)

composer.add_signal_source('mean_reversion', mr_strategy, weight=0.8)



# 生成综合信号

signals = composer.compose_signals(data)
```

### 7. 共振检测 (`ResonanceDetector`)

**功能:**

- 检测多策略同向信号
- 计算共振强度
- 识别高置信度机会

**示例:**

```
Python








# 检测共振

resonance = ResonanceDetector.detect_resonance(

    strategy_signals={'strat1': signals1, 'strat2': signals2},

    min_sources=2,

    time_window=3

)



# 计算共振强度

resonance['strength'] = ResonanceDetector.resonance_strength(resonance)



# 过滤强共振事件

strong_resonance = resonance[resonance['strength'] > 0.8]
```

## 策略开发

### 策略函数规范

策略函数必须遵循以下签名:

```
Python








def strategy_function(data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

    """

    Args:

        data: 价格数据，DataFrame with DatetimeIndex and asset columns

    

    Returns:

        信号DataFrame with columns:

        - timestamp: 信号时间

        - asset: 资产名称

        - strength: 信号强度 [-1, 1]

        - source: 信号来源（策略名）

    """

    signals = []

    

    # 策略逻辑

    for asset in data.columns:

        # 计算信号

        signal_strength = ...  # 范围 [-1, 1]

        

        signals.append({

            'timestamp': data.index[-1],

            'asset': asset,

            'strength': signal_strength,

            'source': 'my_strategy'

        })

    

    return pd.DataFrame(signals)
```

### 策略开发最佳实践

1. **信号归一化**: 将信号强度归一化到 [-1, 1]
2. **数据验证**: 检查数据长度和有效性
3. **异常处理**: 处理缺失数据和边界情况
4. **参数化**: 使参数可配置
5. **文档化**: 清晰描述策略逻辑

### 策略示例库

#### 1. 动量策略

```
Python








def momentum_strategy(data: pd.DataFrame, lookback: int = 20) -> pd.DataFrame:

    """动量策略"""

    if len(data) < lookback:

        return pd.DataFrame()

    

    signals = []

    latest_date = data.index[-1]

    

    for asset in data.columns:

        momentum = data[asset].iloc[-1] / data[asset].iloc[-lookback] - 1

        strength = np.tanh(momentum * 10)

        

        signals.append({

            'timestamp': latest_date,

            'asset': asset,

            'strength': strength,

            'source': f'momentum_{lookback}d'

        })

    

    return pd.DataFrame(signals)
```

#### 2. 均值回归策略

```
Python








def mean_reversion_strategy(data: pd.DataFrame, lookback: int = 20, 

                           threshold: float = 2.0) -> pd.DataFrame:

    """均值回归策略"""

    if len(data) < lookback:

        return pd.DataFrame()

    

    signals = []

    latest_date = data.index[-1]

    

    for asset in data.columns:

        recent = data[asset].iloc[-lookback:]

        z_score = (recent.iloc[-1] - recent.mean()) / recent.std()

        strength = -np.tanh(z_score / threshold)

        

        signals.append({

            'timestamp': latest_date,

            'asset': asset,

            'strength': strength,

            'source': f'mean_reversion_{lookback}d'

        })

    

    return pd.DataFrame(signals)
```

# 策略库配置

strategy_library:

  path: ./strategy_library

  auto_backup: true

  max_versions: 10

  path: ./model_registry

  auto_cleanup: true

  retention_days: 90



# 性能监控配置

  window_size: 30

  alert_threshold: 0.2

  metrics:

    - sharpe_ratio

    - max_drawdown

    - win_rate



# 进化系统配置

evolution:

  n_generations: 10

  survival_rate: 0.6

  mutation_rate: 0.1

  crossover_rate: 0.3



# 回测配置

backtest:

  initial_capital: 1000000

  commission: 0.001

  slippage: 0.0005



# 组合优化配置

portfolio:

  optimization_method: sharpe

  max_weight: 0.4

  min_weight: 0.05

  rebalance_frequency: 20  # days
```

### 1. 数据管理

- 使用一致的数据格式
- 定期清理和验证数据
- 实施数据版本控制

### 2. 策略开发

- 从简单策略开始
- 进行充分的回测
- 避免过拟合
- 使用样本外测试

### 3. 风险管理

- 设置止损和止盈
- 控制单策略权重
- 分散投资组合
- 监控相关性

### 4. 系统运维

- 定期备份策略和模型
- 监控系统性能
- 记录所有交易
- 定期审查策略表现

### 5. 进化策略

- 平衡探索和利用
- 保留多样性
- 避免过早收敛
- 定期引入新策略

## 故障排查

### 常见问题

#### 1. 策略不生成信号

**原因:**

- 数据长度不足
- 参数配置错误
- 逻辑错误

**解决:**

```
Python








# 检查数据长度

print(f"数据长度: {len(data)}")



# 检查策略返回

signals = strategy(data)

print(f"信号数量: {len(signals)}")

print(signals.head())
```

#### 2. 回测性能差

**原因:**

- 策略逻辑问题
- 过拟合
- 市场环境变化

**解决:**

- 检查样本外表现
- 简化策略逻辑
- 增加鲁棒性检验

#### 3. 内存不足

**原因:**

- 数据量过大
- 策略数量过多
- 未及时清理

**解决:**

```
Python








# 限制数据窗口

data = data.iloc[-1000:]



# 限制活跃策略数

evolution.active_strategies = evolution.active_strategies[:20]



# 清理缓存

import gc

gc.collect()
```

#### 4. 模型性能退化

**原因:**

- 市场机制变化
- 特征失效
- 过拟合

**解决:**

```
Python








# 检查退化

degradation = monitor.detect_degradation()

print(degradation)



# 重新训练

if degradation['degraded']:

    auto_ml._retrain_model(X_new, y_new)
```

## 1. 高级因子库

### `quant_lib/factors/factor_library.py`

```
Python








"""

高级因子库

- Alpha因子

- 价值因子

- 质量因子

- 情绪因子

- 宏观因子

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Callable

from dataclasses import dataclass

from scipy import stats





@dataclass

class FactorMetadata:

    """因子元数据"""

    name: str

    category: str  # value, momentum, quality, volatility, sentiment

    description: str

    frequency: str  # daily, weekly, monthly

    data_requirements: List[str]

    calculation_window: int





class AlphaFactors:

    """Alpha因子集合"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def calculate_all_factors(prices: pd.DataFrame, 

                             volumes: Optional[pd.DataFrame] = None,

                             fundamentals: Optional[Dict] = None) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """计算所有因子"""

        factors = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index)

        

        # 动量因子

        factors['momentum_1m'] = AlphaFactors.momentum(prices, 20)

        factors['momentum_3m'] = AlphaFactors.momentum(prices, 60)

        factors['momentum_6m'] = AlphaFactors.momentum(prices, 120)

        factors['momentum_12m'] = AlphaFactors.momentum(prices, 252)

        

        # 反转因子

        factors['reversal_1w'] = AlphaFactors.reversal(prices, 5)

        factors['reversal_1m'] = AlphaFactors.reversal(prices, 20)

        

        # 波动率因子

        factors['volatility_20d'] = AlphaFactors.realized_volatility(prices, 20)

        factors['volatility_60d'] = AlphaFactors.realized_volatility(prices, 60)

        

        # 偏度因子

        factors['skewness_20d'] = AlphaFactors.skewness(prices, 20)

        

        # 峰度因子

        factors['kurtosis_20d'] = AlphaFactors.kurtosis(prices, 20)

        

        # 趋势强度

        factors['trend_strength'] = AlphaFactors.trend_strength(prices, 60)

        

        # 价格位置

        factors['price_position_52w'] = AlphaFactors.price_position(prices, 252)

        

        # Beta因子

        factors['beta_60d'] = AlphaFactors.market_beta(prices, 60)

        

        # 特质波动率

        factors['idiosyncratic_vol'] = AlphaFactors.idiosyncratic_volatility(prices, 60)

        

        if volumes is not None:

            # 成交量因子

            factors['volume_momentum'] = AlphaFactors.volume_momentum(volumes, 20)

            factors['turnover_volatility'] = AlphaFactors.turnover_volatility(volumes, 20)

            factors['amihud_illiquidity'] = AlphaFactors.amihud_illiquidity(prices, volumes, 20)

        

        return factors

    

    @staticmethod

    def momentum(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """动量因子"""

        return prices.pct_change(window)

    

    @staticmethod

    def reversal(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """短期反转因子"""

        return -prices.pct_change(window)

    

    @staticmethod

    def realized_volatility(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """实现波动率"""

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        return returns.rolling(window).std() * np.sqrt(252)

    

    @staticmethod

    def skewness(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """收益率偏度"""

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        return returns.rolling(window).skew()

    

    @staticmethod

    def kurtosis(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """收益率峰度"""

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        return returns.rolling(window).kurt()

    

    @staticmethod

    def trend_strength(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """趋势强度（R²）"""

        def calc_r2(series):

            if len(series) < 2:

                return np.nan

            x = np.arange(len(series))

            slope, intercept, r_value, _, _ = stats.linregress(x, series)

            return r_value ** 2

        

        return prices.rolling(window).apply(calc_r2, raw=False)

    

    @staticmethod

    def price_position(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """价格在周期内的位置 (0-1)"""

        rolling_min = prices.rolling(window).min()

        rolling_max = prices.rolling(window).max()

        return (prices - rolling_min) / (rolling_max - rolling_min)

    

    @staticmethod

    def market_beta(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int, 

                   market_prices: Optional[pd.Series] = None) -> pd.Series:

        """市场Beta"""

        if market_prices is None:

            # 使用等权市场组合

            market_prices = prices.mean(axis=1)

        

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        market_returns = market_prices.pct_change()

        

        def calc_beta(asset_returns):

            if len(asset_returns) < 2:

                return np.nan

            cov = np.cov(asset_returns, market_returns[-len(asset_returns):])[0, 1]

            var = np.var(market_returns[-len(asset_returns):])

            return cov / var if var > 0 else np.nan

        

        return returns.rolling(window).apply(calc_beta, raw=False)

    

    @staticmethod

    def idiosyncratic_volatility(prices: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """特质波动率"""

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        market_returns = returns.mean(axis=1)

        

        def calc_idio_vol(asset_returns):

            if len(asset_returns) < 2:

                return np.nan

            market_ret = market_returns[-len(asset_returns):]

            

            # 回归得到残差

            slope, intercept = np.polyfit(market_ret, asset_returns, 1)

            residuals = asset_returns - (slope * market_ret + intercept)

            return residuals.std() * np.sqrt(252)

        

        return returns.rolling(window).apply(calc_idio_vol, raw=False)

    

    @staticmethod

    def volume_momentum(volumes: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """成交量动量"""

        return volumes.pct_change(window)

    

    @staticmethod

    def turnover_volatility(volumes: pd.DataFrame, window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """换手率波动率"""

        turnover = volumes.pct_change()

        return turnover.rolling(window).std()

    

    @staticmethod

    def amihud_illiquidity(prices: pd.DataFrame, volumes: pd.DataFrame, 

                          window: int) -> pd.Series:

        """Amihud流动性指标"""

        returns = prices.pct_change().abs()

        illiquidity = returns / (volumes + 1e-10)

        return illiquidity.rolling(window).mean()





class ValueFactors:

    """价值因子"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def book_to_market(book_value: pd.Series, market_cap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """账面市值比"""

        return book_value / market_cap

    

    @staticmethod

    def earnings_yield(earnings: pd.Series, market_cap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """盈利收益率"""

        return earnings / market_cap

    

    @staticmethod

    def dividend_yield(dividends: pd.Series, prices: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """股息率"""

        return dividends / prices

    

    @staticmethod

    def cash_flow_yield(cash_flow: pd.Series, market_cap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """现金流收益率"""

        return cash_flow / market_cap

    

    @staticmethod

    def sales_to_price(sales: pd.Series, market_cap: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """销售市值比"""

        return sales / market_cap





class QualityFactors:

    """质量因子"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def roe(net_income: pd.Series, equity: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """净资产收益率"""

        return net_income / equity

    

    @staticmethod

    def roa(net_income: pd.Series, total_assets: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """总资产收益率"""

        return net_income / total_assets

    

    @staticmethod

    def gross_profit_margin(gross_profit: pd.Series, revenue: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """毛利率"""

        return gross_profit / revenue

    

    @staticmethod

    def asset_turnover(revenue: pd.Series, total_assets: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """资产周转率"""

        return revenue / total_assets

    

    @staticmethod

    def accruals(net_income: pd.Series, operating_cf: pd.Series, 

                total_assets: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """应计项目"""

        return (net_income - operating_cf) / total_assets

    

    @staticmethod

    def piotroski_f_score(fundamentals: Dict) -> pd.Series:

        """Piotroski F-Score (9个指标)"""

        score = 0

        

        # 盈利能力 (4项)

        score += (fundamentals['roa'] > 0).astype(int)

        score += (fundamentals['operating_cf'] > 0).astype(int)

        score += (fundamentals['roa'].diff() > 0).astype(int)

        score += (fundamentals['accruals'] < 0).astype(int)

        

        # 杠杆、流动性 (3项)

        score += (fundamentals['long_term_debt'].diff() < 0).astype(int)

        score += (fundamentals['current_ratio'].diff() > 0).astype(int)

        score += (fundamentals['shares_outstanding'].diff() <= 0).astype(int)

        

        # 运营效率 (2项)

        score += (fundamentals['gross_margin'].diff() > 0).astype(int)

        score += (fundamentals['asset_turnover'].diff() > 0).astype(int)

        

        return score





class SentimentFactors:

    """情绪因子"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def analyst_sentiment(upgrades: pd.Series, downgrades: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """分析师情绪"""

        return (upgrades - downgrades) / (upgrades + downgrades + 1)

    

    @staticmethod

    def short_interest(short_volume: pd.Series, total_volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """空头兴趣"""

        return short_volume / total_volume

    

    @staticmethod

    def put_call_ratio(put_volume: pd.Series, call_volume: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """看跌看涨比"""

        return put_volume / call_volume

    

    @staticmethod

    def news_sentiment(sentiment_scores: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """新闻情绪"""

        return sentiment_scores.rolling(20).mean()

    

    @staticmethod

    def social_media_sentiment(mentions: pd.Series, sentiment: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """社交媒体情绪"""

        return mentions * sentiment





class FactorPortfolio:

    """因子组合构建"""

    

    def __init__(self, factors: pd.DataFrame):

        self.factors = factors

        self.factor_returns = {}

    

    def calculate_factor_returns(self, prices: pd.DataFrame, 

                                 quantiles: int = 5) -> Dict[str, pd.Series]:

        """计算因子收益（多空组合）"""

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        

        for factor_name in self.factors.columns:

            factor_values = self.factors[factor_name]

            

            # 按因子值分组

            factor_quantiles = factor_values.rolling(20).apply(

                lambda x: pd.qcut(x, quantiles, labels=False, duplicates='drop')[-1]

                if len(x) == 20 else np.nan

            )

            

            # 计算各组收益

            long_returns = []

            short_returns = []

            

            for date in returns.index:

                if date not in factor_quantiles.index:

                    continue

                

                quantile = factor_quantiles.loc[date]

                if pd.isna(quantile).all():

                    continue

                

                # 做多最高分位

                long_mask = quantile == (quantiles - 1)

                if long_mask.sum() > 0:

                    long_ret = returns.loc[date, long_mask].mean()

                    long_returns.append(long_ret)

                

                # 做空最低分位

                short_mask = quantile == 0

                if short_mask.sum() > 0:

                    short_ret = returns.loc[date, short_mask].mean()

                    short_returns.append(short_ret)

            

            # 多空组合收益

            if long_returns and short_returns:

                min_len = min(len(long_returns), len(short_returns))

                factor_ret = pd.Series(long_returns[:min_len]) - pd.Series(short_returns[:min_len])

                self.factor_returns[factor_name] = factor_ret

        

        return self.factor_returns

    

    def factor_ic(self, forward_returns: pd.DataFrame, method: str = 'spearman') -> pd.DataFrame:

        """计算因子IC（信息系数）"""

        ic_results = []

        

        for date in self.factors.index:

            if date not in forward_returns.index:

                continue

            

            factor_values = self.factors.loc[date]

            future_returns = forward_returns.loc[date]

            

            # 对齐数据

            common_assets = factor_values.index.intersection(future_returns.index)

            if len(common_assets) < 2:

                continue

            

            factor_aligned = factor_values[common_assets]

            returns_aligned = future_returns[common_assets]

            

            # 去除NaN

            valid_mask = ~(factor_aligned.isna() | returns_aligned.isna())

            if valid_mask.sum() < 2:

                continue

            

            # 计算相关系数

            if method == 'spearman':

                ic = stats.spearmanr(factor_aligned[valid_mask], 

                                    returns_aligned[valid_mask])[0]

            else:

                ic = np.corrcoef(factor_aligned[valid_mask], 

                                returns_aligned[valid_mask])[0, 1]

            

            ic_results.append({

                'date': date,

                'ic': ic

            })

        

        ic_df = pd.DataFrame(ic_results)

        

        # 计算IC统计量

        ic_stats = {

            'mean_ic': ic_df['ic'].mean(),

            'ic_std': ic_df['ic'].std(),

            'ic_ir': ic_df['ic'].mean() / ic_df['ic'].std() if ic_df['ic'].std() > 0 else 0,

            'ic_positive_rate': (ic_df['ic'] > 0).mean()

        }

        

        return ic_df, ic_stats

    

    def neutralize_factor(self, factor: pd.Series, 

                         industry: pd.Series = None,

                         market_cap: pd.Series = None) -> pd.Series:

        """因子中性化"""

        neutralized = factor.copy()

        

        if industry is not None:

            # 行业中性化

            for ind in industry.unique():

                mask = industry == ind

                if mask.sum() > 1:

                    neutralized[mask] -= neutralized[mask].mean()

        

        if market_cap is not None:

            # 市值中性化（回归残差）

            valid_mask = ~(neutralized.isna() | market_cap.isna())

            if valid_mask.sum() > 2:

                from sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression

                

                X = np.log(market_cap[valid_mask].values).reshape(-1, 1)

                y = neutralized[valid_mask].values

                

                model = LinearRegression()

                model.fit(X, y)

                

                residuals = y - model.predict(X)

                neutralized.loc[valid_mask] = residuals

        

        return neutralized

    

    def winsorize_factors(self, n_std: float = 3) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """因子去极值"""

        winsorized = self.factors.copy()

        

        for col in winsorized.columns:

            mean = winsorized[col].mean()

            std = winsorized[col].std()

            

            upper = mean + n_std * std

            lower = mean - n_std * std

            

            winsorized[col] = winsorized[col].clip(lower, upper)

        

        return winsorized

    

    def standardize_factors(self) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """因子标准化"""

        return (self.factors - self.factors.mean()) / self.factors.std()





class FactorCombiner:

    """因子合成器"""

    

    def __init__(self, factors: pd.DataFrame):

        self.factors = factors

        self.weights = None

    

    def equal_weight(self) -> pd.Series:

        """等权合成"""

        return self.factors.mean(axis=1)

    

    def ic_weight(self, ic_stats: Dict[str, float]) -> pd.Series:

        """IC加权"""

        weights = pd.Series({k: v['mean_ic'] for k, v in ic_stats.items()})

        weights = weights / weights.abs().sum()

        self.weights = weights

        

        return (self.factors * weights).sum(axis=1)

    

    def ic_ir_weight(self, ic_stats: Dict[str, float]) -> pd.Series:

        """IC_IR加权"""

        weights = pd.Series({k: v['ic_ir'] for k, v in ic_stats.items()})

        weights = weights / weights.abs().sum()

        self.weights = weights

        

        return (self.factors * weights).sum(axis=1)

    

    def pca_weight(self, n_components: int = 1) -> pd.Series:

        """PCA合成"""

        from sklearn.decomposition import PCA

        

        pca = PCA(n_components=n_components)

        combined = pca.fit_transform(self.factors.fillna(0))

        

        return pd.Series(combined[:, 0], index=self.factors.index)

    

    def max_ic_weight(self, forward_returns: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """最大化IC的权重"""

        from scipy.optimize import minimize

        

        n_factors = len(self.factors.columns)

        

        def neg_ic(weights):

            combined_factor = (self.factors * weights).sum(axis=1)

            ic = combined_factor.corr(forward_returns, method='spearman')

            return -ic

        

        constraints = {'type': 'eq', 'fun': lambda w: np.sum(np.abs(w)) - 1}

        bounds = [(-1, 1)] * n_factors

        initial = np.ones(n_factors) / n_factors

        

        result = minimize(neg_ic, initial, method='SLSQP', 

                         bounds=bounds, constraints=constraints)

        

        if result.success:

            self.weights = pd.Series(result.x, index=self.factors.columns)

            return (self.factors * self.weights).sum(axis=1)

        else:

            return self.equal_weight()
```

## 2. 风险模型与归因分析

### `quant_lib/risk/risk_models.py`

```
Python








"""

风险模型与归因分析

- Barra风格因子模型

- Fama-French多因子模型

- 风险分解

- 业绩归因

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import Dict, List, Tuple, Optional

from dataclasses import dataclass

from scipy.optimize import minimize

import warnings





@dataclass

class RiskDecomposition:

    """风险分解结果"""

    total_risk: float

    systematic_risk: float

    idiosyncratic_risk: float

    factor_contributions: Dict[str, float]

    correlation_matrix: pd.DataFrame





class BarraRiskModel:

    """Barra风格因子风险模型"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        self.factor_returns = None

        self.factor_covariance = None

        self.specific_risk = None

        self.factor_exposures = None

    

    def calculate_style_factors(self, prices: pd.DataFrame, 

                               volumes: Optional[pd.DataFrame] = None,

                               fundamentals: Optional[Dict] = None) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """计算Barra风格因子暴露"""

        from quant_lib.factors.factor_library import AlphaFactors

        

        exposures = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index)

        

        # Size - 市值因子

        if fundamentals and 'market_cap' in fundamentals:

            exposures['size'] = np.log(fundamentals['market_cap'])

        else:

            # 用价格近似

            exposures['size'] = np.log(prices.mean(axis=1))

        

        # Beta - 市场风险因子

        exposures['beta'] = AlphaFactors.market_beta(prices, window=60)

        

        # Momentum - 动量因子

        exposures['momentum'] = AlphaFactors.momentum(prices, window=252)

        

        # Volatility - 波动率因子

        exposures['volatility'] = AlphaFactors.realized_volatility(prices, window=252)

        

        # Value - 价值因子

        if fundamentals and 'book_value' in fundamentals:

            exposures['value'] = fundamentals['book_value'] / fundamentals['market_cap']

        

        # Growth - 成长因子

        if fundamentals and 'earnings_growth' in fundamentals:

            exposures['growth'] = fundamentals['earnings_growth']

        

        # Liquidity - 流动性因子

        if volumes is not None:

            exposures['liquidity'] = AlphaFactors.amihud_illiquidity(prices, volumes, 20)

        

        # Leverage - 杠杆因子

        if fundamentals and 'debt_to_equity' in fundamentals:

            exposures['leverage'] = fundamentals['debt_to_equity']

        

        # Earnings Yield - 盈利收益率

        if fundamentals and 'earnings' in fundamentals:

            exposures['earnings_yield'] = fundamentals['earnings'] / fundamentals['market_cap']

        

        # Residual Volatility - 特质波动率

        exposures['residual_volatility'] = AlphaFactors.idiosyncratic_volatility(prices, 60)

        

        # 标准化因子

        for col in exposures.columns:

            exposures[col] = (exposures[col] - exposures[col].mean()) / exposures[col].std()

        

        self.factor_exposures = exposures

        return exposures

    

    def estimate_factor_returns(self, asset_returns: pd.DataFrame, 

                               factor_exposures: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """估计因子收益（截面回归）"""

        factor_returns = []

        

        for date in asset_returns.index:

            if date not in factor_exposures.index:

                continue

            

            returns = asset_returns.loc[date]

            exposures = factor_exposures.loc[date]

            

            # 对齐数据

            common_assets = returns.index.intersection(exposures.index)

            if len(common_assets) < len(factor_exposures.columns) + 1:

                continue

            

            y = returns[common_assets].values

            X = exposures.loc[common_assets].values

            

            # 去除NaN

            valid_mask = ~(np.isnan(y) | np.any(np.isnan(X), axis=1))

            if valid_mask.sum() < len(factor_exposures.columns) + 1:

                continue

            

            y_valid = y[valid_mask]

            X_valid = X[valid_mask]

            

            # 加权最小二乘（可选）

            try:

                # 简单OLS

                beta = np.linalg.lstsq(X_valid, y_valid, rcond=None)[0]

                

                factor_returns.append({

                    'date': date,

                    **dict(zip(factor_exposures.columns, beta))

                })

            except:

                continue

        

        self.factor_returns = pd.DataFrame(factor_returns).set_index('date')

        return self.factor_returns

    

    def estimate_covariance_matrix(self, lookback: int = 252) -> Tuple[pd.DataFrame, pd.Series]:

        """估计因子协方差矩阵和特质风险"""

        if self.factor_returns is None:

            raise ValueError("需要先估计因子收益")

        

        # 因子协方差矩阵

        recent_returns = self.factor_returns.tail(lookback)

        self.factor_covariance = recent_returns.cov() * 252  # 年化

        

        # 特质风险（需要资产收益数据）

        # 这里简化处理，实际应该用回归残差

        self.specific_risk = recent_returns.std() * np.sqrt(252)

        

        return self.factor_covariance, self.specific_risk

    

    def calculate_portfolio_risk(self, weights: pd.Series, 

                                exposures: pd.Series) -> RiskDecomposition:

        """计算组合风险分解"""

        if self.factor_covariance is None:

            raise ValueError("需要先估计协方差矩阵")

        

        # 因子风险

        factor_var = exposures.T @ self.factor_covariance @ exposures

        systematic_risk = np.sqrt(factor_var)

        

        # 特质风险（简化）

        idiosyncratic_var = (weights ** 2).sum() * self.specific_risk.mean() ** 2

        idiosyncratic_risk = np.sqrt(idiosyncratic_var)

        

        # 总风险

        total_var = factor_var + idiosyncratic_var

        total_risk = np.sqrt(total_var)

        

        # 因子贡献

        factor_contributions = {}

        for factor in self.factor_covariance.columns:

            factor_exposure = exposures[factor]

            factor_var_contrib = factor_exposure * (self.factor_covariance[factor] @ exposures)

            factor_contributions[factor] = factor_var_contrib / total_var

        

        return RiskDecomposition(

            total_risk=total_risk,

            systematic_risk=systematic_risk,

            idiosyncratic_risk=idiosyncratic_risk,

            factor_contributions=factor_contributions,

            correlation_matrix=self.factor_covariance

        )





class FamaFrenchModel:

    """Fama-French三因子/五因子模型"""

    

    def __init__(self, model_type: str = 'ff3'):

        """

        Args:

            model_type: 'ff3' (三因子) 或 'ff5' (五因子)

        """

        self.model_type = model_type

        self.factor_returns = None

    

    def calculate_factors(self, prices: pd.DataFrame, 

                         market_caps: pd.DataFrame,

                         book_to_market: pd.DataFrame,

                         operating_profitability: Optional[pd.DataFrame] = None,

                         investment: Optional[pd.DataFrame] = None) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """计算Fama-French因子"""

        returns = prices.pct_change()

        

        factors = pd.DataFrame(index=returns.index)

        

        # Market Factor (Rm - Rf)

        market_return = returns.mean(axis=1)

        risk_free = 0.02 / 252  # 假设2%年化无风险利率

        factors['MKT'] = market_return - risk_free

        

        # Size (SMB - Small Minus Big)

        factors['SMB'] = self._calculate_smb(returns, market_caps)

        

        # Value (HML - High Minus Low)

        factors['HML'] = self._calculate_hml(returns, book_to_market)

        

        if self.model_type == 'ff5':

            # Profitability (RMW - Robust Minus Weak)

            if operating_profitability is not None:

                factors['RMW'] = self._calculate_rmw(returns, operating_profitability)

            

            # Investment (CMA - Conservative Minus Aggressive)

            if investment is not None:

                factors['CMA'] = self._calculate_cma(returns, investment)

        

        self.factor_returns = factors

        return factors

    

    def _calculate_smb(self, returns: pd.DataFrame, 

                      market_caps: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """Small Minus Big"""

        smb = []

        

        for date in returns.index:

            if date not in market_caps.index:

                smb.append(np.nan)

                continue

            

            ret = returns.loc[date]

            mc = market_caps.loc[date]

            

            # 按市值分组

            median_mc = mc.median()

            small = ret[mc <= median_mc].mean()

            big = ret[mc > median_mc].mean()

            

            smb.append(small - big)

        

        return pd.Series(smb, index=returns.index)

    

    def _calculate_hml(self, returns: pd.DataFrame, 

                      book_to_market: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """High Minus Low"""

        hml = []

        

        for date in returns.index:

            if date not in book_to_market.index:

                hml.append(np.nan)

                continue

            

            ret = returns.loc[date]

            bm = book_to_market.loc[date]

            

            # 按BM分组（前30%和后30%）

            high_threshold = bm.quantile(0.7)

            low_threshold = bm.quantile(0.3)

            

            high = ret[bm >= high_threshold].mean()

            low = ret[bm <= low_threshold].mean()

            

            hml.append(high - low)

        

        return pd.Series(hml, index=returns.index)

    

    def _calculate_rmw(self, returns: pd.DataFrame, 

                      operating_profitability: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """Robust Minus Weak"""

        rmw = []

        

        for date in returns.index:

            if date not in operating_profitability.index:

                rmw.append(np.nan)

                continue

            

            ret = returns.loc[date]

            op = operating_profitability.loc[date]

            

            # 按盈利能力分组

            robust_threshold = op.quantile(0.7)

            weak_threshold = op.quantile(0.3)

            

            robust = ret[op >= robust_threshold].mean()

            weak = ret[op <= weak_threshold].mean()

            

            rmw.append(robust - weak)

        

        return pd.Series(rmw, index=returns.index)

    

    def _calculate_cma(self, returns: pd.DataFrame, 

                      investment: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """Conservative Minus Aggressive"""

        cma = []

        

        for date in returns.index:

            if date not in investment.index:

                cma.append(np.nan)

                continue

            

            ret = returns.loc[date]

            inv = investment.loc[date]

            

            # 按投资水平分组

            conservative_threshold = inv.quantile(0.3)

            aggressive_threshold = inv.quantile(0.7)

            

            conservative = ret[inv <= conservative_threshold].mean()

            aggressive = ret[inv >= aggressive_threshold].mean()

            

            cma.append(conservative - aggressive)

        

        return pd.Series(cma, index=returns.index)

    

    def run_regression(self, asset_returns: pd.Series) -> Dict:

        """对单个资产运行因子回归"""

        if self.factor_returns is None:

            raise ValueError("需要先计算因子收益")

        

        # 对齐数据

        common_dates = asset_returns.index.intersection(self.factor_returns.index)

        y = asset_returns.loc[common_dates].values

        X = self.factor_returns.loc[common_dates].values

        

        # 添加常数项

        X_with_const = np.column_stack([np.ones(len(X)), X])

        

        # OLS回归

        beta = np.linalg.lstsq(X_with_const, y, rcond=None)[0]

        

        # 计算统计量

        y_pred = X_with_const @ beta

        residuals = y - y_pred

        

        # R²

        ss_res = np.sum(residuals ** 2)

        ss_tot = np.sum((y - y.mean()) ** 2)

        r_squared = 1 - ss_res / ss_tot

        

        # Alpha（超额收益）

        alpha = beta[0]

        factor_betas = beta[1:]

        

        return {

            'alpha': alpha,

            'betas': dict(zip(self.factor_returns.columns, factor_betas)),

            'r_squared': r_squared,

            'residuals': residuals

        }





class PerformanceAttribution:

    """业绩归因分析"""

    

    def __init__(self, portfolio_returns: pd.Series, 

                 benchmark_returns: pd.Series):

        self.portfolio_returns = portfolio_returns

        self.benchmark_returns = benchmark_returns

    

    def brinson_attribution(self, portfolio_weights: pd.DataFrame,

                           benchmark_weights: pd.DataFrame,

                           sector_returns: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """Brinson业绩归因"""

        attribution = []

        

        for date in portfolio_returns.index:

            if date not in portfolio_weights.index:

                continue

            

            pw = portfolio_weights.loc[date]

            bw = benchmark_weights.loc[date]

            sr = sector_returns.loc[date]

            

            # 配置效应

            allocation_effect = ((pw - bw) * (sr - sr.mean())).sum()

            

            # 选择效应

            selection_effect = (bw * (sr - sr.mean())).sum()

            

            # 交互效应

            interaction_effect = ((pw - bw) * (sr - sr.mean())).sum()

            

            attribution.append({

                'date': date,

                'allocation_effect': allocation_effect,

                'selection_effect': selection_effect,

                'interaction_effect': interaction_effect,

                'total_active_return': allocation_effect + selection_effect + interaction_effect

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(attribution)

    

    def factor_attribution(self, factor_exposures: pd.DataFrame,

                          factor_returns: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """基于因子的归因"""

        attribution = []

        

        for date in self.portfolio_returns.index:

            if date not in factor_exposures.index or date not in factor_returns.index:

                continue

            

            exposures = factor_exposures.loc[date]

            returns = factor_returns.loc[date]

            

            # 因子贡献

            factor_contrib = exposures * returns

            

            # 残差（alpha）

            total_return = self.portfolio_returns.loc[date]

            factor_return = factor_contrib.sum()

            alpha = total_return - factor_return

            

            attribution.append({

                'date': date,

                **factor_contrib.to_dict(),

                'alpha': alpha,

                'total': total_return

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(attribution)

    

    def calculate_information_ratio(self) -> float:

        """信息比率"""

        active_returns = self.portfolio_returns - self.benchmark_returns

        return active_returns.mean() / active_returns.std() * np.sqrt(252)

    

    def calculate_tracking_error(self) -> float:

        """跟踪误差"""

        active_returns = self.portfolio_returns - self.benchmark_returns

        return active_returns.std() * np.sqrt(252)

    

    def calculate_sharpe_ratio(self, risk_free: float = 0.02) -> float:

        """夏普比率"""

        excess_returns = self.portfolio_returns - risk_free / 252

        return excess_returns.mean() / excess_returns.std() * np.sqrt(252)





class RiskBudgeting:

    """风险预算"""

    

    def __init__(self, covariance_matrix: pd.DataFrame):

        self.cov_matrix = covariance_matrix

    

    def risk_parity_weights(self) -> pd.Series:

        """风险平价权重"""

        n = len(self.cov_matrix)

        

        def risk_budget_objective(weights):

            portfolio_var = weights @ self.cov_matrix @ weights

            marginal_contrib = self.cov_matrix @ weights

            risk_contrib = weights * marginal_contrib

            

            # 最小化风险贡献的方差

            return np.sum((risk_contrib - portfolio_var / n) ** 2)

        

        constraints = {'type': 'eq', 'fun': lambda w: np.sum(w) - 1}

        bounds = tuple((0, 1) for _ in range(n))

        initial = np.ones(n) / n

        

        result = minimize(risk_budget_objective, initial,

                         method='SLSQP', bounds=bounds, constraints=constraints)

        

        if result.success:

            return pd.Series(result.x, index=self.cov_matrix.index)

        else:

            return pd.Series(initial, index=self.cov_matrix.index)

    

    def risk_budgeting(self, risk_budgets: Dict[str, float]) -> pd.Series:

        """按指定风险预算分配权重"""

        n = len(self.cov_matrix)

        assets = list(self.cov_matrix.index)

        

        # 将风险预算转换为向量

        target_risk = np.array([risk_budgets.get(asset, 1/n) for asset in assets])

        target_risk = target_risk / target_risk.sum()  # 归一化

        

        def objective(weights):

            portfolio_var = weights @ self.cov_matrix @ weights

            marginal_contrib = self.cov_matrix @ weights

            risk_contrib = weights * marginal_contrib / portfolio_var

            

            # 最小化实际风险贡献与目标的差距

            return np.sum((risk_contrib - target_risk) ** 2)

        

        constraints = {'type': 'eq', 'fun': lambda w: np.sum(w) - 1}

        bounds = tuple((0, 1) for _ in range(n))

        initial = target_risk

        

        result = minimize(objective, initial,

                         method='SLSQP', bounds=bounds, constraints=constraints)

        

        if result.success:

            return pd.Series(result.x, index=assets)

        else:

            return pd.Series(initial, index=assets)

    

    def calculate_risk_contribution(self, weights: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """计算各资产的风险贡献"""

        portfolio_var = weights @ self.cov_matrix @ weights

        marginal_contrib = self.cov_matrix @ weights

        risk_contrib = weights * marginal_contrib

        

        # 归一化为百分比贡献

        return risk_contrib / risk_contrib.sum()





class StressTest:

    """压力测试"""

    

    def __init__(self, portfolio_weights: pd.Series, 

                 returns: pd.DataFrame):

        self.weights = portfolio_weights

        self.returns = returns

    

    def historical_stress_test(self, crisis_periods: List[Tuple[str, str]]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """历史情景压力测试"""

        results = []

        

        for name, (start, end) in crisis_periods:

            crisis_returns = self.returns.loc[start:end]

            

            if crisis_returns.empty:

                continue

            

            # 组合收益

            portfolio_returns = (crisis_returns * self.weights).sum(axis=1)

            

            results.append({

                'scenario': name,

                'start': start,

                'end': end,

                'total_return': portfolio_returns.sum(),

                'max_drawdown': self._max_drawdown(portfolio_returns),

                'volatility': portfolio_returns.std() * np.sqrt(252),

                'worst_day': portfolio_returns.min()

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(results)

    

    def scenario_analysis(self, scenarios: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """情景分析"""

        results = []

        

        for scenario_name, asset_shocks in scenarios.items():

            # 计算组合冲击

            portfolio_shock = sum(

                self.weights.get(asset, 0) * shock 

                for asset, shock in asset_shocks.items()

            )

            

            results.append({

                'scenario': scenario_name,

                'portfolio_impact': portfolio_shock,

                'portfolio_value_change': portfolio_shock  # 假设初始价值为1

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(results)

    

    def _max_drawdown(self, returns: pd.Series) -> float:

        """计算最大回撤"""

        cumulative = (1 + returns).cumprod()

        running_max = cumulative.expanding().max()

        drawdown = (cumulative - running_max) / running_max

        return drawdown.min()

    

    def monte_carlo_stress_test(self, n_simulations: int = 10000,

                                horizon: int = 252) -> Dict:

        """蒙特卡洛压力测试"""

        # 估计收益的协方差矩阵

        cov_matrix = self.returns.cov() * 252  # 年化

        mean_returns = self.returns.mean() * 252

        

        # 模拟

        portfolio_returns = []

        

        for _ in range(n_simulations):

            # 生成多元正态随机收益

            simulated_returns = np.random.multivariate_normal(

                mean_returns, cov_matrix, horizon

            )

            

            # 计算组合收益

            portfolio_return = (simulated_returns @ self.weights).sum()

            portfolio_returns.append(portfolio_return)

        

        portfolio_returns = np.array(portfolio_returns)

        

        return {

            'mean': portfolio_returns.mean(),

            'std': portfolio_returns.std(),

            'var_95': np.percentile(portfolio_returns, 5),

            'var_99': np.percentile(portfolio_returns, 1),

            'cvar_95': portfolio_returns[portfolio_returns <= np.percentile(portfolio_returns, 5)].mean(),

            'worst_case': portfolio_returns.min(),

            'best_case': portfolio_returns.max()

        }
```

------

## 3. 高频交易组件

### `quant_lib/hft/microstructure.py`

```
Python








"""

市场微观结构与高频交易

- 订单簿分析

- 流动性指标

- 价格冲击模型

- 最优执行

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import List, Dict, Tuple, Optional

from dataclasses import dataclass

from collections import deque





@dataclass

class OrderBook:

    """限价订单簿"""

    bids: List[Tuple[float, float]]  # [(price, size), ...]

    asks: List[Tuple[float, float]]

    timestamp: pd.Timestamp

    

    @property

    def mid_price(self) -> float:

        """中间价"""

        if not self.bids or not self.asks:

            return np.nan

        return (self.best_bid + self.best_ask) / 2

    

    @property

    def best_bid(self) -> float:

        """最优买价"""

        return self.bids[0][0] if self.bids else np.nan

    

    @property

    def best_ask(self) -> float:

        """最优卖价"""

        return self.asks[0][0] if self.asks else np.nan

    

    @property

    def spread(self) -> float:

        """买卖价差"""

        return self.best_ask - self.best_bid

    

    @property

    def relative_spread(self) -> float:

        """相对价差"""

        return self.spread / self.mid_price if self.mid_price > 0 else np.nan

    

    def depth_at_level(self, levels: int = 5) -> Tuple[float, float]:

        """档位深度"""

        bid_depth = sum(size for _, size in self.bids[:levels])

        ask_depth = sum(size for _, size in self.asks[:levels])

        return bid_depth, ask_depth

    

    def imbalance(self, levels: int = 5) -> float:

        """订单簿不平衡"""

        bid_depth, ask_depth = self.depth_at_level(levels)

        total_depth = bid_depth + ask_depth

        return (bid_depth - ask_depth) / total_depth if total_depth > 0 else 0





class OrderBookAnalyzer:

    """订单簿分析器"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        self.order_books: deque = deque(maxlen=1000)

    

    def add_order_book(self, order_book: OrderBook):

        """添加订单簿快照"""

        self.order_books.append(order_book)

    

    def calculate_spread_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, float]:

        """计算价差指标"""

        if not self.order_books:

            return {}

        

        spreads = [ob.spread for ob in self.order_books]

        relative_spreads = [ob.relative_spread for ob in self.order_books 

                           if not np.isnan(ob.relative_spread)]

        

        return {

            'mean_spread': np.mean(spreads),

            'median_spread': np.median(spreads),

            'std_spread': np.std(spreads),

            'mean_relative_spread': np.mean(relative_spreads) if relative_spreads else np.nan,

            'spread_volatility': np.std(spreads) / np.mean(spreads) if np.mean(spreads) > 0 else np.nan

        }

    

    def calculate_depth_metrics(self, levels: int = 5) -> Dict[str, float]:

        """计算深度指标"""

        if not self.order_books:

            return {}

        

        bid_depths = []

        ask_depths = []

        

        for ob in self.order_books:

            bid_depth, ask_depth = ob.depth_at_level(levels)

            bid_depths.append(bid_depth)

            ask_depths.append(ask_depth)

        

        return {

            'mean_bid_depth': np.mean(bid_depths),

            'mean_ask_depth': np.mean(ask_depths),

            'depth_imbalance': (np.mean(bid_depths) - np.mean(ask_depths)) / 

                              (np.mean(bid_depths) + np.mean(ask_depths)),

            'depth_volatility': np.std(bid_depths + ask_depths)

        }

    

    def calculate_order_flow_toxicity(self, trade_data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """计算订单流毒性（VPIN）"""

        # Volume-Synchronized Probability of Informed Trading

        

        # 计算成交量桶

        volume_per_bucket = trade_data['volume'].sum() / 50

        

        buckets = []

        current_bucket = {'buy_volume': 0, 'sell_volume': 0}

        

        for _, trade in trade_data.iterrows():

            if trade['side'] == 'buy':

                current_bucket['buy_volume'] += trade['volume']

            else:

                current_bucket['sell_volume'] += trade['volume']

            

            total = current_bucket['buy_volume'] + current_bucket['sell_volume']

            

            if total >= volume_per_bucket:

                buckets.append(current_bucket)

                current_bucket = {'buy_volume': 0, 'sell_volume': 0}

        

        # 计算VPIN

        vpin = []

        window = 50

        

        for i in range(len(buckets) - window):

            bucket_window = buckets[i:i+window]

            

            total_buy = sum(b['buy_volume'] for b in bucket_window)

            total_sell = sum(b['sell_volume'] for b in bucket_window)

            total_volume = total_buy + total_sell

            

            if total_volume > 0:

                vpin_value = abs(total_buy - total_sell) / total_volume

                vpin.append(vpin_value)

            else:

                vpin.append(np.nan)

        

        return pd.Series(vpin)





class PriceImpactModel:

    """价格冲击模型"""

    

    @staticmethod

    def almgren_chriss_impact(order_size: float, 

                             daily_volume: float,

                             volatility: float,

                             temporary_impact: float = 0.1,

                             permanent_impact: float = 0.01) -> float:

        """Almgren-Chriss价格冲击模型"""

        participation_rate = order_size / daily_volume

        

        # 临时冲击

        temp_impact = temporary_impact * volatility * np.sqrt(participation_rate)

        

        # 永久冲击

        perm_impact = permanent_impact * volatility * participation_rate

        

        return temp_impact + perm_impact

    

    @staticmethod

    def square_root_impact(order_size: float,

                          daily_volume: float,

                          volatility: float,

                          gamma: float = 0.5) -> float:

        """平方根价格冲击模型"""

        return gamma * volatility * np.sqrt(order_size / daily_volume)

    @staticmethod
    def estimate_impact_from_trades(trade_prices: pd.Series,
                                   trade_volumes: pd.Series,
                                   benchmark_price: float) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """从实际交易估计价格冲击"""
        impact_data = []
        
        cumulative_volume = 0
        for price, volume in zip(trade_prices, trade_volumes):
            cumulative_volume += volume
            
            # 价格偏离
            price_deviation = (price - benchmark_price) / benchmark_price
            
            impact_data.append({
                'cumulative_volume': cumulative_volume,
                'price': price,
                'price_deviation': price_deviation,
                'impact_bps': price_deviation * 10000
            })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(impact_data)
class OptimalExecution:
    """最优执行算法"""
    
    def __init__(self, total_shares: float, time_horizon: int,
                 risk_aversion: float = 1e-6):
        self.total_shares = total_shares
        self.time_horizon = time_horizon
        self.risk_aversion = risk_aversion
    
    def almgren_chriss_trajectory(self, volatility: float,
                                  temporary_impact: float = 0.1,
                                  permanent_impact: float = 0.01) -> np.ndarray:
        """Almgren-Chriss最优执行轨迹"""
        lambda_param = self.risk_aversion * volatility ** 2
        
        # 临时冲击参数
        eta = temporary_impact * volatility
        
        # 永久冲击参数
        gamma = permanent_impact * volatility
        
        # 计算最优执行速度
        kappa = np.sqrt(lambda_param / eta)
        tau = self.time_horizon
        
        # 生成执行轨迹
        t = np.arange(0, tau + 1)
        
        # 使用双曲正弦函数
        trajectory = self.total_shares * np.sinh(kappa * (tau - t)) / np.sinh(kappa * tau)
        
        return trajectory
    
    def vwap_schedule(self, historical_volumes: pd.Series) -> np.ndarray:
        """VWAP（成交量加权平均价）执行计划"""
        # 预测未来成交量分布
        volume_profile = historical_volumes / historical_volumes.sum()
        
        # 按成交量比例分配订单
        schedule = self.total_shares * volume_profile.values[:self.time_horizon]
        
        return schedule
    
    def twap_schedule(self) -> np.ndarray:
        """TWAP（时间加权平均价）执行计划"""
        # 均匀分配
        return np.ones(self.time_horizon) * (self.total_shares / self.time_horizon)
    
    def participation_rate_schedule(self, target_rate: float,
                                   forecast_volumes: pd.Series) -> np.ndarray:
        """目标参与率执行计划"""
        schedule = forecast_volumes.values[:self.time_horizon] * target_rate
        
        # 调整以满足总量约束
        schedule = schedule * (self.total_shares / schedule.sum())
        
        return schedule
    
    def adaptive_execution(self, current_position: float,
                          remaining_time: int,
                          market_conditions: Dict) -> float:
        """自适应执行（根据市场状况调整）"""
        remaining_shares = self.total_shares - current_position
        
        # 基础执行速度
        base_rate = remaining_shares / remaining_time if remaining_time > 0 else remaining_shares
        
        # 根据市场条件调整
        spread = market_conditions.get('spread', 0)
        imbalance = market_conditions.get('imbalance', 0)
        volatility = market_conditions.get('volatility', 0)
        
        # 价差过大时减速
        spread_factor = 1 / (1 + spread * 100)
        
        # 订单簿不平衡时调整（同向加速，反向减速）
        imbalance_factor = 1 + imbalance * 0.5
        
        # 波动率过高时减速
        volatility_factor = 1 / (1 + volatility * 10)
        
        adjusted_rate = base_rate * spread_factor * imbalance_factor * volatility_factor
        
        return adjusted_rate
class LiquidityMetrics:
    """流动性指标"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def amihud_illiquidity(returns: pd.Series, volumes: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
        """Amihud非流动性指标"""
        return returns.abs() / (volumes + 1e-10)
    
    @staticmethod
    def roll_spread(prices: pd.Series) -> float:
        """Roll价差估计"""
        price_changes = prices.diff()
        
        # 计算价格变化的自协方差
        cov = price_changes.cov(price_changes.shift(1))
        
        if cov < 0:
            return 2 * np.sqrt(-cov)
        else:
            return 0
    
    @staticmethod
    def effective_spread(trade_prices: pd.Series,
                        mid_prices: pd.Series,
                        trade_directions: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
        """有效价差"""
        # trade_directions: 1 for buy, -1 for sell
        return 2 * trade_directions * (trade_prices - mid_prices)
    
    @staticmethod
    def realized_spread(trade_prices: pd.Series,
                       mid_prices: pd.Series,
                       future_mid_prices: pd.Series,
                       trade_directions: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
        """实现价差"""
        return 2 * trade_directions * (trade_prices - future_mid_prices)
    
    @staticmethod
    def price_impact(trade_prices: pd.Series,
                    mid_prices: pd.Series,
                    future_mid_prices: pd.Series,
                    trade_directions: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:
        """价格冲击"""
        return trade_directions * (future_mid_prices - mid_prices)
    
    @staticmethod
    def kyle_lambda(price_changes: pd.Series,
                   signed_volumes: pd.Series) -> float:
        """Kyle's Lambda（价格冲击系数）"""
        from sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression
        
        X = signed_volumes.values.reshape(-1, 1)
        y = price_changes.values
        
        model = LinearRegression()
        model.fit(X, y)
        
        return model.coef_[0]
    
    @staticmethod
    def market_depth(order_book: OrderBook, price_levels: int = 10) -> Dict:
        """市场深度分析"""
        bid_depth = sum(size for _, size in order_book.bids[:price_levels])
        ask_depth = sum(size for _, size in order_book.asks[:price_levels])
        
        total_depth = bid_depth + ask_depth
        depth_imbalance = (bid_depth - ask_depth) / total_depth if total_depth > 0 else 0
        
        # 累计深度曲线
        bid_cumulative = np.cumsum([size for _, size in order_book.bids[:price_levels]])
        ask_cumulative = np.cumsum([size for _, size in order_book.asks[:price_levels]])
        
        return {
            'bid_depth': bid_depth,
            'ask_depth': ask_depth,
            'total_depth': total_depth,
            'depth_imbalance': depth_imbalance,
            'bid_cumulative': bid_cumulative,
            'ask_cumulative': ask_cumulative
        }
class HighFrequencySignals:
    """高频交易信号"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def orderbook_imbalance_signal(order_book: OrderBook, threshold: float = 0.3) -> int:
        """订单簿不平衡信号"""
        imbalance = order_book.imbalance(levels=5)
        
        if imbalance > threshold:
            return 1  # 买入
        elif imbalance < -threshold:
            return -1  # 卖出
        else:
            return 0  # 持有
    
    @staticmethod
    def spread_reversion_signal(order_book: OrderBook,
                               historical_spreads: List[float]) -> int:
        """价差回归信号"""
        current_spread = order_book.relative_spread
