        mean_spread = np.mean(historical_spreads)
        std_spread = np.std(historical_spreads)
        
        z_score = (current_spread - mean_spread) / std_spread if std_spread > 0 else 0
        
        if z_score > 2:
            return -1  # 价差过大，预期收敛
        elif z_score < -2:
            return 1  # 价差过小，预期扩大
        else:
            return 0
    
    @staticmethod
    def volume_momentum_signal(recent_volumes: pd.Series,
                              threshold_percentile: float = 0.8) -> int:
        """成交量动量信号"""
        current_volume = recent_volumes.iloc[-1]
        volume_threshold = recent_volumes.quantile(threshold_percentile)
        
        if current_volume > volume_threshold:
            # 异常成交量，可能是趋势开始
            price_change = recent_volumes.index[-1] - recent_volumes.index[0]
            return 1 if price_change > 0 else -1
        else:
            return 0
    
    @staticmethod
    def microstructure_noise_filter(prices: pd.Series, window: int = 10) -> pd.Series:
        """市场微观结构噪音过滤"""
        # 使用移动中位数过滤高频噪音
        return prices.rolling(window, center=True).median()
    
    @staticmethod
    def lead_lag_signal(leader_prices: pd.Series,
                       follower_prices: pd.Series,
                       lookback: int = 20) -> pd.Series:
        """领先-滞后关系信号"""
        # 计算领先者的收益
        leader_returns = leader_prices.pct_change()
        
        # 计算跟随者应该的收益
        from scipy.stats import pearsonr
        
        signals = []
        for i in range(lookback, len(leader_returns)):
            # 估计领先-滞后关系
            leader_window = leader_returns.iloc[i-lookback:i]
            follower_window = follower_prices.pct_change().iloc[i-lookback:i]
            
            corr, _ = pearsonr(leader_window, follower_window)
            
            # 根据领先者预测跟随者
            expected_move = leader_returns.iloc[i] * corr
            signals.append(expected_move)
        
        return pd.Series(signals, index=leader_returns.index[lookback:])
class MarketMakingStrategy:
    """做市策略"""
    
    def __init__(self, inventory_target: float = 0,
                 risk_aversion: float = 0.01):
        self.inventory_target = inventory_target
        self.risk_aversion = risk_aversion
        self.current_inventory = 0
    
    def avellaneda_stoikov_quotes(self, mid_price: float,
                                  volatility: float,
                                  time_to_end: float,
                                  tick_size: float = 0.01) -> Tuple[float, float]:
        """Avellaneda-Stoikov做市报价"""
        # 保留价格
        reservation_price = mid_price - self.current_inventory * self.risk_aversion * volatility ** 2 * time_to_end
        
        # 最优价差
        optimal_spread = self.risk_aversion * volatility ** 2 * time_to_end + (2 / self.risk_aversion) * np.log(1 + self.risk_aversion / 2)
        
        # 买卖报价
        bid_price = reservation_price - optimal_spread / 2
        ask_price = reservation_price + optimal_spread / 2
        
        # 调整到tick size
        bid_price = np.floor(bid_price / tick_size) * tick_size
        ask_price = np.ceil(ask_price / tick_size) * tick_size
        
        return bid_price, ask_price
    
    def update_inventory(self, trade_quantity: float, trade_side: str):
        """更新库存"""
        if trade_side == 'buy':
            self.current_inventory += trade_quantity
        else:
            self.current_inventory -= trade_quantity
    
    def inventory_skew_adjustment(self, base_spread: float) -> Tuple[float, float]:
        """库存偏斜调整"""
        # 库存过多时，降低卖价，提高买价
        # 库存过少时，提高卖价，降低买价
        
        inventory_diff = self.current_inventory - self.inventory_target
        skew = inventory_diff * 0.001  # 调整系数
        
        bid_adjustment = -skew
        ask_adjustment = skew
        
        return bid_adjustment, ask_adjustment
class StatisticalArbitrage:
    """统计套利（高频版本）"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def pairs_trading_signal(spread: pd.Series,
                            lookback: int = 100,
                            entry_threshold: float = 2.0,
                            exit_threshold: float = 0.5) -> pd.Series:
        """配对交易信号"""
        # 计算z-score
        mean = spread.rolling(lookback).mean()
        std = spread.rolling(lookback).std()
        z_score = (spread - mean) / std
        
        # 生成信号
        signals = pd.Series(0, index=spread.index)
        
        position = 0
        for i in range(len(z_score)):
            if pd.isna(z_score.iloc[i]):
                continue
            
            if position == 0:
                # 开仓条件
                if z_score.iloc[i] > entry_threshold:
                    position = -1  # 做空价差
                elif z_score.iloc[i] < -entry_threshold:
                    position = 1  # 做多价差
            else:
                # 平仓条件
                if abs(z_score.iloc[i]) < exit_threshold:
                    position = 0
                # 止损条件（价差继续扩大）
                elif position == 1 and z_score.iloc[i] < -entry_threshold * 1.5:
                    position = 0
                elif position == -1 and z_score.iloc[i] > entry_threshold * 1.5:
                    position = 0
            
            signals.iloc[i] = position
        
        return signals
    
    @staticmethod
    def cointegration_trading(price1: pd.Series,
                             price2: pd.Series,
                             hedge_ratio: float) -> pd.Series:
        """协整交易"""
        # 构建价差
        spread = price1 - hedge_ratio * price2
        
        # 使用配对交易信号
        return StatisticalArbitrage.pairs_trading_signal(spread)
    
    @staticmethod
    def triangular_arbitrage(price_a_b: float, price_b_c: float,
                           price_a_c: float, threshold: float = 0.001) -> Dict:
        """三角套利"""
        # 检查套利机会
        implied_price = price_a_b * price_b_c
        
        if abs(implied_price - price_a_c) / price_a_c > threshold:
            arbitrage_profit = (implied_price - price_a_c) / price_a_c
            
            if arbitrage_profit > 0:
                # 买A/C，卖A/B和B/C
                return {
                    'arbitrage': True,
                    'profit': arbitrage_profit,
                    'direction': 'buy_AC_sell_AB_BC'
                }
            else:
                # 卖A/C，买A/B和B/C
                return {
                    'arbitrage': True,
                    'profit': -arbitrage_profit,
                    'direction': 'sell_AC_buy_AB_BC'
                }
        
        return {'arbitrage': False, 'profit': 0}
4. 深度学习与强化学习模型
quant_lib/ml/deep_learning.py
Python
"""
深度学习模型
- LSTM预测模型
- Transformer模型
- 注意力机制
- 深度强化学习
"""
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass
# 注意：以下代码需要安装 tensorflow/pytorch
# 这里提供框架设计，实际使用需要安装相应库
@dataclass
class ModelConfig:
    """模型配置"""
    input_dim: int
    output_dim: int
    hidden_dims: List[int]
    dropout_rate: float = 0.2
    learning_rate: float = 0.001
    batch_size: int = 32
    epochs: int = 100
class LSTMPredictor:
    """LSTM时序预测模型"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: ModelConfig):
        self.config = config
        self.model = None
        self.scaler = None
    
    def build_model(self):
        """构建LSTM模型"""
        try:
            from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
            from tensorflow.keras.layers import LSTM, Dense, Dropout, BatchNormalization
            from tensorflow.keras.optimizers import Adam
            from tensorflow.keras.callbacks import EarlyStopping
            
            model = Sequential()
            
            # 第一层LSTM
            model.add(LSTM(self.config.hidden_dims[0],
                          return_sequences=True,
                          input_shape=(None, self.config.input_dim)))
            model.add(Dropout(self.config.dropout_rate))
            model.add(BatchNormalization())
            
            # 中间层
            for hidden_dim in self.config.hidden_dims[1:-1]:
                model.add(LSTM(hidden_dim, return_sequences=True))
                model.add(Dropout(self.config.dropout_rate))
                model.add(BatchNormalization())
            
            # 最后一层LSTM
            model.add(LSTM(self.config.hidden_dims[-1]))
            model.add(Dropout(self.config.dropout_rate))
            
            # 输出层
            model.add(Dense(self.config.output_dim))
            
            # 编译
            model.compile(optimizer=Adam(learning_rate=self.config.learning_rate),
                         loss='mse',
                         metrics=['mae'])
            
            self.model = model
            return model
            
        except ImportError:
            print("需要安装 tensorflow: pip install tensorflow")
            return None
    
    def prepare_sequences(self, data: pd.DataFrame,
                         sequence_length: int,
                         target_column: str) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
        """准备序列数据"""
        from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler
        
        # 标准化
        self.scaler = StandardScaler()
        scaled_data = self.scaler.fit_transform(data)
        
        X, y = [], []
        for i in range(len(scaled_data) - sequence_length):
            X.append(scaled_data[i:i+sequence_length])
            y.append(scaled_data[i+sequence_length][data.columns.get_loc(target_column)])
        
        return np.array(X), np.array(y)
    
    def train(self, X_train: np.ndarray, y_train: np.ndarray,
              X_val: Optional[np.ndarray] = None,
              y_val: Optional[np.ndarray] = None):
        """训练模型"""
        try:
            from tensorflow.keras.callbacks import EarlyStopping, ReduceLROnPlateau
            
            if self.model is None:
                self.build_model()
            
            callbacks = [
                EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', patience=10, restore_best_weights=True),
                ReduceLROnPlateau(monitor='val_loss', factor=0.5, patience=5)
            ]
            
            validation_data = (X_val, y_val) if X_val is not None else None
            
            history = self.model.fit(
                X_train, y_train,
                validation_data=validation_data,
                epochs=self.config.epochs,
                batch_size=self.config.batch_size,
                callbacks=callbacks,
                verbose=1
            )
            
            return history
            
        except ImportError:
            print("需要安装 tensorflow: pip install tensorflow")
            return None
    
    def predict(self, X: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        """预测"""
        if self.model is None:
            raise ValueError("模型未训练")
        
        return self.model.predict(X)
class TransformerPredictor:
    """Transformer时序预测模型"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: ModelConfig,
                 num_heads: int = 4,
                 num_layers: int = 2):
        self.config = config
        self.num_heads = num_heads
        self.num_layers = num_layers
        self.model = None
    
    def build_model(self):
        """构建Transformer模型"""
        try:
            from tensorflow.keras.models import Model
            from tensorflow.keras.layers import (Input, Dense, Dropout, LayerNormalization,
                                                MultiHeadAttention, GlobalAveragePooling1D)
            
            # 输入层
            inputs = Input(shape=(None, self.config.input_dim))
            x = inputs
            
            # Transformer层
            for _ in range(self.num_layers):
                # Multi-head attention
                attention_output = MultiHeadAttention(
                    num_heads=self.num_heads,
                    key_dim=self.config.input_dim // self.num_heads
                )(x, x)
                
                attention_output = Dropout(self.config.dropout_rate)(attention_output)
                x = LayerNormalization(epsilon=1e-6)(x + attention_output)
                
                # Feed forward
                ffn_output = Dense(self.config.hidden_dims[0], activation='relu')(x)
                ffn_output = Dropout(self.config.dropout_rate)(ffn_output)
                ffn_output = Dense(self.config.input_dim)(ffn_output)
                
                x = LayerNormalization(epsilon=1e-6)(x + ffn_output)
            
            # 池化和输出
            x = GlobalAveragePooling1D()(x)
            x = Dropout(self.config.dropout_rate)(x)
            outputs = Dense(self.config.output_dim)(x)
            
            model = Model(inputs=inputs, outputs=outputs)
            model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='mse', metrics=['mae'])
            
            self.model = model
            return model
            
        except ImportError:
            print("需要安装 tensorflow: pip install tensorflow")
            return None
class DeepQLearning:
    """深度Q学习（DQN）交易智能体"""
    
    def __init__(self, state_dim: int, action_dim: int,
                 hidden_dims: List[int] = [128, 128],
                 gamma: float = 0.99,
                 epsilon: float = 1.0,
                 epsilon_decay: float = 0.995,
                 epsilon_min: float = 0.01):
        self.state_dim = state_dim
        self.action_dim = action_dim
        self.hidden_dims = hidden_dims
        self.gamma = gamma  # 折扣因子
        self.epsilon = epsilon  # 探索率
        self.epsilon_decay = epsilon_decay
        self.epsilon_min = epsilon_min
        
        self.model = None
        self.target_model = None
        self.memory = []
        self.memory_size = 10000
    
    def build_model(self):
        """构建DQN模型"""
        try:
            from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
            from tensorflow.keras.layers import Dense, Dropout
            from tensorflow.keras.optimizers import Adam
            
            model = Sequential()
            model.add(Dense(self.hidden_dims[0], input_dim=self.state_dim, activation='relu'))
            model.add(Dropout(0.2))
            
            for hidden_dim in self.hidden_dims[1:]:
                model.add(Dense(hidden_dim, activation='relu'))
                model.add(Dropout(0.2))
            
            model.add(Dense(self.action_dim, activation='linear'))
            
            model.compile(loss='mse', optimizer=Adam(learning_rate=0.001))
            
            self.model = model
            self.target_model = Sequential.from_config(model.get_config())
            self.target_model.set_weights(model.get_weights())
            
            return model
            
        except ImportError:
            print("需要安装 tensorflow: pip install tensorflow")
            return None
    
    def remember(self, state, action, reward, next_state, done):
        """存储经验"""
        self.memory.append((state, action, reward, next_state, done))
        if len(self.memory) > self.memory_size:
            self.memory.pop(0)
    
    def act(self, state: np.ndarray, training: bool = True) -> int:
        """选择动作"""
        if training and np.random.rand() <= self.epsilon:
            return np.random.randint(self.action_dim)
        
        q_values = self.model.predict(state.reshape(1, -1), verbose=0)
        return np.argmax(q_values[0])
    
    def replay(self, batch_size: int = 32):
        """经验回放"""
        if len(self.memory) < batch_size:
            return
        
        minibatch = np.random.choice(len(self.memory), batch_size, replace=False)
        
        for idx in minibatch:
            state, action, reward, next_state, done = self.memory[idx]
            
            target = reward
            if not done:
                target = reward + self.gamma * np.amax(
                    self.target_model.predict(next_state.reshape(1, -1), verbose=0)[0]
                )
            
            target_f = self.model.predict(state.reshape(1, -1), verbose=0)
            target_f[0][action] = target
            
            self.model.fit(state.reshape(1, -1), target_f, epochs=1, verbose=0)
        
        # 衰减探索率
        if self.epsilon > self.epsilon_min:
            self.epsilon *= self.epsilon_decay
    
    def update_target_model(self):
        """更新目标网络"""
        self.target_model.set_weights(self.model.get_weights())
class PPOTrader:
    """PPO (Proximal Policy Optimization) 交易智能体"""
    
    def __init__(self, state_dim: int, action_dim: int):
        self.state_dim = state_dim
        self.action_dim = action_dim
        self.actor = None
        self.critic = None
    
    def build_networks(self):
        """构建Actor-Critic网络"""
        try:
            from tensorflow.keras.models import Model
            from tensorflow.keras.layers import Input, Dense
            
            # Actor网络
            state_input = Input(shape=(self.state_dim,))
            x = Dense(128, activation='relu')(state_input)
            x = Dense(128, activation='relu')(x)
            action_probs = Dense(self.action_dim, activation='softmax')(x)
            self.actor = Model(state_input, action_probs)
            
            # Critic网络
            value = Dense(128, activation='relu')(state_input)
            value = Dense(128, activation='relu')(value)
            value = Dense(1)(value)
            self.critic = Model(state_input, value)
            
            return self.actor, self.critic
            
        except ImportError:
            print("需要安装 tensorflow: pip install tensorflow")
            return None, None


```

## 5. 事件驱动策略

### `quant_lib/events/event_driven.py`

```
Python








"""

事件驱动策略

- 财报事件

- 公司行为（并购、回购、分红）

- 宏观经济数据发布

- 新闻情绪分析

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple

from dataclasses import dataclass

from datetime import datetime, timedelta

from enum import Enum





class EventType(Enum):

    """事件类型"""

    EARNINGS = "earnings"

    DIVIDEND = "dividend"

    MERGER = "merger"

    BUYBACK = "buyback"

    MACRO = "macro"

    NEWS = "news"

    ANALYST_UPGRADE = "analyst_upgrade"

    ANALYST_DOWNGRADE = "analyst_downgrade"





@dataclass

class Event:

    """事件数据结构"""

    event_type: EventType

    symbol: str

    timestamp: datetime

    data: Dict

    importance: float = 0.5  # 0-1





class EarningsStrategy:

    """财报事件策略"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        self.earnings_history = []

    

    def calculate_earnings_surprise(self, actual: float, 

                                   estimate: float) -> float:

        """计算财报超预期程度"""

        if estimate == 0:

            return 0

        return (actual - estimate) / abs(estimate)

    

    def post_earnings_drift(self, earnings_data: pd.DataFrame,

                           prices: pd.DataFrame,

                           holding_period: int = 60) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """盈余公告后漂移 (PEAD) 策略"""

        signals = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index, columns=prices.columns)

        signals[:] = 0

        

        for _, earning in earnings_data.iterrows():

            symbol = earning['symbol']

            announce_date = earning['announce_date']

            surprise = self.calculate_earnings_surprise(

                earning['actual_eps'], 

                earning['estimated_eps']

            )

            

            # 根据超预期程度生成信号

            if abs(surprise) > 0.05:  # 超过5%阈值

                signal_strength = np.sign(surprise) * min(abs(surprise), 1.0)

                

                # 在公告后持有一段时间

                end_date = announce_date + timedelta(days=holding_period)

                

                if announce_date in signals.index and symbol in signals.columns:

                    mask = (signals.index >= announce_date) & (signals.index < end_date)

                    signals.loc[mask, symbol] = signal_strength

        

        return signals

    

    def pre_earnings_announcement_effect(self, 

                                        earnings_calendar: pd.DataFrame,

                                        prices: pd.DataFrame,

                                        lookback_days: int = 30) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """财报前效应策略"""

        signals = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index, columns=prices.columns)

        signals[:] = 0

        

        for _, event in earnings_calendar.iterrows():

            symbol = event['symbol']

            announce_date = event['announce_date']

            

            # 计算历史财报超预期方向

            historical = self.earnings_history.get(symbol, [])

            if len(historical) >= 4:

                avg_surprise = np.mean([h['surprise'] for h in historical[-4:]])

                

                # 在财报前建立头寸

                start_date = announce_date - timedelta(days=lookback_days)

                

                if start_date in signals.index and symbol in signals.columns:

                    mask = (signals.index >= start_date) & (signals.index < announce_date)

                    signals.loc[mask, symbol] = np.sign(avg_surprise) * 0.5

        

        return signals

    

    def earnings_quality_score(self, financial_data: Dict) -> float:

        """财报质量评分"""

        score = 0

        

        # 1. 收入增长质量

        if 'revenue_growth' in financial_data:

            score += min(financial_data['revenue_growth'] / 0.1, 2)  # 最多2分

        

        # 2. 盈利质量（现金流vs利润）

        if 'operating_cash_flow' in financial_data and 'net_income' in financial_data:

            ocf = financial_data['operating_cash_flow']

            ni = financial_data['net_income']

            if ni > 0:

                quality_ratio = ocf / ni

                score += min(quality_ratio, 2)  # 最多2分

        

        # 3. 应计项目（越低越好）

        if 'accruals' in financial_data:

            accruals_penalty = abs(financial_data['accruals']) * 2

            score -= min(accruals_penalty, 2)

        

        # 4. 利润率趋势

        if 'margin_trend' in financial_data:

            score += financial_data['margin_trend'] * 2

        

        # 5. 是否超预期

        if 'earnings_surprise' in financial_data:

            score += financial_data['earnings_surprise'] * 2

        

        return max(0, min(score, 10))  # 0-10分





class CorporateActionStrategy:

    """公司行为策略"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        pass

    

    def merger_arbitrage(self, merger_data: pd.DataFrame,

                        acquirer_prices: pd.Series,

                        target_prices: pd.Series) -> Dict:

        """并购套利"""

        signals = {}

        

        for _, deal in merger_data.iterrows():

            acquirer = deal['acquirer']

            target = deal['target']

            deal_value = deal['deal_value_per_share']

            deal_type = deal['type']  # cash, stock, mixed

            announcement_date = deal['announcement_date']

            expected_close = deal['expected_close_date']

            

            if announcement_date not in target_prices.index:

                continue

            

            current_target_price = target_prices.loc[announcement_date]

            

            if deal_type == 'cash':

                # 现金收购：做多目标公司

                spread = (deal_value - current_target_price) / current_target_price

                

                if spread > 0.02:  # 2%以上套利空间

                    signals[target] = {

                        'action': 'long',

                        'spread': spread,

                        'risk_score': self._merger_risk_score(deal)

                    }

            

            elif deal_type == 'stock':

                # 换股并购：做多目标，做空收购方

                exchange_ratio = deal['exchange_ratio']

                current_acquirer_price = acquirer_prices.loc[announcement_date]

                

                implied_target_value = current_acquirer_price * exchange_ratio

                spread = (implied_target_value - current_target_price) / current_target_price

                

                if spread > 0.02:

                    signals[f"{target}_{acquirer}"] = {

                        'action': 'long_short',

                        'long': target,

                        'short': acquirer,

                        'spread': spread,

                        'hedge_ratio': exchange_ratio

                    }

        

        return signals

    

    def _merger_risk_score(self, deal: pd.Series) -> float:

        """并购风险评分"""

        risk = 0

        

        # 监管风险

        if deal.get('regulatory_approval_pending', False):

            risk += 0.3

        

        # 规模风险

        if deal.get('deal_size', 0) > 10e9:  # 超过100亿

            risk += 0.2

        

        # 跨境风险

        if deal.get('cross_border', False):

            risk += 0.2

        

        # 敌意收购风险

        if deal.get('hostile', False):

            risk += 0.3

        

        return min(risk, 1.0)

    

    def buyback_strategy(self, buyback_announcements: pd.DataFrame,

                        prices: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """股票回购策略"""

        signals = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index, columns=prices.columns)

        signals[:] = 0

        

        for _, buyback in buyback_announcements.iterrows():

            symbol = buyback['symbol']

            announce_date = buyback['announce_date']

            program_size = buyback['program_size']

            market_cap = buyback['market_cap']

            

            # 回购规模占市值比例

            buyback_ratio = program_size / market_cap

            

            if buyback_ratio > 0.05:  # 超过5%

                # 回购通常是正面信号

                signal_strength = min(buyback_ratio / 0.1, 1.0)

                

                # 持有6-12个月

                end_date = announce_date + timedelta(days=180)

                

                if announce_date in signals.index and symbol in signals.columns:

                    mask = (signals.index >= announce_date) & (signals.index < end_date)

                    signals.loc[mask, symbol] = signal_strength

        

        return signals

    

    def dividend_capture(self, dividend_data: pd.DataFrame,

                        prices: pd.DataFrame,

                        holding_days: int = 5) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """股息捕获策略"""

        signals = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index, columns=prices.columns)

        signals[:] = 0

        

        for _, div in dividend_data.iterrows():

            symbol = div['symbol']

            ex_date = div['ex_dividend_date']

            dividend_yield = div['dividend_amount'] / div['price']

            

            # 只交易高股息率的股票

            if dividend_yield > 0.02:  # 年化超过2%

                # 在除息日前买入

                buy_date = ex_date - timedelta(days=holding_days)

                

                if buy_date in signals.index and symbol in signals.columns:

                    mask = (signals.index >= buy_date) & (signals.index < ex_date)

                    signals.loc[mask, symbol] = 1.0

        

        return signals





class MacroEventStrategy:

    """宏观事件策略"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        self.event_impact_map = {

            'gdp': {'equities': 0.5, 'bonds': -0.3, 'commodities': 0.4},

            'inflation': {'equities': -0.4, 'bonds': -0.6, 'commodities': 0.7},

            'unemployment': {'equities': -0.3, 'bonds': 0.2, 'commodities': -0.2},

            'interest_rate': {'equities': -0.5, 'bonds': -0.8, 'commodities': 0.1},

        }

    

    def macro_surprise_strategy(self, macro_data: pd.DataFrame,

                               asset_class: str = 'equities') -> pd.Series:

        """宏观数据超预期策略"""

        signals = pd.Series(0, index=macro_data.index)

        

        for date, row in macro_data.iterrows():

            event_type = row['event_type']

            actual = row['actual']

            forecast = row['forecast']

            

            # 计算超预期程度

            if forecast != 0:

                surprise = (actual - forecast) / abs(forecast)

                

                # 根据事件类型和资产类别生成信号

                if event_type in self.event_impact_map:

                    impact = self.event_impact_map[event_type].get(asset_class, 0)

                    signals.loc[date] = surprise * impact

        

        return signals

    

    def fomc_trading_strategy(self, fomc_dates: pd.DataFrame,

                             prices: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """FOMC会议交易策略"""

        signals = pd.DataFrame(index=prices.index, columns=prices.columns)

        signals[:] = 0

        

        for _, meeting in fomc_dates.iterrows():

            meeting_date = meeting['date']

            rate_decision = meeting['rate_decision']  # hike, cut, hold

            surprise = meeting.get('surprise', False)

            

            if meeting_date not in signals.index:

                continue

            

            # 会议前降低仓位（不确定性）

            pre_meeting_dates = pd.date_range(

                end=meeting_date - timedelta(days=1),

                periods=5

            )

            

            for date in pre_meeting_dates:

                if date in signals.index:

                    signals.loc[date] = -0.3  # 减仓信号

            

            # 会议后根据决定调整

            if rate_decision == 'hike' and not surprise:

                # 预期内加息：短期负面

                signals.loc[meeting_date:meeting_date + timedelta(days=5)] = -0.5

            elif rate_decision == 'cut':

                # 降息：短期正面

                signals.loc[meeting_date:meeting_date + timedelta(days=5)] = 0.5

        

        return signals

    

    def economic_regime_detection(self, macro_indicators: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """经济周期识别"""

        from sklearn.cluster import KMeans

        

        # 使用K-means聚类识别经济周期

        features = macro_indicators[['gdp_growth', 'inflation', 'unemployment']].fillna(method='ffill')

        

        kmeans = KMeans(n_clusters=4, random_state=42)

        regimes = kmeans.fit_predict(features)

        

        regime_names = {

            0: 'expansion',

            1: 'peak',

            2: 'recession',

            3: 'recovery'

        }

        

        return pd.Series(regimes, index=features.index).map(regime_names)





class NewsSentimentStrategy:

    """新闻情绪策略"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        self.sentiment_history = {}

    

    def news_momentum(self, sentiment_scores: pd.DataFrame,

                     lookback: int = 20) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """新闻情绪动量"""

        # 计算移动平均

        ma_sentiment = sentiment_scores.rolling(lookback).mean()

        

        # 情绪动量信号

        signals = (sentiment_scores - ma_sentiment).clip(-1, 1)

        

        return signals

    

    def sentiment_reversal(self, sentiment_scores: pd.DataFrame,

                          threshold: float = 2.0) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """极端情绪反转"""

        signals = pd.DataFrame(0, index=sentiment_scores.index, 

                              columns=sentiment_scores.columns)

        

        # 计算z-score

        z_scores = (sentiment_scores - sentiment_scores.rolling(60).mean()) / \

                   sentiment_scores.rolling(60).std()

        

        # 极端负面情绪后做多

        signals[z_scores < -threshold] = 1

        

        # 极端正面情绪后做空

        signals[z_scores > threshold] = -1

        

        return signals

    

    def news_volume_surge(self, news_counts: pd.Series,

                         price_changes: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """新闻量激增策略"""

        # 计算新闻量异常

        news_ma = news_counts.rolling(20).mean()

        news_std = news_counts.rolling(20).std()

        news_zscore = (news_counts - news_ma) / news_std

        

        signals = pd.Series(0, index=news_counts.index)

        

        # 新闻量激增 + 价格上涨 = 买入信号

        signals[(news_zscore > 2) & (price_changes > 0)] = 1

        

        # 新闻量激增 + 价格下跌 = 卖出信号

        signals[(news_zscore > 2) & (price_changes < 0)] = -1

        

        return signals

    

    def calculate_news_sentiment_impact(self, 

                                       news_data: pd.DataFrame,

                                       returns: pd.Series,

                                       lag_days: List[int] = [0, 1, 2, 5]) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """计算新闻情绪对收益的影响"""

        results = []

        

        for lag in lag_days:

            # 滞后收益

            lagged_returns = returns.shift(-lag)

            

            # 计算相关性

            correlation = news_data['sentiment'].corr(lagged_returns)

            

            # 信息系数

            from scipy.stats import spearmanr

            ic, p_value = spearmanr(news_data['sentiment'], lagged_returns, nan_policy='omit')

            

            results.append({

                'lag_days': lag,

                'correlation': correlation,

                'ic': ic,

                'p_value': p_value

            })

        

        return pd.DataFrame(results)





class EventCalendar:

    """事件日历管理"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        self.events = []

    

    def add_event(self, event: Event):

        """添加事件"""

        self.events.append(event)

    

    def get_upcoming_events(self, days_ahead: int = 30,

                           event_types: Optional[List[EventType]] = None) -> List[Event]:

        """获取未来事件"""

        now = datetime.now()

        future_cutoff = now + timedelta(days=days_ahead)

        

        upcoming = [

            e for e in self.events 

            if now <= e.timestamp <= future_cutoff

        ]

        

        if event_types:

            upcoming = [e for e in upcoming if e.event_type in event_types]

        

        return sorted(upcoming, key=lambda x: x.timestamp)

    

    def get_events_by_symbol(self, symbol: str,

                            start_date: Optional[datetime] = None,

                            end_date: Optional[datetime] = None) -> List[Event]:

        """按标的获取事件"""

        events = [e for e in self.events if e.symbol == symbol]

        

        if start_date:

            events = [e for e in events if e.timestamp >= start_date]

        

        if end_date:

            events = [e for e in events if e.timestamp <= end_date]

        

        return sorted(events, key=lambda x: x.timestamp)

    

    def event_clustering_analysis(self, window_days: int = 5) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """事件聚类分析（识别多事件重叠期）"""

        if not self.events:

            return pd.DataFrame()

        

        # 创建时间序列

        dates = pd.date_range(

            start=min(e.timestamp for e in self.events),

            end=max(e.timestamp for e in self.events),

            freq='D'

        )

        

        event_counts = pd.Series(0, index=dates)

        importance_scores = pd.Series(0.0, index=dates)

        

        for event in self.events:

            date = event.timestamp.date()

            if date in event_counts.index:

                event_counts[date] += 1

                importance_scores[date] += event.importance

        

        # 计算移动窗口内的事件密度

        event_density = event_counts.rolling(window_days).sum()

        avg_importance = importance_scores.rolling(window_days).mean()

        

        return pd.DataFrame({

            'event_count': event_counts,

            'event_density': event_density,

            'avg_importance': avg_importance,

            'cluster_score': event_density * avg_importance

        })





class EventBacktester:

    """事件策略回测"""

    

    def __init__(self, initial_capital: float = 1000000):

        self.initial_capital = initial_capital

        self.results = None

    

    def backtest_event_strategy(self, 

                               events: List[Event],

                               prices: pd.DataFrame,

                               strategy_func: callable,

                               holding_period: int = 20) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """回测事件驱动策略"""

        portfolio_value = pd.Series(self.initial_capital, index=prices.index)

        positions = pd.DataFrame(0, index=prices.index, columns=prices.columns)

        

        for event in events:

            # 生成交易信号

            signal = strategy_func(event, prices)

            

            if signal is None:

                continue

            

            symbol = event.symbol

            event_date = event.timestamp

            

            if event_date not in prices.index or symbol not in prices.columns:

                continue

            

            # 计算持仓

            entry_price = prices.loc[event_date, symbol]

            position_size = (portfolio_value.loc[event_date] * signal['weight']) / entry_price

            

            # 设置持仓期

            exit_date = event_date + timedelta(days=holding_period)

            

            mask = (positions.index >= event_date) & (positions.index < exit_date)

            positions.loc[mask, symbol] = position_size

        

        # 计算组合价值

        portfolio_returns = (positions * prices.pct_change()).sum(axis=1)

        portfolio_value = self.initial_capital * (1 + portfolio_returns).cumprod()

        

        self.results = pd.DataFrame({

            'portfolio_value': portfolio_value,

            'returns': portfolio_returns,

            'positions': positions.sum(axis=1)

        })

        

        return self.results

    

    def calculate_event_metrics(self) -> Dict:

        """计算事件策略指标"""

        if self.results is None:

            return {}

        

        returns = self.results['returns']

        portfolio_value = self.results['portfolio_value']

        

        total_return = (portfolio_value.iloc[-1] - self.initial_capital) / self.initial_capital

        sharpe_ratio = returns.mean() / returns.std() * np.sqrt(252)

        max_dd = self._calculate_max_drawdown(portfolio_value)

        

        return {

            'total_return': total_return,

            'annualized_return': (1 + total_return) ** (252 / len(returns)) - 1,

            'sharpe_ratio': sharpe_ratio,

            'max_drawdown': max_dd,

            'win_rate': (returns > 0).mean(),

            'avg_win': returns[returns > 0].mean(),

            'avg_loss': returns[returns < 0].mean()

        }

    

    def _calculate_max_drawdown(self, portfolio_value: pd.Series) -> float:

        """计算最大回撤"""

        cumulative_max = portfolio_value.expanding().max()

        drawdown = (portfolio_value - cumulative_max) / cumulative_max

        return drawdown.min()
```

## 6. 另类数据处理

### `quant_lib/alternative_data/alt_data.py`

```
Python








"""

另类数据处理

- 卫星图像分析

- 网络爬虫数据

- 社交媒体数据

- 信用卡交易数据

- 地理位置数据

"""

import pandas as pd

import numpy as np

from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple

from datetime import datetime, timedelta

import re

from collections import Counter





class SatelliteImageAnalysis:

    """卫星图像分析（车位数量、油罐液位等）"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        pass

    

    def parking_lot_analysis(self, car_counts: pd.DataFrame,

                            store_revenues: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """停车场车辆数量分析"""

        # 计算车辆数量变化率

        car_count_growth = car_counts.pct_change()

        

        # 与收入数据关联

        correlation = pd.DataFrame(index=car_counts.columns)

        

        for store in car_counts.columns:

            if store in store_revenues.columns:

                corr = car_counts[store].corr(store_revenues[store])

                correlation.loc[store, 'correlation'] = corr

                

                # 领先-滞后分析

                for lag in range(1, 13):  # 测试1-12周的领先关系

                    lagged_corr = car_counts[store].corr(

                        store_revenues[store].shift(-lag)

                    )

                    correlation.loc[store, f'lag_{lag}_weeks'] = lagged_corr

        

        return correlation

    

    def oil_tank_level_monitoring(self, tank_levels: pd.DataFrame,

                                  oil_prices: pd.Series) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """油罐液位监测"""

        # 计算库存变化

        inventory_change = tank_levels.diff()

        

        # 与油价关系

        signals = pd.DataFrame(index=tank_levels.index)

        

        # 库存大幅下降 + 油价上涨 = 需求旺盛

        signals['demand_signal'] = (

            (inventory_change < inventory_change.quantile(0.2)) & 

            (oil_prices.pct_change() > 0)

        ).astype(int)

        

        # 库存大幅上升 + 油价下跌 = 供给过剩

        signals['supply_signal'] = (

            (inventory_change > inventory_change.quantile(0.8)) & 

            (oil_prices.pct_change() < 0)

        ).astype(int)

        

        return signals

    

    def construction_activity_index(self, construction_sites: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """建筑活动指数"""

        # 统计活跃工地数量

        active_sites = (construction_sites > 0).sum(axis=1)

        

        # 标准化

        index = (active_sites - active_sites.mean()) / active_sites.std()

        

        return index





class WebScrapingData:

    """网络爬虫数据"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        pass

    

    def ecommerce_pricing_analysis(self, price_data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """电商价格分析"""

        metrics = pd.DataFrame(index=price_data.index)

        

        # 价格趋势

        metrics['avg_price'] = price_data.mean(axis=1)

        metrics['price_volatility'] = price_data.std(axis=1)

        

        # 价格分布

        metrics['price_range'] = price_data.max(axis=1) - price_data.min(axis=1)

        metrics['price_dispersion'] = metrics['price_range'] / metrics['avg_price']

        

        # 价格动量

        metrics['price_momentum'] = metrics['avg_price'].pct_change(20)

        

        return metrics

    

    def product_availability_index(self, stock_status: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """产品可用性指数"""

        # stock_status: True/False DataFrame表示是否有货

        

        availability = stock_status.mean(axis=1)

        

        # 计算缺货率变化

        outofstock_rate = 1 - availability

        outofstock_change = outofstock_rate.diff()

        

        # 缺货率上升 = 需求旺盛信号

        return -outofstock_change  # 负号使其成为正向信号

    

    def review_sentiment_analysis(self, reviews: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """评论情绪分析"""

        sentiment_scores = pd.DataFrame(index=reviews.index)

        

        # 简单情绪词典（实际应使用NLP模型）

        positive_words = set(['good', 'great', 'excellent', 'amazing', 'love', 'best'])

        negative_words = set(['bad', 'terrible', 'awful', 'hate', 'worst', 'poor'])

        

        for col in reviews.columns:

            scores = []

            for text in reviews[col]:

                if pd.isna(text):

                    scores.append(0)

                    continue

                

                words = re.findall(r'\w+', str(text).lower())

                pos_count = sum(1 for w in words if w in positive_words)

                neg_count = sum(1 for w in words if w in negative_words)

                

                score = (pos_count - neg_count) / (len(words) + 1)

                scores.append(score)

            

            sentiment_scores[col] = scores

        

        return sentiment_scores





class SocialMediaData:

    """社交媒体数据"""

    

    def __init__(self):

        pass

    

    def twitter_sentiment_index(self, tweets: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:

        """Twitter情绪指数"""

        # tweets: columns=['timestamp', 'text', 'sentiment', 'retweets', 'likes']

        

        # 加权情绪（考虑转发和点赞）

        tweets['weighted_sentiment'] = (

            tweets['sentiment'] * 

            (1 + np.log1p(tweets['retweets'] + tweets['likes']))

        )

        

        # 按日期聚合

        daily_sentiment = tweets.groupby(tweets['timestamp'].dt.date)['weighted_sentiment'].mean()

        

        return daily_sentiment

    

    def social_media_momentum(self, mention_counts: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:

        """社交媒体关注度动量"""

        # 计算提及量变化

        mention_growth = mention_counts.pct_change()

        

        # 平滑

        smoothed_growth = mention_growth.rolling(7).mean()

        

        return smoothed_growth

    

    def influencer_sentiment(self, influencer_posts: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """意见领袖情绪分析"""

        # influencer_posts: columns=['influencer_id', 'follower_count', 'timestamp', 'sentiment']

        

        # 按影响力加权

        influencer_posts['weighted_sentiment'] = (

            influencer_posts['sentiment'] * 

            np.log1p(influencer_posts['follower_count'])

        )

        

        # 按时间聚合

        time_series = influencer_posts.groupby('timestamp')['weighted_sentiment'].mean()

        

        return time_series

    

    def hashtag_trend_analysis(self, hashtag_data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:

        """标签趋势分析"""

        # 计算标签使用频率
        trend_metrics = pd.DataFrame(index=hashtag_data.index)
        
        for hashtag in hashtag_data.columns:
            counts = hashtag_data[hashtag]
            
            # 原始计数
            trend_metrics[f'{hashtag}_count'] = counts
            
            # 增长率
            trend_metrics[f'{hashtag}_growth'] = counts.pct_change()
            
            # 动量（20日变化率）
            trend_metrics[f'{hashtag}_momentum'] = counts.pct_change(20)
            
            # 相对强度（与平均值比较）
            avg_count = counts.rolling(60).mean()
            trend_metrics[f'{hashtag}_relative_strength'] = counts / avg_count - 1
        
        return trend_metrics
class CreditCardData:
    """信用卡交易数据"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    
    def consumer_spending_index(self, transaction_data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """消费支出指数"""
        # transaction_data: columns=['date', 'category', 'amount', 'merchant']
        
        spending_metrics = pd.DataFrame()
        
        # 按类别分析
        for category in transaction_data['category'].unique():
            category_data = transaction_data[transaction_data['category'] == category]
            
            daily_spending = category_data.groupby('date')['amount'].sum()
            spending_metrics[f'{category}_spending'] = daily_spending
            
            # 同比增长
            spending_metrics[f'{category}_yoy'] = daily_spending.pct_change(365)
        
        # 总体消费指数
        spending_metrics['total_spending'] = spending_metrics.filter(like='_spending').sum(axis=1)
        
        return spending_metrics
    
    def merchant_performance_tracker(self, transaction_data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """商户表现追踪"""
        merchant_metrics = []
        
        for merchant in transaction_data['merchant'].unique():
            merchant_data = transaction_data[transaction_data['merchant'] == merchant]
            
            # 计算指标
            total_transactions = len(merchant_data)
            total_revenue = merchant_data['amount'].sum()
            avg_ticket = merchant_data['amount'].mean()
            
            # 时间序列分析
            daily_trans = merchant_data.groupby('date').size()
            transaction_growth = daily_trans.pct_change(30).mean()
            
            merchant_metrics.append({
                'merchant': merchant,
                'total_transactions': total_transactions,
                'total_revenue': total_revenue,
                'avg_ticket_size': avg_ticket,
                'transaction_growth_30d': transaction_growth
            })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(merchant_metrics)
    
    def category_rotation(self, spending_by_category: pd.DataFrame,
                         window: int = 90) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """消费类别轮动"""
        # 计算各类别的相对强度
        relative_strength = pd.DataFrame(index=spending_by_category.index)
        
        for category in spending_by_category.columns:
            # 标准化
            normalized = (spending_by_category[category] - 
                         spending_by_category[category].rolling(window).mean()) / \
                        spending_by_category[category].rolling(window).std()
            
            relative_strength[category] = normalized
        
        # 识别强势类别
        strongest_category = relative_strength.idxmax(axis=1)
        
        return pd.DataFrame({
            'strongest_category': strongest_category,
            'relative_strength': relative_strength
        })
class GeolocationData:
    """地理位置数据"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    
    def foot_traffic_analysis(self, location_data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """客流量分析"""
        # location_data: columns=['timestamp', 'location_id', 'visitor_count']
        
        traffic_metrics = pd.DataFrame()
        
        for location in location_data['location_id'].unique():
            loc_data = location_data[location_data['location_id'] == location]
            
            # 按时间聚合
            daily_traffic = loc_data.groupby(loc_data['timestamp'].dt.date)['visitor_count'].sum()
            
            traffic_metrics[f'{location}_traffic'] = daily_traffic
            traffic_metrics[f'{location}_growth'] = daily_traffic.pct_change(7)
            
            # 周末 vs 工作日
            loc_data['is_weekend'] = loc_data['timestamp'].dt.dayofweek >= 5
            weekend_traffic = loc_data[loc_data['is_weekend']].groupby(
                loc_data['timestamp'].dt.date)['visitor_count'].sum()
            weekday_traffic = loc_data[~loc_data['is_weekend']].groupby(
                loc_data['timestamp'].dt.date)['visitor_count'].sum()
            
            traffic_metrics[f'{location}_weekend_ratio'] = weekend_traffic / weekday_traffic
        
        return traffic_metrics
    
    def store_cannibalization_analysis(self, store_locations: pd.DataFrame,
                                      store_sales: pd.DataFrame,
                                      distance_threshold: float = 5.0) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """门店蚕食分析"""
        from scipy.spatial.distance import cdist
        
        # 计算门店间距离
        coords = store_locations[['latitude', 'longitude']].values
        distances = cdist(coords, coords, metric='euclidean')
        
        cannibalization_scores = []
        
        for i, store_id in enumerate(store_locations['store_id']):
            # 找到附近门店
            nearby_indices = np.where((distances[i] < distance_threshold) & (distances[i] > 0))[0]
            
            if len(nearby_indices) == 0:
                cannibalization_scores.append(0)
                continue
            
            # 计算销售相关性
            store_sales_series = store_sales[store_id]
            nearby_sales = store_sales.iloc[:, nearby_indices]
            
            # 负相关表示蚕食
            avg_correlation = nearby_sales.corrwith(store_sales_series).mean()
            cannibalization_score = max(0, -avg_correlation)
            
            cannibalization_scores.append(cannibalization_score)
        
        store_locations['cannibalization_score'] = cannibalization_scores
        return store_locations
    
    def geographic_expansion_opportunity(self, 
                                        existing_locations: pd.DataFrame,
                                        demographic_data: pd.DataFrame,
                                        performance_metrics: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """地理扩张机会分析"""
        # 识别高绩效门店特征
        high_performers = performance_metrics[
            performance_metrics['revenue'] > performance_metrics['revenue'].quantile(0.75)
        ]
        
        # 分析人口统计特征
        successful_demographics = demographic_data[
            demographic_data['location_id'].isin(high_performers.index)
        ].mean()
        
        # 评分潜在新位置
        potential_scores = []
        
        for _, location in demographic_data.iterrows():
            if location['location_id'] in existing_locations['location_id'].values:
                continue
            
            # 与成功门店人口特征的相似度
            similarity = 1 - np.abs(location - successful_demographics).mean()
            
            potential_scores.append({
                'location_id': location['location_id'],
                'similarity_score': similarity,
                'latitude': location['latitude'],
                'longitude': location['longitude']
            })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(potential_scores).sort_values('similarity_score', ascending=False)
class AlternativeDataIntegration:
    """另类数据整合"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.data_sources = {}
    
    def add_data_source(self, name: str, data: pd.DataFrame, weight: float = 1.0):
        """添加数据源"""
        self.data_sources[name] = {'data': data, 'weight': weight}
    
    def create_composite_signal(self, normalization: str = 'zscore') -> pd.Series:
        """创建综合信号"""
        if not self.data_sources:
            return pd.Series()
        
        # 获取所有数据
        all_signals = []
        weights = []
        
        for name, source in self.data_sources.items():
            data = source['data']
            weight = source['weight']
            
            # 标准化
            if normalization == 'zscore':
                normalized = (data - data.mean()) / data.std()
            elif normalization == 'minmax':
                normalized = (data - data.min()) / (data.max() - data.min())
            else:
                normalized = data
            
            # 如果是DataFrame，取平均
            if isinstance(normalized, pd.DataFrame):
                normalized = normalized.mean(axis=1)
            
            all_signals.append(normalized * weight)
            weights.append(weight)
        
        # 加权平均
        composite = sum(all_signals) / sum(weights)
        
        return composite
    
    def data_quality_assessment(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """数据质量评估"""
        quality_metrics = []
        
        for name, source in self.data_sources.items():
            data = source['data']
            
            # 计算质量指标
            completeness = 1 - data.isnull().mean().mean()
            
            if isinstance(data, pd.DataFrame):
                timeliness = (data.index[-1] - data.index[0]).days / len(data)
            else:
                timeliness = np.nan
            
            # 数据一致性（标准差）
            consistency = 1 / (1 + data.std().mean())
            
            quality_metrics.append({
                'source': name,
                'completeness': completeness,
                'timeliness': timeliness,
                'consistency': consistency,
                'overall_quality': (completeness + consistency) / 2
            })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(quality_metrics)
    
    def correlation_analysis(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """数据源相关性分析"""
        if len(self.data_sources) < 2:
            return pd.DataFrame()
        
        # 提取所有信号
        signals = {}
        for name, source in self.data_sources.items():
            data = source['data']
            if isinstance(data, pd.DataFrame):
                signals[name] = data.mean(axis=1)
            else:
                signals[name] = data
        
        signal_df = pd.DataFrame(signals)
        
        return signal_df.corr()
class RealTimeDataProcessor:
    """实时数据处理器"""
    
    def __init__(self, buffer_size: int = 1000):
        self.buffer_size = buffer_size
        self.data_buffer = {}
    
    def process_streaming_data(self, data_point: Dict, source: str):
        """处理流式数据"""
        if source not in self.data_buffer:
            self.data_buffer[source] = []
        
        # 添加时间戳
        data_point['timestamp'] = datetime.now()
        
        # 添加到缓冲区
        self.data_buffer[source].append(data_point)
        
        # 限制缓冲区大小
        if len(self.data_buffer[source]) > self.buffer_size:
            self.data_buffer[source].pop(0)
    
    def get_real_time_signal(self, source: str, 
                            window: int = 100) -> Optional[float]:
        """获取实时信号"""
        if source not in self.data_buffer:
            return None
        
        recent_data = self.data_buffer[source][-window:]
        
        if not recent_data:
            return None
        
        # 提取数值
        values = [d.get('value', 0) for d in recent_data]
        
        # 计算移动平均
        return np.mean(values)
    
    def detect_anomalies(self, source: str, threshold: float = 3.0) -> List[Dict]:
        """检测异常值"""
        if source not in self.data_buffer:
            return []
        
        data = self.data_buffer[source]
        values = [d.get('value', 0) for d in data]
        
        # 计算z-score
        mean = np.mean(values)
        std = np.std(values)
        
        anomalies = []
        for i, (value, point) in enumerate(zip(values, data)):
            z_score = (value - mean) / std if std > 0 else 0
            
            if abs(z_score) > threshold:
                anomalies.append({
                    'index': i,
                    'value': value,
                    'z_score': z_score,
                    'timestamp': point['timestamp']
                })
        
        return anomalies
7. 系统集成与生产环境
quant_lib/system/production.py
Python
"""
生产环境系统
- 实时交易执行
- 订单管理
- 风险监控
- 日志与监控
"""
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Callable
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from enum import Enum
import logging
import json
from queue import Queue
import threading
class OrderSide(Enum):
    """订单方向"""
    BUY = "buy"
    SELL = "sell"
class OrderType(Enum):
    """订单类型"""
    MARKET = "market"
    LIMIT = "limit"
    STOP = "stop"
    STOP_LIMIT = "stop_limit"
class OrderStatus(Enum):
    """订单状态"""
    PENDING = "pending"
    SUBMITTED = "submitted"
    PARTIAL_FILLED = "partial_filled"
    FILLED = "filled"
    CANCELLED = "cancelled"
    REJECTED = "rejected"
@dataclass
class Order:
    """订单对象"""
    order_id: str
    symbol: str
    side: OrderSide
    order_type: OrderType
    quantity: float
    price: Optional[float] = None
    stop_price: Optional[float] = None
    status: OrderStatus = OrderStatus.PENDING
    filled_quantity: float = 0
    avg_fill_price: float = 0
    timestamp: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    metadata: Dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    
    def is_complete(self) -> bool:
        """订单是否完成"""
        return self.status in [OrderStatus.FILLED, OrderStatus.CANCELLED, OrderStatus.REJECTED]
@dataclass
class Position:
    """持仓对象"""
    symbol: str
    quantity: float
    avg_cost: float
    market_value: float = 0
    unrealized_pnl: float = 0
    realized_pnl: float = 0
    
    def update_market_value(self, current_price: float):
        """更新市值"""
        self.market_value = self.quantity * current_price
        self.unrealized_pnl = self.market_value - (self.quantity * self.avg_cost)
class OrderManager:
    """订单管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.orders: Dict[str, Order] = {}
        self.order_queue = Queue()
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    
    def create_order(self, symbol: str, side: OrderSide, 
                    order_type: OrderType, quantity: float,
                    price: Optional[float] = None,
                    stop_price: Optional[float] = None) -> Order:
        """创建订单"""
        order_id = f"{symbol}_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S%f')}"
        
        order = Order(
            order_id=order_id,
            symbol=symbol,
            side=side,
            order_type=order_type,
            quantity=quantity,
            price=price,
            stop_price=stop_price
        )
        
        self.orders[order_id] = order
        self.order_queue.put(order)
        
        self.logger.info(f"Created order: {order_id}")
        return order
    
    def update_order(self, order_id: str, **kwargs):
        """更新订单状态"""
        if order_id not in self.orders:
            self.logger.error(f"Order {order_id} not found")
            return
        
        order = self.orders[order_id]
        
        for key, value in kwargs.items():
            if hasattr(order, key):
                setattr(order, key, value)
        
        self.logger.info(f"Updated order {order_id}: {kwargs}")
    
    def cancel_order(self, order_id: str) -> bool:
        """取消订单"""
        if order_id not in self.orders:
            return False
        
        order = self.orders[order_id]
        
        if order.is_complete():
            self.logger.warning(f"Cannot cancel completed order {order_id}")
            return False
        
        order.status = OrderStatus.CANCELLED
        self.logger.info(f"Cancelled order {order_id}")
        return True
    
    def get_active_orders(self) -> List[Order]:
        """获取活跃订单"""
        return [o for o in self.orders.values() if not o.is_complete()]
    
    def get_order_history(self, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> List[Order]:
        """获取订单历史"""
        orders = list(self.orders.values())
        
        if symbol:
            orders = [o for o in orders if o.symbol == symbol]
        
        return sorted(orders, key=lambda x: x.timestamp, reverse=True)
class PositionManager:
    """持仓管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self, initial_capital: float = 1000000):
        self.initial_capital = initial_capital
        self.cash = initial_capital
        self.positions: Dict[str, Position] = {}
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    
    def update_position(self, symbol: str, quantity: float, price: float):
        """更新持仓"""
        if symbol not in self.positions:
            if quantity == 0:
                return
            
            self.positions[symbol] = Position(
                symbol=symbol,
                quantity=quantity,
                avg_cost=price
            )
        else:
            position = self.positions[symbol]
            
            # 计算新的平均成本
            if np.sign(quantity) == np.sign(position.quantity):
                # 加仓
                total_cost = position.quantity * position.avg_cost + quantity * price
                position.quantity += quantity
                position.avg_cost = total_cost / position.quantity
            else:
                # 减仓或反向
                if abs(quantity) <= abs(position.quantity):
                    # 部分平仓
                    realized_pnl = quantity * (price - position.avg_cost)
                    position.realized_pnl += realized_pnl
                    position.quantity += quantity
                else:
                    # 完全平仓并反向
                    realized_pnl = -position.quantity * (price - position.avg_cost)
                    position.realized_pnl += realized_pnl
                    
                    remaining_quantity = quantity + position.quantity
                    position.quantity = remaining_quantity
                    position.avg_cost = price
            
            # 更新现金
            self.cash -= quantity * price
            
            # 如果持仓为0，移除
            if abs(position.quantity) < 1e-6:
                del self.positions[symbol]
    
    def get_position(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[Position]:
        """获取持仓"""
        return self.positions.get(symbol)
    
    def get_total_value(self, current_prices: Dict[str, float]) -> float:
        """获取总资产"""
        portfolio_value = self.cash
        
        for symbol, position in self.positions.items():
            if symbol in current_prices:
                position.update_market_value(current_prices[symbol])
                portfolio_value += position.market_value
        
        return portfolio_value
    
    def get_portfolio_summary(self, current_prices: Dict[str, float]) -> Dict:
        """获取组合摘要"""
        total_value = self.get_total_value(current_prices)
        
        return {
            'total_value': total_value,
            'cash': self.cash,
            'equity': total_value - self.cash,
            'num_positions': len(self.positions),
            'total_pnl': total_value - self.initial_capital,
            'total_return': (total_value - self.initial_capital) / self.initial_capital
        }
class RiskMonitor:
    """风险监控器"""
    
    def __init__(self, max_position_size: float = 0.1,
                 max_portfolio_leverage: float = 1.0,
                 max_drawdown: float = 0.2):
        self.max_position_size = max_position_size
        self.max_portfolio_leverage = max_portfolio_leverage
        self.max_drawdown = max_drawdown
        
        self.portfolio_values = []
        self.peak_value = 0
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    
    def check_position_size(self, symbol: str, quantity: float,
                           price: float, portfolio_value: float) -> bool:
        """检查持仓大小"""
        position_value = abs(quantity * price)
        position_ratio = position_value / portfolio_value
        
        if position_ratio > self.max_position_size:
            self.logger.warning(
                f"Position size check failed for {symbol}: "
                f"{position_ratio:.2%} > {self.max_position_size:.2%}"
            )
            return False
        
        return True
    
    def check_leverage(self, total_exposure: float, 
                      portfolio_value: float) -> bool:
        """检查杠杆"""
        leverage = total_exposure / portfolio_value
        
        if leverage > self.max_portfolio_leverage:
            self.logger.warning(
                f"Leverage check failed: {leverage:.2f}x > {self.max_portfolio_leverage:.2f}x"
            )
            return False
        
        return True
    
    def check_drawdown(self, current_value: float) -> bool:
        """检查回撤"""
        self.portfolio_values.append(current_value)
        
        if current_value > self.peak_value:
            self.peak_value = current_value
        
        if self.peak_value > 0:
            drawdown = (self.peak_value - current_value) / self.peak_value
            
            if drawdown > self.max_drawdown:
                self.logger.error(
                    f"Maximum drawdown exceeded: {drawdown:.2%} > {self.max_drawdown:.2%}"
                )
                return False
        
        return True
    
    def get_risk_metrics(self, returns: pd.Series) -> Dict:
        """计算风险指标"""
        return {
            'volatility': returns.std() * np.sqrt(252),
            'sharpe_ratio': returns.mean() / returns.std() * np.sqrt(252),
            'max_drawdown': self._calculate_max_drawdown(returns),
            'var_95': np.percentile(returns, 5),
            'cvar_95': returns[returns <= np.percentile(returns, 5)].mean()
        }
    
    def _calculate_max_drawdown(self, returns: pd.Series) -> float:
        """计算最大回撤"""
        cumulative = (1 + returns).cumprod()
        running_max = cumulative.expanding().max()
        drawdown = (cumulative - running_max) / running_max
        return drawdown.min()
class ExecutionEngine:
    """交易执行引擎"""
    
    def __init__(self, order_manager: OrderManager,
                 position_manager: PositionManager,
                 risk_monitor: RiskMonitor):
        self.order_manager = order_manager
        self.position_manager = position_manager
        self.risk_monitor = risk_monitor
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        
        self.is_running = False
        self.execution_thread = None
    
    def start(self):
        """启动执行引擎"""
        if self.is_running:
            return
        
        self.is_running = True
        self.execution_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._execution_loop)
        self.execution_thread.start()
        
        self.logger.info("Execution engine started")
    
    def stop(self):
        """停止执行引擎"""
        self.is_running = False
        
        if self.execution_thread:
            self.execution_thread.join()
        
        self.logger.info("Execution engine stopped")
    
    def _execution_loop(self):
        """执行循环"""
        while self.is_running:
            if not self.order_manager.order_queue.empty():
                order = self.order_manager.order_queue.get()
                self._execute_order(order)
    
    def _execute_order(self, order: Order):
        """执行订单"""
        # 风险检查
        portfolio_value = self.position_manager.get_total_value({})
        
        if not self.risk_monitor.check_position_size(
            order.symbol, order.quantity, order.price or 0, portfolio_value
        ):
            order.status = OrderStatus.REJECTED
            self.logger.warning(f"Order {order.order_id} rejected by risk check")
            return
        
        # 模拟执行（实际应该连接交易所API）
        try:
            # 更新订单状态
            order.status = OrderStatus.SUBMITTED
            
            # 模拟成交
            fill_price = order.price if order.price else self._get_market_price(order.symbol)
            order.filled_quantity = order.quantity
            order.avg_fill_price = fill_price
            order.status = OrderStatus.FILLED
            
            # 更新持仓
            quantity = order.quantity if order.side == OrderSide.BUY else -order.quantity
            self.position_manager.update_position(order.symbol, quantity, fill_price)
            
            self.logger.info(f"Order {order.order_id} filled at {fill_price}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            order.status = OrderStatus.REJECTED
            self.logger.error(f"Order execution failed: {e}")
    
    def _get_market_price(self, symbol: str) -> float:
        """获取市场价格（模拟）"""
        # 实际应该从市场数据源获取
        return 100.0
class PerformanceTracker:
    """性能追踪器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.trades = []
        self.daily_returns = []
        self.equity_curve = []
    
    def record_trade(self, trade: Dict):
        """记录交易"""
        trade['timestamp'] = datetime.now()
        self.trades.append(trade)
    
    def record_daily_return(self, date: datetime, return_value: float, 
                           portfolio_value: float):
        """记录每日收益"""
        self.daily_returns.append({
            'date': date,
            'return': return_value,
            'portfolio_value': portfolio_value
        })
        
        self.equity_curve.append(portfolio_value)
    
    def get_performance_summary(self) -> Dict:
        """获取性能摘要"""
        if not self.daily_returns:
            return {}
        
        returns_df = pd.DataFrame(self.daily_returns)
        returns_series = returns_df['return']
        
        # 计算指标
        total_return = (returns_df['portfolio_value'].iloc[-1] / 
                       returns_df['portfolio_value'].iloc[0] - 1)
        
        annual_return = (1 + total_return) ** (252 / len(returns_series)) - 1
        
        sharpe = returns_series.mean() / returns_series.std() * np.sqrt(252)
        
        cumulative = (1 + returns_series).cumprod()
        max_dd = ((cumulative - cumulative.expanding().max()) / cumulative.expanding().max()).min()
        
        win_rate = (returns_series > 0).mean()
        
        return {
            'total_return': total_return,
            'annual_return': annual_return,
            'sharpe_ratio': sharpe,
            'max_drawdown': max_dd,
            'win_rate': win_rate,
            'total_trades': len(self.trades),
            'avg_return': returns_series.mean(),
            'return_std': returns_series.std()
        }
# 示例使用
def create_trading_system():
    """创建完整交易系统"""
    # 初始化组件
    order_manager = OrderManager()
    position_manager = PositionManager(initial_capital=1000000)
    risk_monitor = RiskMonitor(max_position_size=0.1, max_drawdown=0.2)
    
    # 执行引擎
    execution_engine = ExecutionEngine(
        order_manager, position_manager, risk_monitor
    )
    
    # 性能追踪
    performance_tracker = PerformanceTracker()
    
    return {
        'order_manager': order_manager,
        'position_manager': position_manager,
        'risk_monitor': risk_monitor,
        'execution_engine': execution_engine,
        'performance_tracker': performance_tracker
    }
整个量化交易库的核心模块已经完成！包括：

基础因子与技术指标
风险模型与归因分析（Barra、Fama-French）
高频交易组件（订单簿、最优执行、做市）
深度学习模型（LSTM、Transformer、强化学习）
事件驱动策略（财报、并购、宏观事件）
另类数据处理（卫星、社交媒体、信用卡、地理位置）
生产系统（订单管理、风险监控、执行引擎）
